namespace milesing {

inline constexpr double pi = 3.141592653589793238462643383279502884;

struct Vec2 {
    double x{};
    double y{};
};

struct Vec3 {
    double x{};
    double y{};
    double z{};
};

struct Color {
    float r{};
    float g{};
    float b{};
    float a{1.0f};
};

inline Vec2 operator+(Vec2 a, Vec2 b) { return {a.x + b.x, a.y + b.y}; }
inline Vec2 operator-(Vec2 a, Vec2 b) { return {a.x - b.x, a.y - b.y}; }
inline Vec2 operator*(Vec2 a, double s) { return {a.x * s, a.y * s}; }
inline Vec3 operator+(Vec3 a, Vec3 b) { return {a.x + b.x, a.y + b.y, a.z + b.z}; }
inline Vec3 operator*(Vec3 a, double s) { return {a.x * s, a.y * s, a.z * s}; }

inline double length(Vec2 v) { return std::sqrt(v.x * v.x + v.y * v.y); }
inline double length(Vec3 v) { return std::sqrt(v.x * v.x + v.y * v.y + v.z * v.z); }

inline Vec2 logarithmic_spiral(double a, double b, double theta) {
    const double radius = a * std::exp(b * theta);
    return {radius * std::cos(theta), radius * std::sin(theta)};
}

inline std::array<double, 5> givens_rotation(double a, double b) {
    const double radius = std::hypot(a, b);
    const double c = radius == 0.0 ? 1.0 : a / radius;
    const double s = radius == 0.0 ? 0.0 : -b / radius;
    return {c, -s, s, c, radius};
}

inline Vec3 rotate_xy_givens(Vec3 value, double angle) {
    const auto g = givens_rotation(std::cos(angle), -std::sin(angle));
    return {g[0] * value.x + g[1] * value.y,
            g[2] * value.x + g[3] * value.y,
            value.z};
}

struct ExpressionRoute {
    std::size_t value{};
};

using NumberList = std::vector<double>;
using NameList = std::vector<std::string>;
using ComplexList = std::vector<std::complex<double>>;
using Point2List = std::vector<Vec2>;
using Point3List = std::vector<Vec3>;

struct Matrix {
    std::size_t rows{};
    std::size_t columns{};
    NumberList values;

    bool valid() const noexcept {
        return rows == 0 ? columns == 0 && values.empty() : columns <= values.size() / rows && rows * columns == values.size();
    }

    double at(std::size_t row, std::size_t column) const {
        if (!valid() || row >= rows || column >= columns) throw std::out_of_range("matrix position");
        return values[row * columns + column];
    }
};

struct RelationValue {
    std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::string>> pairs;
};

struct GraphEdge {
    std::string source;
    std::string target;
    double weight{1.0};
};

struct GraphValue {
    NameList vertices;
    std::vector<GraphEdge> edges;
};

struct ProbabilityValue {
    NameList outcomes;
    NumberList weights;
};

struct TimeValue {
    double seconds{};
};

struct ResourceRoute {
    std::string path;
};

struct AuthoredBodyRoute {
    std::string route;
};

struct TermValue {
    std::string operation;
    NameList arguments;
};

struct OperadTreeValue {
    NameList labels;
    std::vector<std::int64_t> parents;

    bool valid() const noexcept {
        if (labels.empty() || labels.size() != parents.size() || parents[0] != -1) return false;
        for (std::size_t i = 1; i < parents.size(); ++i) if (parents[i] < 0 || static_cast<std::size_t>(parents[i]) >= i) return false;
        return true;
    }
};

struct OperadGraft {
    std::string slot;
    OperadTreeValue tree;
};

struct OperadSubstitutions {
    std::vector<OperadGraft> grafts;
};

struct VoronoiDiagram {
    Point2List sites;
    std::vector<Point2List> cells;
};

struct FreeModuleValue {
    std::string ring;
    NameList basis;
    NumberList coordinates;
};

struct DivinandValue {
    NameList units;
    NameList assigned_operators;
    std::uint64_t catalog_extent{};
};

// A measurement is a whole authored occurrence. Its bits retain the exact
// source, duration, graph position, byte position, and bit position from which
// later Light operations derive. Numeric coordinates are technical views of
// this whole; they are never a replacement name for a self number.
struct DurationWhole {
    std::uint64_t begin_tick{};
    std::uint64_t end_tick{};
    std::uint64_t ticks_per_second{};
    std::string clock_source{"QueryPerformanceCounter"};

    bool valid() const noexcept {
        return ticks_per_second != 0 && end_tick >= begin_tick && !clock_source.empty();
    }

    std::uint64_t tick_extent() const noexcept { return end_tick - begin_tick; }
};

inline bool same_duration_whole(const DurationWhole& left,
                                const DurationWhole& right) noexcept {
    return left.begin_tick == right.begin_tick && left.end_tick == right.end_tick &&
           left.ticks_per_second == right.ticks_per_second &&
           left.clock_source == right.clock_source;
}

struct MeasuredBitWhole {
    std::string measure_whole;
    std::uint64_t sample_ordinal{};
    std::uint64_t byte_position{};
    std::uint8_t bit_position{};
    bool value{};
    Vec3 graph_position{};
    DurationWhole duration;

    bool valid() const noexcept {
        return !measure_whole.empty() && bit_position < 8 && duration.valid() &&
               std::isfinite(graph_position.x) && std::isfinite(graph_position.y) &&
               std::isfinite(graph_position.z);
    }
};

inline bool same_measured_bit_whole(const MeasuredBitWhole& left,
                                    const MeasuredBitWhole& right) noexcept {
    return left.measure_whole == right.measure_whole &&
           left.sample_ordinal == right.sample_ordinal &&
           left.byte_position == right.byte_position &&
           left.bit_position == right.bit_position && left.value == right.value &&
           left.graph_position.x == right.graph_position.x &&
           left.graph_position.y == right.graph_position.y &&
           left.graph_position.z == right.graph_position.z &&
           same_duration_whole(left.duration, right.duration);
}

inline bool measured_bit_whole_less(const MeasuredBitWhole& left,
                                    const MeasuredBitWhole& right) noexcept {
    if (left.measure_whole != right.measure_whole) return left.measure_whole < right.measure_whole;
    if (left.sample_ordinal != right.sample_ordinal) return left.sample_ordinal < right.sample_ordinal;
    if (left.byte_position != right.byte_position) return left.byte_position < right.byte_position;
    if (left.bit_position != right.bit_position) return left.bit_position < right.bit_position;
    if (left.duration.begin_tick != right.duration.begin_tick) return left.duration.begin_tick < right.duration.begin_tick;
    return left.duration.end_tick < right.duration.end_tick;
}

struct MeasureWhole {
    std::string name;
    std::string source;
    std::string quantity;
    std::string unit;
    std::string declared_measured_domain;
    DurationWhole duration;
    std::vector<std::uint8_t> exact_bytes;
    std::vector<MeasuredBitWhole> measured_bits;
    GraphValue measurement_graph;
    bool complete_for_declared_measured_domain{};
};

enum class WholeViewKind : std::uint8_t {
    truth,
    integer,
    real_scalar,
    real_sequence,
    names,
    matrix,
    relation,
    graph,
    probability,
    time,
    term
};

struct WholeGraphFact {
    std::string member;
    std::string exact_value;
};

    std::string name;
    std::string self_number;
    std::string operation_code;
    std::string equation;
    std::string direct_proof;
    std::string declared_measured_domain;
    DurationWhole duration;
    GraphValue graph;
    std::vector<WholeGraphFact> facts;
    NameList source_measure_wholes;
    NameList source_graph_wholes;
    std::vector<DurationWhole> source_durations;
    std::vector<MeasuredBitWhole> exact_bit_ancestry;
    bool complete_for_declared_measured_domain{};
};

    std::string self_number;
    std::string operation_code;
    std::string substituted_equation;
    std::string direct_proof;
    std::string declared_measured_domain;
    NameList source_measure_wholes;
    NameList source_graph_wholes;
    std::vector<DurationWhole> source_durations;
};

    std::string name;
    WholeSelfRecipe recipe;
    DerivedGraphWhole graph_whole;
};

    std::string name;
    NameList members;
};

    std::string name;
    std::string declared_measured_domain;

    NameList global_members;

    std::string open_name;

    std::vector<LocalWholeSection> sections;
};

struct SheafWholeMismatch {
    std::string left_open;
    std::string right_open;
    std::string member;
    std::string reason;
};

struct SheafGlueResult {
    std::optional<WholeSelfFormation> whole;
    std::vector<SheafWholeMismatch> mismatches;
    bool restrictions_recover_local_sections{};
    bool unique_for_declared_measured_domain{};
    std::string direct_proof;

    explicit operator bool() const noexcept {
        return whole.has_value() && mismatches.empty() &&
               restrictions_recover_local_sections &&
               unique_for_declared_measured_domain;
    }
};

struct Operand {
    using Body = std::variant<std::monostate, bool, std::int64_t, double, std::string,
                              NumberList, NameList, ComplexList, Point2List, Point3List,
                              Vec2, Vec3, Matrix, RelationValue, GraphValue, ProbabilityValue,
                              TimeValue, ResourceRoute, AuthoredBodyRoute, TermValue,
                              OperadTreeValue, OperadSubstitutions, VoronoiDiagram, FreeModuleValue,
                              DivinandValue, ExpressionRoute>;
    Body body{};

    static Operand truth(bool value) { return Operand{value}; }
    static Operand integer(std::int64_t value) { return Operand{value}; }
    static Operand number(double value) { return Operand{value}; }
    static Operand text(std::string value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand numbers(NumberList value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand names(NameList value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand complexes(ComplexList value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand points(Point2List value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand points(Point3List value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand point(Vec2 value) { return Operand{value}; }
    static Operand point(Vec3 value) { return Operand{value}; }
    static Operand matrix(Matrix value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand relation(RelationValue value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand graph(GraphValue value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand probability(ProbabilityValue value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand time(double seconds) { return Operand{TimeValue{seconds}}; }
    static Operand resource(std::string path) { return Operand{ResourceRoute{std::move(path)}}; }
    static Operand authored(std::string route) { return Operand{AuthoredBodyRoute{std::move(route)}}; }
    static Operand term(TermValue value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand operad_tree(OperadTreeValue value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand operad_substitutions(OperadSubstitutions value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand voronoi(VoronoiDiagram value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand free_module(FreeModuleValue value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand divinand(DivinandValue value) { return Operand{std::move(value)}; }
    static Operand expression(std::size_t value) { return Operand{ExpressionRoute{value}}; }

    bool numeric() const {
        return std::holds_alternative<double>(body) || std::holds_alternative<std::int64_t>(body);
    }

    double as_number() const {
        if (const auto* value = std::get_if<double>(&body)) return *value;
        if (const auto* value = std::get_if<std::int64_t>(&body)) return static_cast<double>(*value);
        throw std::runtime_error("operand is not numeric");
    }
};

struct TypedWholeView {
    std::string name;
    std::string source_measure_whole;
    std::string source_graph_whole;
    WholeViewKind kind{WholeViewKind::real_scalar};
    std::string mathematical_origin;
    std::string mathematical_notation;
    DurationWhole duration;
    Operand technical_value;
    GraphValue view_graph;
    std::vector<MeasuredBitWhole> exact_bit_ancestry;
};

inline bool finite_graph_whole(const GraphValue& graph) {
    std::unordered_set<std::string> vertices;
    vertices.reserve(graph.vertices.size());
    for (const auto& vertex : graph.vertices) {
        if (vertex.empty() || !vertices.insert(vertex).second) return false;
    }
    return std::all_of(graph.edges.begin(), graph.edges.end(), [&](const GraphEdge& edge) {
        return !edge.source.empty() && !edge.target.empty() &&
               vertices.contains(edge.source) && vertices.contains(edge.target) &&
               std::isfinite(edge.weight);
    });
}

inline bool exact_measure_whole(const MeasureWhole& measure) {
    if (measure.name.empty() || measure.source.empty() || measure.quantity.empty() ||
        measure.unit.empty() || measure.declared_measured_domain.empty() ||
        !measure.duration.valid() || !measure.complete_for_declared_measured_domain ||
        !finite_graph_whole(measure.measurement_graph)) return false;
    if (measure.exact_bytes.size() > (std::numeric_limits<std::size_t>::max)() / 8 ||
        measure.measured_bits.size() != measure.exact_bytes.size() * 8) return false;
    std::vector<MeasuredBitWhole> ordered = measure.measured_bits;
    std::sort(ordered.begin(), ordered.end(), measured_bit_whole_less);
    for (std::size_t byte = 0; byte < measure.exact_bytes.size(); ++byte) {
        for (std::uint8_t bit = 0; bit < 8; ++bit) {
            const std::size_t index = byte * 8 + bit;
            const auto& occurrence = ordered[index];
            if (!occurrence.valid() || occurrence.measure_whole != measure.name ||
                occurrence.byte_position != byte || occurrence.bit_position != bit ||
                occurrence.value != ((measure.exact_bytes[byte] >> bit) & 1u) ||
                !same_duration_whole(occurrence.duration, measure.duration)) return false;
            if (index != 0 && !measured_bit_whole_less(ordered[index - 1], occurrence)) return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
}

inline MeasureWhole form_measure_whole(std::string name,
                                       std::string source,
                                       std::string quantity,
                                       std::string unit,
                                       std::string declared_measured_domain,
                                       DurationWhole duration,
                                       std::vector<std::uint8_t> exact_bytes,
                                       Vec3 graph_origin = {},
                                       double graph_spacing = 1.0,
                                       std::uint64_t sample_ordinal = 0) {
    if (name.empty() || source.empty() || quantity.empty() || unit.empty() ||
        declared_measured_domain.empty() || !duration.valid() ||
        !std::isfinite(graph_spacing) || graph_spacing <= 0.0) {
        throw std::invalid_argument("measure whole requires an exact name, source, quantity, unit, duration, and declared measured domain");
    }
    MeasureWhole answer{std::move(name), std::move(source), std::move(quantity), std::move(unit),
                        std::move(declared_measured_domain), std::move(duration),
                        std::move(exact_bytes), {}, {}, true};
    if (answer.exact_bytes.size() > 131072) {
        throw std::length_error("one measure whole exceeds the bounded measured-bit formation extent");
    }
    answer.measured_bits.reserve(answer.exact_bytes.size() * 8);
    answer.measurement_graph.vertices.reserve(answer.exact_bytes.size() * 8);
    for (std::size_t byte = 0; byte < answer.exact_bytes.size(); ++byte) {
        for (std::uint8_t bit = 0; bit < 8; ++bit) {
            const auto bit_name = answer.name + ":" + std::to_string(byte) + ":" + std::to_string(bit);
            answer.measurement_graph.vertices.push_back(bit_name);
            const Vec3 position{graph_origin.x + graph_spacing * static_cast<double>(bit),
                                graph_origin.y + graph_spacing * static_cast<double>(byte),
                                graph_origin.z + graph_spacing * static_cast<double>(sample_ordinal)};
            answer.measured_bits.push_back(MeasuredBitWhole{
                answer.name, sample_ordinal, static_cast<std::uint64_t>(byte), bit,
                ((answer.exact_bytes[byte] >> bit) & 1u) != 0u, position, answer.duration});
            if (bit != 0) {
                answer.measurement_graph.edges.push_back({
                    answer.name + ":" + std::to_string(byte) + ":" + std::to_string(bit - 1),
                    bit_name, 1.0});
            } else if (byte != 0) {
                answer.measurement_graph.edges.push_back({
                    answer.name + ":" + std::to_string(byte - 1) + ":7", bit_name, 1.0});
            }
        }
    }
    if (!exact_measure_whole(answer)) throw std::logic_error("formed measure whole failed exact bit ancestry");
    return answer;
}

inline bool exact_derived_graph_whole(const DerivedGraphWhole& whole);

inline bool typed_whole_view_retains_ancestry(const TypedWholeView& view,
                                              const MeasureWhole& source) {
    if (!exact_measure_whole(source) || view.name.empty() ||
        view.source_measure_whole != source.name ||
        view.mathematical_origin.empty() || view.mathematical_notation.empty() ||
        !view.source_graph_whole.empty() ||
        !same_duration_whole(view.duration, source.duration) ||
        !finite_graph_whole(view.view_graph) ||
        view.exact_bit_ancestry.size() != source.measured_bits.size()) return false;
    auto actual = view.exact_bit_ancestry;
    auto expected = source.measured_bits;
    std::sort(actual.begin(), actual.end(), measured_bit_whole_less);
    std::sort(expected.begin(), expected.end(), measured_bit_whole_less);
    return std::equal(actual.begin(), actual.end(), expected.begin(), same_measured_bit_whole);
}

inline bool typed_whole_view_retains_ancestry(const TypedWholeView& view,
                                              const DerivedGraphWhole& source) {
    if (!exact_derived_graph_whole(source) || view.name.empty() ||
        !view.source_measure_whole.empty() || view.source_graph_whole != source.name ||
        view.mathematical_origin.empty() || view.mathematical_notation.empty() ||
        !same_duration_whole(view.duration, source.duration) ||
        !finite_graph_whole(view.view_graph) ||
        view.exact_bit_ancestry.size() != source.exact_bit_ancestry.size()) return false;
    auto actual = view.exact_bit_ancestry;
    auto expected = source.exact_bit_ancestry;
    std::sort(actual.begin(), actual.end(), measured_bit_whole_less);
    std::sort(expected.begin(), expected.end(), measured_bit_whole_less);
    return std::equal(actual.begin(), actual.end(), expected.begin(), same_measured_bit_whole);
}

inline TypedWholeView form_typed_whole_view(std::string name,
                                            const MeasureWhole& source,
                                            WholeViewKind kind,
                                            std::string mathematical_origin,
                                            std::string mathematical_notation,
                                            Operand technical_value,
                                            GraphValue view_graph) {
    TypedWholeView answer{std::move(name), source.name, {}, kind,
                          std::move(mathematical_origin), std::move(mathematical_notation),
                          source.duration, std::move(technical_value), std::move(view_graph),
                          source.measured_bits};
    if (!typed_whole_view_retains_ancestry(answer, source)) {
        throw std::invalid_argument("typed mathematical view must retain its measure whole's exact duration, graph, and measured-bit ancestry");
    }
    return answer;
}

inline TypedWholeView form_typed_whole_view(std::string name,
                                            const DerivedGraphWhole& source,
                                            WholeViewKind kind,
                                            std::string mathematical_origin,
                                            std::string mathematical_notation,
                                            Operand technical_value,
                                            GraphValue view_graph) {
    TypedWholeView answer{std::move(name), {}, source.name, kind,
                          std::move(mathematical_origin), std::move(mathematical_notation),
                          source.duration, std::move(technical_value), std::move(view_graph),
                          source.exact_bit_ancestry};
    if (!typed_whole_view_retains_ancestry(answer, source)) {
        throw std::invalid_argument("typed mathematical view must retain its graph whole's exact duration, graph, and measured-bit ancestry");
    }
    return answer;
}

// The generic Operand variant deliberately does not pretend to carry a
// measured whole.  DivinandWhole is the whole-self carrier used once an exact
// TypedWholeView and its exact derived graph whole are both available.
struct DivinandWhole {
    TypedWholeView source_whole;
    NameList operations;
    DerivedGraphWhole derived_whole;
    DurationWhole duration;
    std::vector<MeasuredBitWhole> exact_bit_ancestry;
    ExpressionRoute carrier_expression;
};

inline DivinandWhole form_divinand_whole(TypedWholeView source_whole,
                                         NameList operations,
                                         DerivedGraphWhole derived_whole,
                                         ExpressionRoute carrier_expression);

inline std::string canonical_operand(const Operand& operand);

struct LightDefinition {
    std::string_view branch;
    std::string_view self_number;
    // Compatibility spelling for the v0.1 source bodies. New visible and
    // mathematical routes use self_number.
    std::string_view unit;
    std::string_view function;
    std::string_view code;
    std::string_view signature;
    std::string_view origin;
    std::uint8_t minimum_operands{};
    std::uint8_t maximum_operands{};

    constexpr LightDefinition(std::string_view source_branch,
                              std::string_view source_self_number,
                              std::string_view source_function,
                              std::string_view source_code,
                              std::string_view source_signature,
                              std::string_view source_origin,
                              std::uint8_t source_minimum_operands,
                              std::uint8_t source_maximum_operands) noexcept
        : branch(source_branch), self_number(source_self_number), unit(source_self_number),
          function(source_function), code(source_code), signature(source_signature),
          origin(source_origin), minimum_operands(source_minimum_operands),
          maximum_operands(source_maximum_operands) {}
};

#include "Generated/SELF_NUMBER_BINDINGS.inc"

inline constexpr std::size_t authoritative_binding_source_byte_count = 89390;
inline constexpr std::string_view authoritative_binding_source_sha256 =
    "2AB1027F230D63237422B75AC98371C1895237FA38DFFB84B49C37D83ED7E440";

inline constexpr std::string_view binding_without_markdown_ticks(
    std::string_view value) noexcept {
    return value.size() >= 2 && value.front() == '`' && value.back() == '`'
        ? value.substr(1, value.size() - 2) : std::string_view{};
}

inline constexpr std::string_view binding_code_from_symbol(
    std::string_view symbol) noexcept {
    const std::string_view unquoted = binding_without_markdown_ticks(symbol);
    const std::size_t open = unquoted.find('(');
    return open == std::string_view::npos ? std::string_view{} : unquoted.substr(0, open);
}

static_assert(generated_self_number_bindings::entry_count == light_catalog.size());
static_assert(generated_self_number_bindings::field_count == 10);
static_assert(generated_self_number_bindings::entry_count *
              generated_self_number_bindings::field_count == 1120);
static_assert(generated_self_number_bindings::source_byte_count ==
              authoritative_binding_source_byte_count);
static_assert(generated_self_number_bindings::source_sha256 ==
              authoritative_binding_source_sha256);

inline const LightDefinition* find_light_by_self_number(std::string_view self_number) noexcept {
    const auto found = std::find_if(light_catalog.begin(), light_catalog.end(),
                                    [self_number](const LightDefinition& value) {
                                        return value.self_number == self_number;
                                    });
    return found == light_catalog.end() ? nullptr : &*found;
}

inline const LightDefinition* find_light_by_code(std::string_view code) noexcept {
    const auto found = std::find_if(light_catalog.begin(), light_catalog.end(),
                                    [code](const LightDefinition& value) { return value.code == code; });
    return found == light_catalog.end() ? nullptr : &*found;
}

inline const LightDefinition* find_light_by_unit(std::string_view unit) noexcept {
    return find_light_by_self_number(unit);
}

inline std::size_t light_catalog_index(const LightDefinition& definition) noexcept {
    return static_cast<std::size_t>(&definition - light_catalog.data());
}

struct CatalogValidation {
    bool valid{};
    std::vector<std::string> errors;
};

inline CatalogValidation validate_light_catalog() {
    CatalogValidation answer{true, {}};
    if (light_catalog.size() != 112 || light_catalog.front().self_number != "MY LIGHT" ||
        light_catalog.front().code != "divinand" ||
        light_catalog.back().self_number != "LIGHT TREATMENT" ||
        light_catalog.back().code != "sheaf_glue") {
        answer.errors.emplace_back("catalog root or extent changed");
    }
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < light_catalog.size(); ++i) {
        const auto& item = light_catalog[i];
        if (item.branch.empty() || item.self_number.empty() || item.code.empty() || item.origin.empty()) {
            answer.errors.emplace_back("catalog entry has an empty identifying field");
        }
        if (item.minimum_operands > item.maximum_operands) {
            answer.errors.emplace_back("catalog entry has an inverted arity");
        }
        for (std::size_t j = i + 1; j < light_catalog.size(); ++j) {
            if (item.code == light_catalog[j].code) answer.errors.emplace_back("duplicate Light code: " + std::string(item.code));
            if (item.self_number == light_catalog[j].self_number) answer.errors.emplace_back("duplicate self number: " + std::string(item.self_number));
        }
    }
    if (generated_self_number_bindings::entry_count != light_catalog.size() ||
        generated_self_number_bindings::field_count != 10 ||
        generated_self_number_bindings::entry_count *
                generated_self_number_bindings::field_count != 1120 ||
        generated_self_number_bindings::source_byte_count !=
                authoritative_binding_source_byte_count ||
        generated_self_number_bindings::source_sha256 !=
                authoritative_binding_source_sha256) {
        answer.errors.emplace_back("binding ledger extent or authoritative source metadata changed");
    }
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < light_catalog.size(); ++i) {
        const auto& item = light_catalog[i];
        for (std::size_t field = 0;
             field < generated_self_number_bindings::field_count; ++field) {
            if (generated_self_number_bindings::value(i, field).empty()) {
                answer.errors.emplace_back("binding ledger contains an empty field at catalog route " +
                                           std::to_string(i));
            }
        }
        const std::string_view binding_name =
            generated_self_number_bindings::value(i, 0);
        const std::string_view binding_operation =
            generated_self_number_bindings::value(i, 1);
        const std::string_view binding_symbol =
            generated_self_number_bindings::value(i, 2);
        const std::string_view binding_origin =
            generated_self_number_bindings::value(i, 4);
        const std::string_view binding_signature =
            binding_without_markdown_ticks(binding_symbol);
        if (binding_name != item.self_number) {
            answer.errors.emplace_back("binding self number disagrees with catalog route " +
                                       std::to_string(i));
        }
        if (binding_operation != item.function) {
            answer.errors.emplace_back("binding operation disagrees with catalog route " +
                                       std::to_string(i));
        }
        if (binding_signature != item.signature ||
            binding_code_from_symbol(binding_symbol) != item.code) {
            answer.errors.emplace_back("binding codable symbol disagrees with catalog route " +
                                       std::to_string(i));
        }
        if (binding_origin != item.origin) {
            answer.errors.emplace_back("binding origin disagrees with catalog route " +
                                       std::to_string(i));
        }
    }
    static constexpr std::array<std::string_view, 10> branches{
        "NIHILISM", "REALITY", "INTIMACY", "FUSING", "DESIGNING",
        "METHODOLOGIES", "PURPOSE", "GROWING", "UNIVERSING", "CEREMONIES"
    };
    for (const auto branch : branches) {
        const auto count = std::count_if(light_catalog.begin(), light_catalog.end(),
                                         [branch](const LightDefinition& item) { return item.branch == branch; });
        if (count != 11) answer.errors.emplace_back("Light branch does not contain its root and ten subclasses: " + std::string(branch));
    }
    answer.valid = answer.errors.empty();
    return answer;
}

inline bool exact_derived_graph_whole(const DerivedGraphWhole& whole) {
    if (whole.name.empty() || whole.self_number.empty() || whole.operation_code.empty() ||
        whole.equation.empty() || whole.direct_proof.empty() ||
        whole.declared_measured_domain.empty() || !whole.duration.valid() ||
        !whole.complete_for_declared_measured_domain || !finite_graph_whole(whole.graph)) return false;
    NameList vertices = whole.graph.vertices;
    std::sort(vertices.begin(), vertices.end());
    std::vector<WholeGraphFact> facts = whole.facts;
    std::sort(facts.begin(), facts.end(), [](const WholeGraphFact& left, const WholeGraphFact& right) {
        return left.member < right.member;
    });
    if (facts.size() != vertices.size()) return false;
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < facts.size(); ++i) {
        if (facts[i].member != vertices[i] || facts[i].exact_value.empty() ||
            (i != 0 && facts[i - 1].member == facts[i].member)) return false;
    }
    if (!std::all_of(whole.source_durations.begin(), whole.source_durations.end(),
                     [](const DurationWhole& duration) { return duration.valid(); })) return false;
    return std::all_of(whole.exact_bit_ancestry.begin(), whole.exact_bit_ancestry.end(),
                       [](const MeasuredBitWhole& bit) { return bit.valid(); });
}

inline DivinandWhole form_divinand_whole(TypedWholeView source_whole,
                                         NameList operations,
                                         DerivedGraphWhole derived_whole,
                                         ExpressionRoute carrier_expression) {
    if (source_whole.name.empty() ||
        (source_whole.source_measure_whole.empty() == source_whole.source_graph_whole.empty()) ||
        source_whole.mathematical_origin.empty() || source_whole.mathematical_notation.empty() ||
        !source_whole.duration.valid() || !finite_graph_whole(source_whole.view_graph) ||
        !exact_derived_graph_whole(derived_whole) ||
        derived_whole.self_number != "MY LIGHT" || derived_whole.operation_code != "divinand" ||
        !same_duration_whole(source_whole.duration, derived_whole.duration) ||
        operations.size() > 64) {
        throw std::invalid_argument("DivinandWhole requires one exact typed source whole, one finite route, and one exact MY LIGHT derived whole on the same duration");
    }
    for (const auto& operation_name : operations) {
        const auto* operation = find_light_by_code(operation_name);
        if (!operation) operation = find_light_by_self_number(operation_name);
        if (!operation || operation->minimum_operands != 1 ||
            operation->maximum_operands != 1 || operation->code == "divinand") {
            throw std::invalid_argument("DivinandWhole route contains a non-unary or absent Light operation");
        }
    }
    const auto associated = [&](const NameList& names, const std::string& name) {
        return std::find(names.begin(), names.end(), name) != names.end();
    };
    if ((!source_whole.source_measure_whole.empty() &&
         !associated(derived_whole.source_measure_wholes, source_whole.source_measure_whole)) ||
        (!source_whole.source_graph_whole.empty() &&
         !associated(derived_whole.source_graph_wholes, source_whole.source_graph_whole))) {
        throw std::invalid_argument("DivinandWhole derived whole does not retain its supplied source association");
    }
    auto source_ancestry = source_whole.exact_bit_ancestry;
    auto derived_ancestry = derived_whole.exact_bit_ancestry;
    std::sort(source_ancestry.begin(), source_ancestry.end(), measured_bit_whole_less);
    std::sort(derived_ancestry.begin(), derived_ancestry.end(), measured_bit_whole_less);
    std::size_t derived_position = 0;
    for (const auto& source_bit : source_ancestry) {
        bool found = false;
        while (derived_position < derived_ancestry.size()) {
            const auto& candidate = derived_ancestry[derived_position++];
            if (same_measured_bit_whole(source_bit, candidate)) { found = true; break; }
            if (measured_bit_whole_less(source_bit, candidate)) break;
        }
        if (!found) {
            throw std::invalid_argument("DivinandWhole derived ancestry must contain every exact source-whole measured bit");
        }
    }
    const DurationWhole duration = source_whole.duration;
    return DivinandWhole{std::move(source_whole), std::move(operations),
                         std::move(derived_whole), duration,
                         std::move(derived_ancestry), carrier_expression};
}

inline NameList sorted_unique_names(NameList values) {
    std::sort(values.begin(), values.end());
    values.erase(std::unique(values.begin(), values.end()), values.end());
    return values;
}

inline GraphValue restrict_finite_graph(const GraphValue& graph,
                                        const NameList& supplied_members) {
    const auto members = sorted_unique_names(supplied_members);
    GraphValue answer{members, {}};
    for (const auto& edge : graph.edges) {
        if (std::binary_search(members.begin(), members.end(), edge.source) &&
            std::binary_search(members.begin(), members.end(), edge.target)) {
            answer.edges.push_back(edge);
        }
    }
    std::sort(answer.edges.begin(), answer.edges.end(), [](const GraphEdge& left, const GraphEdge& right) {
        if (left.source != right.source) return left.source < right.source;
        if (left.target != right.target) return left.target < right.target;
        return std::bit_cast<std::uint64_t>(left.weight) < std::bit_cast<std::uint64_t>(right.weight);
    });
    answer.edges.erase(std::unique(answer.edges.begin(), answer.edges.end(), [](const GraphEdge& left, const GraphEdge& right) {
        return left.source == right.source && left.target == right.target &&
               std::bit_cast<std::uint64_t>(left.weight) == std::bit_cast<std::uint64_t>(right.weight);
    }), answer.edges.end());
    return answer;
}

inline std::vector<WholeGraphFact> restrict_whole_facts(
    const std::vector<WholeGraphFact>& facts, const NameList& supplied_members) {
    const auto members = sorted_unique_names(supplied_members);
    std::vector<WholeGraphFact> answer;
    for (const auto& fact : facts) {
        if (std::binary_search(members.begin(), members.end(), fact.member)) answer.push_back(fact);
    }
    std::sort(answer.begin(), answer.end(), [](const WholeGraphFact& left, const WholeGraphFact& right) {
        if (left.member != right.member) return left.member < right.member;
        return left.exact_value < right.exact_value;
    });
    return answer;
}

inline bool same_finite_graph(const GraphValue& left, const GraphValue& right) {
    const auto canonical_left = restrict_finite_graph(left, left.vertices);
    const auto canonical_right = restrict_finite_graph(right, right.vertices);
    if (canonical_left.vertices != canonical_right.vertices ||
        canonical_left.edges.size() != canonical_right.edges.size()) return false;
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < canonical_left.edges.size(); ++i) {
        const auto& a = canonical_left.edges[i];
        const auto& b = canonical_right.edges[i];
        if (a.source != b.source || a.target != b.target ||
            std::bit_cast<std::uint64_t>(a.weight) != std::bit_cast<std::uint64_t>(b.weight)) return false;
    }
    return true;
}

inline DerivedGraphWhole restrict_derived_graph_whole(const DerivedGraphWhole& whole,
                                                       const NameList& members,
                                                       std::string restricted_name) {
    if (!exact_derived_graph_whole(whole)) throw std::invalid_argument("graph whole is not complete for its declared measured domain");
    DerivedGraphWhole answer = whole;
    answer.name = std::move(restricted_name);
    answer.graph = restrict_finite_graph(whole.graph, members);
    answer.facts = restrict_whole_facts(whole.facts, members);
    answer.equation = "restrict(" + whole.name + ", supplied_open)";
    answer.direct_proof = "Restriction keeps exactly the supplied open's members, their exact values, and every graph edge whose endpoints both lie in that open.";
    if (!exact_derived_graph_whole(answer)) throw std::logic_error("finite graph restriction did not form a complete declared-domain graph whole");
    return answer;
}

inline SheafGlueResult sheaf_glue(const FiniteWholeCover& supplied_cover,
                                  const FiniteLocalWholeSections& supplied_local_sections) {
    SheafGlueResult answer;
    const auto mismatch = [&](std::string left, std::string right,
                              std::string member, std::string reason) {
        answer.mismatches.push_back({std::move(left), std::move(right),
                                     std::move(member), std::move(reason)});
    };
    if (supplied_cover.name.empty() || supplied_cover.declared_measured_domain.empty() ||
        !supplied_cover.duration.valid()) {
        mismatch("cover", {}, {}, "finite cover requires a name, an exact duration, and a declared measured domain");
        return answer;
    }
    FiniteWholeCover cover = supplied_cover;
    if (cover.global_members.empty()) {
        mismatch("cover", {}, {}, "LIGHT TREATMENT requires at least one measured member in this finite construction");
        return answer;
    }
    const auto distinct_global = sorted_unique_names(cover.global_members);
    if (distinct_global.size() != cover.global_members.size() ||
        std::any_of(distinct_global.begin(), distinct_global.end(), [](const std::string& value) { return value.empty(); })) {
        mismatch("cover", {}, {}, "global measured members must be nonempty and unique");
        return answer;
    }
    cover.global_members = distinct_global;
    std::sort(cover.opens.begin(), cover.opens.end(), [](const FiniteWholeOpen& left, const FiniteWholeOpen& right) {
        return left.name < right.name;
    });
    NameList covered_members;
    std::unordered_set<std::string> open_names;
    for (auto& open : cover.opens) {
        if (open.name.empty() || !open_names.insert(open.name).second) {
            mismatch(open.name, {}, {}, "finite cover open names must be nonempty and unique");
            continue;
        }
        const auto distinct_members = sorted_unique_names(open.members);
        if (distinct_members.empty() || distinct_members.size() != open.members.size()) {
            mismatch(open.name, {}, {}, "each finite open requires a nonempty unique member list");
            continue;
        }
        open.members = distinct_members;
        for (const auto& member : open.members) {
            if (!std::binary_search(cover.global_members.begin(), cover.global_members.end(), member)) {
                mismatch(open.name, {}, member, "open member is outside the declared measured whole");
            } else covered_members.push_back(member);
        }
    }
    if (sorted_unique_names(covered_members) != cover.global_members) {
        mismatch("cover", {}, {}, "finite opens do not cover every declared measured member");
    }

    std::vector<LocalWholeSection> sections = supplied_local_sections.sections;
    std::sort(sections.begin(), sections.end(), [](const LocalWholeSection& left, const LocalWholeSection& right) {
        return left.open_name < right.open_name;
    });
    if (sections.size() != cover.opens.size()) {
        mismatch("local_sections", {}, {}, "exactly one local graph whole is required for every finite open");
    }
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < sections.size(); ++i) {
        const auto& section = sections[i];
        const auto open = std::lower_bound(cover.opens.begin(), cover.opens.end(), section.open_name,
                                           [](const FiniteWholeOpen& value, const std::string& name) {
                                               return value.name < name;
                                           });
        if (open == cover.opens.end() || open->name != section.open_name) {
            mismatch(section.open_name, {}, {}, "local graph whole names an absent finite open");
            continue;
        }
        if (i != 0 && sections[i - 1].open_name == section.open_name) {
            mismatch(section.open_name, {}, {}, "finite open has more than one local graph whole");
            continue;
        }
        if (!exact_derived_graph_whole(section.graph_whole)) {
            mismatch(section.open_name, {}, {}, "local graph whole is incomplete for its declared measured domain");
            continue;
        }
        if (!same_duration_whole(section.graph_whole.duration, cover.duration) ||
            section.graph_whole.declared_measured_domain != cover.declared_measured_domain) {
            mismatch(section.open_name, {}, {}, "local graph whole duration or declared measured domain differs from the cover");
        }
        if (sorted_unique_names(section.graph_whole.graph.vertices) != open->members) {
            mismatch(section.open_name, {}, {}, "local graph whole does not have exactly its open's measured members");
        }
    }

    for (std::size_t left = 0; left < cover.opens.size(); ++left) {
        const auto left_section = std::find_if(sections.begin(), sections.end(), [&](const LocalWholeSection& value) {
            return value.open_name == cover.opens[left].name;
        });
        if (left_section == sections.end() || !exact_derived_graph_whole(left_section->graph_whole)) continue;
        for (std::size_t right = left + 1; right < cover.opens.size(); ++right) {
            const auto right_section = std::find_if(sections.begin(), sections.end(), [&](const LocalWholeSection& value) {
                return value.open_name == cover.opens[right].name;
            });
            if (right_section == sections.end() || !exact_derived_graph_whole(right_section->graph_whole)) continue;
            NameList overlap;
            std::set_intersection(cover.opens[left].members.begin(), cover.opens[left].members.end(),
                                  cover.opens[right].members.begin(), cover.opens[right].members.end(),
                                  std::back_inserter(overlap));
            const auto left_facts = restrict_whole_facts(left_section->graph_whole.facts, overlap);
            const auto right_facts = restrict_whole_facts(right_section->graph_whole.facts, overlap);
            if (left_facts.size() != right_facts.size()) {
                mismatch(cover.opens[left].name, cover.opens[right].name, {}, "overlap restrictions have different measured values");
            } else {
                for (std::size_t i = 0; i < left_facts.size(); ++i) {
                    if (left_facts[i].member != right_facts[i].member ||
                        left_facts[i].exact_value != right_facts[i].exact_value) {
                        mismatch(cover.opens[left].name, cover.opens[right].name,
                                 left_facts[i].member, "overlap restrictions disagree on the exact value");
                    }
                }
            }
            if (!same_finite_graph(restrict_finite_graph(left_section->graph_whole.graph, overlap),
                                   restrict_finite_graph(right_section->graph_whole.graph, overlap))) {
                mismatch(cover.opens[left].name, cover.opens[right].name, {}, "overlap restrictions disagree on graph relations");
            }
        }
    }
    if (!answer.mismatches.empty()) return answer;

    DerivedGraphWhole glued;
    glued.name = cover.name + ":LIGHT TREATMENT";
    glued.self_number = "LIGHT TREATMENT";
    glued.operation_code = "sheaf_glue";
    glued.equation = "sheaf_glue(" + cover.name + ", local_sections)";
    glued.direct_proof = "Every declared measured member lies in a finite open. Pairwise restrictions agree on each overlap, so choosing a local value at any containing open is well-defined. The resulting global graph whole restricts to every supplied local graph whole. Any other such global whole agrees at every covered member and is therefore equal.";
    glued.declared_measured_domain = cover.declared_measured_domain;
    glued.duration = cover.duration;
    glued.graph.vertices = cover.global_members;
    for (const auto& section : sections) {
        glued.facts.insert(glued.facts.end(), section.graph_whole.facts.begin(), section.graph_whole.facts.end());
        glued.graph.edges.insert(glued.graph.edges.end(), section.graph_whole.graph.edges.begin(), section.graph_whole.graph.edges.end());
        glued.source_measure_wholes.insert(glued.source_measure_wholes.end(),
                                           section.graph_whole.source_measure_wholes.begin(),
                                           section.graph_whole.source_measure_wholes.end());
        glued.source_graph_wholes.push_back(section.graph_whole.name);
        glued.source_durations.insert(glued.source_durations.end(),
                                      section.graph_whole.source_durations.begin(),
                                      section.graph_whole.source_durations.end());
        glued.source_durations.push_back(section.graph_whole.duration);
        glued.exact_bit_ancestry.insert(glued.exact_bit_ancestry.end(),
                                        section.graph_whole.exact_bit_ancestry.begin(),
                                        section.graph_whole.exact_bit_ancestry.end());
    }
    std::sort(glued.facts.begin(), glued.facts.end(), [](const WholeGraphFact& left, const WholeGraphFact& right) {
        if (left.member != right.member) return left.member < right.member;
        return left.exact_value < right.exact_value;
    });
    glued.facts.erase(std::unique(glued.facts.begin(), glued.facts.end(), [](const WholeGraphFact& left, const WholeGraphFact& right) {
        return left.member == right.member && left.exact_value == right.exact_value;
    }), glued.facts.end());
    glued.graph = restrict_finite_graph(glued.graph, glued.graph.vertices);
    glued.source_measure_wholes = sorted_unique_names(std::move(glued.source_measure_wholes));
    glued.source_graph_wholes = sorted_unique_names(std::move(glued.source_graph_wholes));
    std::sort(glued.source_durations.begin(), glued.source_durations.end(), [](const DurationWhole& left, const DurationWhole& right) {
        if (left.clock_source != right.clock_source) return left.clock_source < right.clock_source;
        if (left.ticks_per_second != right.ticks_per_second) return left.ticks_per_second < right.ticks_per_second;
        if (left.begin_tick != right.begin_tick) return left.begin_tick < right.begin_tick;
        return left.end_tick < right.end_tick;
    });
    glued.source_durations.erase(std::unique(glued.source_durations.begin(), glued.source_durations.end(), same_duration_whole),
                                  glued.source_durations.end());
    std::sort(glued.exact_bit_ancestry.begin(), glued.exact_bit_ancestry.end(), measured_bit_whole_less);
    glued.exact_bit_ancestry.erase(std::unique(glued.exact_bit_ancestry.begin(), glued.exact_bit_ancestry.end(),
                                               same_measured_bit_whole), glued.exact_bit_ancestry.end());
    glued.complete_for_declared_measured_domain = true;
    if (!exact_derived_graph_whole(glued)) {
        mismatch("glued_whole", {}, {}, "finite sheaf gluing did not produce one exact fact for every declared measured member");
        return answer;
    }

    bool restrictions_recover = true;
    for (const auto& open : cover.opens) {
        const auto section = std::find_if(sections.begin(), sections.end(), [&](const LocalWholeSection& value) {
            return value.open_name == open.name;
        });
        if (section == sections.end()) { restrictions_recover = false; break; }
        const auto restricted_graph = restrict_finite_graph(glued.graph, open.members);
        const auto restricted_facts = restrict_whole_facts(glued.facts, open.members);
        const auto expected_facts = restrict_whole_facts(section->graph_whole.facts, open.members);
        restrictions_recover = same_finite_graph(restricted_graph, section->graph_whole.graph) &&
                               restricted_facts.size() == expected_facts.size() &&
                               std::equal(restricted_facts.begin(), restricted_facts.end(), expected_facts.begin(),
                                          [](const WholeGraphFact& left, const WholeGraphFact& right) {
                                              return left.member == right.member && left.exact_value == right.exact_value;
                                          });
        if (!restrictions_recover) break;
    }
    answer.restrictions_recover_local_sections = restrictions_recover;
    answer.unique_for_declared_measured_domain = restrictions_recover;
    answer.direct_proof = glued.direct_proof;
    if (!restrictions_recover) {
        mismatch("glued_whole", {}, {}, "a restriction of the glued graph whole did not recover its supplied local graph whole");
        return answer;
    }
    WholeSelfRecipe recipe{"LIGHT TREATMENT", "sheaf_glue", glued.equation,
                           glued.direct_proof, glued.declared_measured_domain,
                           glued.source_measure_wholes, glued.source_graph_wholes,
                           glued.source_durations};
    answer.whole = WholeSelfFormation{glued.name, std::move(recipe), std::move(glued)};
    return answer;
}

struct PortrayalIdentification {
    std::string whole_self_formation;
    std::string portrayal_name;
    GraphValue portrayal_graph;
};

inline PortrayalIdentification identify_whole_portrayal(const WholeSelfFormation& whole,
                                                        std::string portrayal_name,
                                                        GraphValue portrayal_graph) {
    if (whole.name.empty() || !exact_derived_graph_whole(whole.graph_whole) ||
        whole.recipe.declared_measured_domain != whole.graph_whole.declared_measured_domain) {
        throw std::invalid_argument("portrayal requires an already complete declared-domain whole-self formation");
    }
    if (portrayal_name.empty() || !finite_graph_whole(portrayal_graph)) {
        throw std::invalid_argument("portrayal identification requires a name and finite graph");
    }
    return {whole.name, std::move(portrayal_name), std::move(portrayal_graph)};
}

inline bool integral_operand(const Operand& operand, std::int64_t& value) noexcept {
    if (const auto* integer = std::get_if<std::int64_t>(&operand.body)) {
        value = *integer;
        return true;
    }
    if (const auto* number = std::get_if<double>(&operand.body)) {
        if (std::isfinite(*number) && std::floor(*number) == *number &&
            *number >= static_cast<double>((std::numeric_limits<std::int64_t>::min)()) &&
            *number <= static_cast<double>((std::numeric_limits<std::int64_t>::max)())) {
            value = static_cast<std::int64_t>(*number);
            return true;
        }
    }
    return false;
}

inline bool truth_operand(const Operand& operand, bool& value) noexcept {
    if (const auto* truth = std::get_if<bool>(&operand.body)) {
        value = *truth;
        return true;
    }
    return false;
}

inline std::optional<std::size_t> finite_carrier_cardinality(const Operand& operand) {
    return std::visit([](const auto& value) -> std::optional<std::size_t> {
        using T = std::decay_t<decltype(value)>;
        if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, NameList>) {
            std::unordered_set<std::string> members;
            for (const auto& member : value) {
                if (member.empty()) return std::nullopt;
                members.insert(member);
            }
            return members.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, NumberList>) {
            if (!std::all_of(value.begin(), value.end(), [](double member) { return std::isfinite(member); })) return std::nullopt;
            auto members = value;
            std::sort(members.begin(), members.end());
            members.erase(std::unique(members.begin(), members.end()), members.end());
            return members.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, ComplexList>) {
            if (!std::all_of(value.begin(), value.end(), [](std::complex<double> member) {
                    return std::isfinite(member.real()) && std::isfinite(member.imag());
                })) return std::nullopt;
            auto members = value;
            std::sort(members.begin(), members.end(), [](auto left, auto right) {
                return left.real() != right.real() ? left.real() < right.real() : left.imag() < right.imag();
            });
            members.erase(std::unique(members.begin(), members.end()), members.end());
            return members.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, Point2List>) {
            if (!std::all_of(value.begin(), value.end(), [](Vec2 member) {
                    return std::isfinite(member.x) && std::isfinite(member.y);
                })) return std::nullopt;
            auto members = value;
            std::sort(members.begin(), members.end(), [](Vec2 left, Vec2 right) {
                return left.x != right.x ? left.x < right.x : left.y < right.y;
            });
            members.erase(std::unique(members.begin(), members.end(), [](Vec2 left, Vec2 right) {
                return left.x == right.x && left.y == right.y;
            }), members.end());
            return members.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, Point3List>) {
            if (!std::all_of(value.begin(), value.end(), [](Vec3 member) {
                    return std::isfinite(member.x) && std::isfinite(member.y) && std::isfinite(member.z);
                })) return std::nullopt;
            auto members = value;
            std::sort(members.begin(), members.end(), [](Vec3 left, Vec3 right) {
                if (left.x != right.x) return left.x < right.x;
                return left.y != right.y ? left.y < right.y : left.z < right.z;
            });
            members.erase(std::unique(members.begin(), members.end(), [](Vec3 left, Vec3 right) {
                return left.x == right.x && left.y == right.y && left.z == right.z;
            }), members.end());
            return members.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, Matrix>) {
            if (!value.valid() || !std::all_of(value.values.begin(), value.values.end(), [](double member) { return std::isfinite(member); })) return std::nullopt;
            return value.values.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, RelationValue>) {
            auto pairs = value.pairs;
            if (std::any_of(pairs.begin(), pairs.end(), [](const auto& pair) { return pair.first.empty() || pair.second.empty(); })) return std::nullopt;
            std::sort(pairs.begin(), pairs.end());
            pairs.erase(std::unique(pairs.begin(), pairs.end()), pairs.end());
            return pairs.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, GraphValue>) {
            return finite_graph_whole(value) ? std::optional<std::size_t>{value.vertices.size()} : std::nullopt;
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, ProbabilityValue>) {
            if (value.outcomes.size() != value.weights.size() ||
                !std::all_of(value.weights.begin(), value.weights.end(), [](double weight) { return std::isfinite(weight) && weight >= 0.0; })) return std::nullopt;
            std::unordered_set<std::string> outcomes;
            for (const auto& outcome : value.outcomes) if (outcome.empty() || !outcomes.insert(outcome).second) return std::nullopt;
            return outcomes.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, OperadTreeValue>) {
            return value.labels.empty() || value.valid() ? std::optional<std::size_t>{value.labels.size()} : std::nullopt;
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, OperadSubstitutions>) {
            std::unordered_set<std::string> slots;
            for (const auto& graft : value.grafts)
                if (graft.slot.empty() || !slots.insert(graft.slot).second || !graft.tree.valid()) return std::nullopt;
            return value.grafts.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, VoronoiDiagram>) {
            if (value.sites.size() != value.cells.size() ||
                !std::all_of(value.sites.begin(), value.sites.end(), [](Vec2 point) {
                    return std::isfinite(point.x) && std::isfinite(point.y);
                })) return std::nullopt;
            for (const auto& cell : value.cells)
                if (!std::all_of(cell.begin(), cell.end(), [](Vec2 point) {
                        return std::isfinite(point.x) && std::isfinite(point.y);
                    })) return std::nullopt;
            auto sites = value.sites;
            std::sort(sites.begin(), sites.end(), [](Vec2 left, Vec2 right) {
                return left.x != right.x ? left.x < right.x : left.y < right.y;
            });
            sites.erase(std::unique(sites.begin(), sites.end(), [](Vec2 left, Vec2 right) {
                return left.x == right.x && left.y == right.y;
            }), sites.end());
            return sites.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, FreeModuleValue>) {
            if (value.ring.empty() || value.coordinates.size() != value.basis.size() ||
                !std::all_of(value.coordinates.begin(), value.coordinates.end(), [](double coordinate) { return std::isfinite(coordinate); })) return std::nullopt;
            std::unordered_set<std::string> basis;
            for (const auto& member : value.basis) if (member.empty() || !basis.insert(member).second) return std::nullopt;
            return basis.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, DivinandValue>) {
            if (value.catalog_extent != value.units.size() || value.units.size() != value.assigned_operators.size()) return std::nullopt;
            std::unordered_set<std::string> units, operators;
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < value.units.size(); ++i)
                if (value.units[i].empty() || value.assigned_operators[i].empty() ||
                    !units.insert(value.units[i]).second || !operators.insert(value.assigned_operators[i]).second) return std::nullopt;
            return value.units.size();
        } else {
            return std::nullopt;
        }
    }, operand.body);
}

inline bool normalized_probability(const ProbabilityValue& probability) {
    if (probability.outcomes.empty() || probability.outcomes.size() != probability.weights.size()) return false;
    std::unordered_set<std::string> outcomes;
    double total = 0.0;
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < probability.outcomes.size(); ++i) {
        if (probability.outcomes[i].empty() || !outcomes.insert(probability.outcomes[i]).second ||
            !std::isfinite(probability.weights[i]) || probability.weights[i] < 0.0) return false;
        total += probability.weights[i];
    }
    return std::isfinite(total) && std::abs(total - 1.0) <= 1e-10 * (std::max)(std::size_t{1}, probability.weights.size());
}

inline bool normalized_weights(const NumberList& weights) {
    if (weights.empty()) return false;
    double total = 0.0;
    for (const auto weight : weights) {
        if (!std::isfinite(weight) || weight < 0.0) return false;
        total += weight;
    }
    return std::isfinite(total) && std::abs(total - 1.0) <= 1e-10 * (std::max)(std::size_t{1}, weights.size());
}

inline bool valid_workspace_utf8(std::string_view value) noexcept {
    if (value.empty()) return true;
    if (value.size() > static_cast<std::size_t>((std::numeric_limits<int>::max)())) return false;
    return MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, MB_ERR_INVALID_CHARS, value.data(),
                               static_cast<int>(value.size()), nullptr, 0) > 0;
}

inline bool operand_within_workspace_bounds(const Operand& operand) {
    constexpr std::size_t collection_limit = 65536;
    constexpr std::size_t string_limit = 1024ull * 1024ull;
    const auto valid_names = [=](const NameList& values) {
        return values.size() <= collection_limit &&
            std::all_of(values.begin(), values.end(), [=](const std::string& value) {
                return value.size() <= string_limit && valid_workspace_utf8(value);
            });
    };
    return std::visit([&](const auto& value) -> bool {
        using T = std::decay_t<decltype(value)>;
        if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, std::string>) {
            return value.size() <= string_limit && valid_workspace_utf8(value);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, NumberList> || std::is_same_v<T, ComplexList> ||
                             std::is_same_v<T, Point2List> || std::is_same_v<T, Point3List>) {
            return value.size() <= collection_limit;
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, NameList>) {
            return valid_names(value);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, Matrix>) {
            if (value.rows > collection_limit || value.columns > collection_limit ||
                value.values.size() > collection_limit || ((value.rows == 0) != (value.columns == 0)) ||
                (value.rows != 0 && value.columns > (std::numeric_limits<std::size_t>::max)() / value.rows)) return false;
            return value.rows * value.columns == value.values.size() && value.valid();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, RelationValue>) {
            return value.pairs.size() <= collection_limit &&
                std::all_of(value.pairs.begin(), value.pairs.end(), [=](const auto& pair) {
                    return pair.first.size() <= string_limit && pair.second.size() <= string_limit &&
                           valid_workspace_utf8(pair.first) && valid_workspace_utf8(pair.second);
                });
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, GraphValue>) {
            if (!valid_names(value.vertices) || value.edges.size() > collection_limit) return false;
            std::unordered_set<std::string> vertices(value.vertices.begin(), value.vertices.end());
            if (vertices.size() != value.vertices.size()) return false;
            return std::all_of(value.edges.begin(), value.edges.end(), [&](const GraphEdge& edge) {
                return edge.source.size() <= string_limit && edge.target.size() <= string_limit &&
                       valid_workspace_utf8(edge.source) && valid_workspace_utf8(edge.target) &&
                       vertices.contains(edge.source) && vertices.contains(edge.target) && std::isfinite(edge.weight);
            });
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, ProbabilityValue>) {
            return valid_names(value.outcomes) && value.weights.size() == value.outcomes.size();
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, ResourceRoute>) {
            return value.path.size() <= string_limit && valid_workspace_utf8(value.path);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, AuthoredBodyRoute>) {
            return value.route.size() <= string_limit && valid_workspace_utf8(value.route);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, TermValue>) {
            return value.operation.size() <= string_limit && valid_workspace_utf8(value.operation) && valid_names(value.arguments);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, OperadTreeValue>) {
            return valid_names(value.labels) && value.parents.size() <= collection_limit;
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, OperadSubstitutions>) {
            if (value.grafts.size() > collection_limit) return false;
            return std::all_of(value.grafts.begin(), value.grafts.end(), [&](const OperadGraft& graft) {
                return graft.slot.size() <= string_limit && valid_workspace_utf8(graft.slot) &&
                       valid_names(graft.tree.labels) && graft.tree.parents.size() <= collection_limit;
            });
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, VoronoiDiagram>) {
            if (value.sites.size() > collection_limit || value.cells.size() > collection_limit) return false;
            std::size_t points{};
            for (const auto& cell : value.cells) {
                if (cell.size() > collection_limit - points) return false;
                points += cell.size();
            }
            return true;
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, FreeModuleValue>) {
            return value.ring.size() <= string_limit && valid_workspace_utf8(value.ring) &&
                   valid_names(value.basis) && value.coordinates.size() <= collection_limit;
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, DivinandValue>) {
            return valid_names(value.units) && valid_names(value.assigned_operators);
        } else return true;
    }, operand.body);
}

struct Expression {
    ExpressionRoute route;
    std::size_t catalog_index{};
    std::vector<Operand> operands;
    std::optional<Operand> value;
    std::string note;
};

namespace canonical_detail {
inline bool claim_expression_replay_work(const Expression& expression,
                                         std::size_t& total,
                                         std::size_t limit);
}

struct Invocation {
    ExpressionRoute expression;
    std::optional<Operand> value;
    std::string note;

    bool exact() const noexcept { return value.has_value(); }
    Operand as_operand() const { return value ? *value : Operand::expression(expression.value); }
};

struct OperandDesignation {
    std::size_t operand_index{};
    Operand value;
    std::string role;
    std::optional<std::size_t> authored_node;
    std::optional<Vec3> spatial_position;
};

struct AppliedOperation {
    ExpressionRoute expression;
    std::size_t operator_world_node{(std::numeric_limits<std::size_t>::max)()};
    std::size_t catalog_index{};
    std::vector<OperandDesignation> operands;
    std::optional<Operand> result;
    std::string consumer;
    std::string purpose;
};

class LightRuntime {
public:
    explicit LightRuntime(std::size_t expression_limit = 65536) : expression_limit_((std::max)(std::size_t{1}, expression_limit)) {}
    Invocation invoke(std::string_view code, std::vector<Operand> operands);
    Invocation invoke_with_validated_prefix(std::string_view code,
                                            std::vector<Operand> operands,
                                            std::size_t prior_route_extent);

    const Expression* find(ExpressionRoute route) const noexcept {
        return route.value < expressions_.size() ? &expressions_[route.value] : nullptr;
    }

    const std::vector<Expression>& expressions() const noexcept { return expressions_; }
    void clear() noexcept { expressions_.clear(); replay_work_retained_ = 0; }
    std::size_t expression_limit() const noexcept { return expression_limit_; }
    std::size_t remaining_expression_capacity() const noexcept { return expression_limit_ - expressions_.size(); }
    std::size_t replay_work_retained() const noexcept { return replay_work_retained_; }
    std::size_t replay_work_limit() const noexcept { return replay_work_limit_; }
    // Restoration is deliberately separate from invocation: a complete parsed
    // expression ledger is validated first, then swapped in as one mutation.
    bool restore_expressions(std::vector<Expression> expressions, std::string& error,
                             std::size_t maximum_replay_work = 64000000);

private:
    std::optional<Operand> try_realize(const LightDefinition& definition,
                                       const std::vector<Operand>& operands,
                                       std::string& note);
    std::vector<Expression> expressions_;
    std::size_t expression_limit_{};
    std::size_t replay_work_retained_{};
    std::size_t replay_prior_route_extent_{};
    static constexpr std::size_t replay_work_limit_{64000000};
};

inline std::optional<AppliedOperation> designate_applied_operation(
    const LightRuntime& runtime,
    ExpressionRoute route,
    std::span<const std::string_view> roles = {},
    std::string consumer = {},
    std::string purpose = {}) {
    const auto* expression = runtime.find(route);
    if (!expression) return std::nullopt;
    AppliedOperation applied{route, expression->catalog_index, expression->catalog_index, {}, expression->value,
                             std::move(consumer), std::move(purpose)};
    applied.operands.reserve(expression->operands.size());
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < expression->operands.size(); ++i) {
        applied.operands.push_back(OperandDesignation{i, expression->operands[i],
            i < roles.size() ? std::string(roles[i]) : "operand", std::nullopt, std::nullopt});
    }
    return applied;
}

inline Invocation LightRuntime::invoke(std::string_view code, std::vector<Operand> operands) {
    if (expressions_.size() >= expression_limit_) throw std::length_error("Light expression retention bound reached; deliberately clear or open a fresh ephemeral runtime");
    const auto* definition = find_light_by_code(code);
    if (!definition) throw std::invalid_argument("unknown Light code: " + std::string(code));
    if (operands.size() < definition->minimum_operands || operands.size() > definition->maximum_operands) {
        throw std::invalid_argument("Light arity does not match " + std::string(definition->signature));
    }
    for (const Operand& operand : operands) {
        if (!operand_within_workspace_bounds(operand)) {
            throw std::invalid_argument("Light operand exceeds the bounded canonical workspace extent");
        }
        if (const auto* route = std::get_if<ExpressionRoute>(&operand.body);
            route && route->value >= (std::max)(expressions_.size(), replay_prior_route_extent_)) {
            throw std::invalid_argument("Light operand ExpressionRoute is absent, forward, or self-referential");
        }
    }
    const auto prior_expression_count = expressions_.size();
    const auto prior_replay_work = replay_work_retained_;
    Expression work_shape{{}, light_catalog_index(*definition), operands, std::nullopt, {}};
    if (!canonical_detail::claim_expression_replay_work(
            work_shape, replay_work_retained_, replay_work_limit_)) {
        replay_work_retained_ = prior_replay_work;
        throw std::length_error("Light operation exceeds the bounded save-and-replay work extent");
    }
    try {
        std::string note;
        auto value = try_realize(*definition, operands, note);
        if (value && !operand_within_workspace_bounds(*value)) {
            throw std::length_error("Light result exceeds the bounded canonical workspace extent");
        }
        if (note.empty()) note = value ? "exact finite realization" : "preserved symbolic Light expression";
        const ExpressionRoute route{expressions_.size()};
        if (expressions_.size() >= expression_limit_) throw std::length_error("nested Light realization exhausted the expression retention bound");
        expressions_.push_back(Expression{route, light_catalog_index(*definition), std::move(operands), value, note});
        return Invocation{route, std::move(value), std::move(note)};
    } catch (...) {
        expressions_.resize(prior_expression_count);
        replay_work_retained_ = prior_replay_work;
        throw;
    }
}

inline Invocation LightRuntime::invoke_with_validated_prefix(
    std::string_view code, std::vector<Operand> operands,
    std::size_t prior_route_extent) {
    if (!expressions_.empty() || replay_prior_route_extent_ != 0) {
        throw std::logic_error("validated-prefix replay requires a fresh isolated runtime");
    }
    replay_prior_route_extent_ = prior_route_extent;
    try {
        Invocation answer = invoke(code, std::move(operands));
        replay_prior_route_extent_ = 0;
        return answer;
    } catch (...) {
        replay_prior_route_extent_ = 0;
        throw;
    }
}

template <class T>
inline std::vector<T> cyclically_shifted(const std::vector<T>& input, std::int64_t amount) {
    if (input.empty()) return {};
    std::vector<T> answer = input;
    const auto size = static_cast<std::int64_t>(answer.size());
    const auto normalized = ((amount % size) + size) % size;
    std::rotate(answer.begin(), answer.begin() + normalized, answer.end());
    return answer;
}

inline double cross(Vec2 origin, Vec2 a, Vec2 b) noexcept {
    return (a.x - origin.x) * (b.y - origin.y) - (a.y - origin.y) * (b.x - origin.x);
}

inline Point2List finite_convex_hull(Point2List points) {
    if (points.size() < 2) return points;
    std::sort(points.begin(), points.end(), [](Vec2 a, Vec2 b) {
        return a.x < b.x || (a.x == b.x && a.y < b.y);
    });
    points.erase(std::unique(points.begin(), points.end(), [](Vec2 a, Vec2 b) {
        return a.x == b.x && a.y == b.y;
    }), points.end());
    if (points.size() < 3) return points;
    Point2List hull(points.size() * 2);
    std::size_t count = 0;
    for (const auto point : points) {
        while (count >= 2 && cross(hull[count - 2], hull[count - 1], point) <= 0.0) --count;
        hull[count++] = point;
    }
    const auto lower = count + 1;
    for (auto cursor = points.rbegin() + 1; cursor != points.rend(); ++cursor) {
        while (count >= lower && cross(hull[count - 2], hull[count - 1], *cursor) <= 0.0) --count;
        hull[count++] = *cursor;
    }
    hull.resize(count > 1 ? count - 1 : count);
    return hull;
}

inline std::optional<NumberList> solve_square(Matrix matrix, NumberList right,
                                               double tolerance = 1e-11) {
    if (!matrix.valid() || matrix.rows != matrix.columns || right.size() != matrix.rows) return std::nullopt;
    const auto n = matrix.rows;
    for (std::size_t column = 0; column < n; ++column) {
        std::size_t pivot = column;
        for (std::size_t row = column + 1; row < n; ++row)
            if (std::abs(matrix.at(row, column)) > std::abs(matrix.at(pivot, column))) pivot = row;
        if (std::abs(matrix.at(pivot, column)) <= tolerance) return std::nullopt;
        if (pivot != column) {
            for (std::size_t j = column; j < n; ++j) std::swap(matrix.values[pivot * n + j], matrix.values[column * n + j]);
            std::swap(right[pivot], right[column]);
        }
        const auto divisor = matrix.at(column, column);
        for (std::size_t j = column; j < n; ++j) matrix.values[column * n + j] /= divisor;
        right[column] /= divisor;
        for (std::size_t row = 0; row < n; ++row) if (row != column) {
            const auto factor = matrix.at(row, column);
            if (std::abs(factor) <= tolerance) continue;
            for (std::size_t j = column; j < n; ++j) matrix.values[row * n + j] -= factor * matrix.at(column, j);
            right[row] -= factor * right[column];
        }
    }
    return right;
}

inline std::size_t real_matrix_rank(Matrix matrix, double tolerance = 1e-10) {
    if (!matrix.valid()) return 0;
    std::size_t rank = 0;
    for (std::size_t column = 0; column < matrix.columns && rank < matrix.rows; ++column) {
        std::size_t pivot = rank;
        for (std::size_t row = rank + 1; row < matrix.rows; ++row)
            if (std::abs(matrix.at(row, column)) > std::abs(matrix.at(pivot, column))) pivot = row;
        if (std::abs(matrix.at(pivot, column)) <= tolerance) continue;
        for (std::size_t j = column; j < matrix.columns; ++j) std::swap(matrix.values[pivot * matrix.columns + j], matrix.values[rank * matrix.columns + j]);
        const auto divisor = matrix.at(rank, column);
        for (std::size_t j = column; j < matrix.columns; ++j) matrix.values[rank * matrix.columns + j] /= divisor;
        for (std::size_t row = 0; row < matrix.rows; ++row) if (row != rank) {
            const auto factor = matrix.at(row, column);
            for (std::size_t j = column; j < matrix.columns; ++j) matrix.values[row * matrix.columns + j] -= factor * matrix.at(rank, j);
        }
        ++rank;
    }
    return rank;
}

inline std::size_t binary_matrix_rank(Matrix matrix) {
    if (!matrix.valid()) return 0;
    for (auto& value : matrix.values) value = std::fmod(std::abs(std::round(value)), 2.0);
    std::size_t rank = 0;
    for (std::size_t column = 0; column < matrix.columns && rank < matrix.rows; ++column) {
        std::size_t pivot = rank;
        while (pivot < matrix.rows && matrix.values[pivot * matrix.columns + column] == 0.0) ++pivot;
        if (pivot == matrix.rows) continue;
        for (std::size_t j = 0; j < matrix.columns; ++j) std::swap(matrix.values[pivot * matrix.columns + j], matrix.values[rank * matrix.columns + j]);
        for (std::size_t row = 0; row < matrix.rows; ++row) if (row != rank && matrix.values[row * matrix.columns + column] != 0.0)
            for (std::size_t j = column; j < matrix.columns; ++j)
                matrix.values[row * matrix.columns + j] = std::fmod(matrix.values[row * matrix.columns + j] + matrix.values[rank * matrix.columns + j], 2.0);
        ++rank;
    }
    return rank;
}

inline Point2List clip_half_plane(const Point2List& polygon, double a, double b, double c) {
    Point2List result;
    if (polygon.empty()) return result;
    const auto signed_distance = [=](Vec2 point) { return a * point.x + b * point.y - c; };
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < polygon.size(); ++i) {
        const auto current = polygon[i];
        const auto next = polygon[(i + 1) % polygon.size()];
        const auto dc = signed_distance(current), dn = signed_distance(next);
        const bool current_inside = dc <= 1e-9, next_inside = dn <= 1e-9;
