        if (current_inside) result.push_back(current);
        if (current_inside != next_inside) {
            const auto fraction = dc / (dc - dn);
            result.push_back({current.x + fraction * (next.x - current.x), current.y + fraction * (next.y - current.y)});
        }
    }
    return result;
}

inline VoronoiDiagram finite_voronoi(const Point2List& sites) {
    VoronoiDiagram diagram{sites, {}};
    if (sites.empty()) return diagram;
    double min_x = sites[0].x, max_x = sites[0].x, min_y = sites[0].y, max_y = sites[0].y;
    for (const auto site : sites) {
        min_x = (std::min)(min_x, site.x); max_x = (std::max)(max_x, site.x);
        min_y = (std::min)(min_y, site.y); max_y = (std::max)(max_y, site.y);
    }
    const auto margin = (std::max)({max_x - min_x, max_y - min_y, 1.0}) * 2.0;
    const Point2List bounds{{min_x - margin, min_y - margin}, {max_x + margin, min_y - margin},
                            {max_x + margin, max_y + margin}, {min_x - margin, max_y + margin}};
    diagram.cells.reserve(sites.size());
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < sites.size(); ++i) {
        auto cell = bounds;
        for (std::size_t j = 0; j < sites.size() && !cell.empty(); ++j) if (i != j) {
            const auto a = 2.0 * (sites[j].x - sites[i].x);
            const auto b = 2.0 * (sites[j].y - sites[i].y);
            const auto c = sites[j].x * sites[j].x + sites[j].y * sites[j].y - sites[i].x * sites[i].x - sites[i].y * sites[i].y;
            cell = clip_half_plane(cell, a, b, c);
        }
        diagram.cells.push_back(std::move(cell));
    }
    return diagram;
}

inline NameList split_set_label(std::string_view label) {
    NameList result;
    std::size_t begin = 0;
    while (begin <= label.size()) {
        const auto end = label.find('|', begin);
        result.emplace_back(label.substr(begin, end == std::string_view::npos ? label.size() - begin : end - begin));
        if (end == std::string_view::npos) break;
        begin = end + 1;
    }
    std::sort(result.begin(), result.end());
    result.erase(std::unique(result.begin(), result.end()), result.end());
    return result;
}

inline std::string intersect_set_labels(std::string_view left, std::string_view right) {
    const auto a = split_set_label(left), b = split_set_label(right);
    NameList intersection;
    std::set_intersection(a.begin(), a.end(), b.begin(), b.end(), std::back_inserter(intersection));
    std::string result;
    for (const auto& name : intersection) { if (!result.empty()) result.push_back('|'); result += name; }
    return result;
}

struct FinitePosetView {
    NameList members;
    std::vector<bool> less_equal;

    bool leq(std::size_t left, std::size_t right) const noexcept {
        return left < members.size() && right < members.size() &&
               less_equal[left * members.size() + right];
    }
};

inline std::optional<FinitePosetView> finite_poset_view(const RelationValue& relation,
                                                        std::size_t maximum_members = 256) {
    NameList members;
    members.reserve(relation.pairs.size() * 2);
    for (const auto& [left, right] : relation.pairs) {
        if (left.empty() || right.empty()) return std::nullopt;
        members.push_back(left); members.push_back(right);
    }
    std::sort(members.begin(), members.end());
    members.erase(std::unique(members.begin(), members.end()), members.end());
    if (members.empty() || members.size() > maximum_members) return std::nullopt;
    std::vector<bool> leq(members.size() * members.size(), false);
    for (const auto& [left, right] : relation.pairs) {
        const auto i = static_cast<std::size_t>(std::lower_bound(members.begin(), members.end(), left) - members.begin());
        const auto j = static_cast<std::size_t>(std::lower_bound(members.begin(), members.end(), right) - members.begin());
        if (leq[i * members.size() + j]) return std::nullopt;
        leq[i * members.size() + j] = true;
    }
    const auto n = members.size();
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < n; ++i) if (!leq[i * n + i]) return std::nullopt;
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < n; ++i) for (std::size_t j = 0; j < n; ++j) {
        if (i != j && leq[i * n + j] && leq[j * n + i]) return std::nullopt;
        if (!leq[i * n + j]) continue;
        for (std::size_t k = 0; k < n; ++k)
            if (leq[j * n + k] && !leq[i * n + k]) return std::nullopt;
    }
    return FinitePosetView{std::move(members), std::move(leq)};
}

struct LambdaTerm {
    enum class Kind : std::uint8_t { variable, abstraction, application } kind{Kind::variable};
    std::string name;
    std::vector<LambdaTerm> children;
};

class FiniteLambdaParser {
public:
    explicit FiniteLambdaParser(std::string_view source) : source_(source) { advance(); }

    std::optional<LambdaTerm> parse() {
        auto term = parse_term(0);
        skip_space();
        if (!term || token_.kind != TokenKind::end) return std::nullopt;
        return term;
    }

private:
    enum class TokenKind : std::uint8_t { identifier, lambda, dot, left, right, end, invalid };
    struct Token { TokenKind kind{TokenKind::invalid}; std::string text; };

    void skip_space() {
        while (position_ < source_.size() && std::isspace(static_cast<unsigned char>(source_[position_]))) ++position_;
    }

    void advance() {
        skip_space();
        if (position_ == source_.size()) { token_ = {TokenKind::end, {}}; return; }
        const char c = source_[position_];
        if (c == '.') { ++position_; token_ = {TokenKind::dot, "."}; return; }
        if (c == '(') { ++position_; token_ = {TokenKind::left, "("}; return; }
        if (c == ')') { ++position_; token_ = {TokenKind::right, ")"}; return; }
        if (c == '\\') { ++position_; token_ = {TokenKind::lambda, "lambda"}; return; }
        const auto byte = static_cast<unsigned char>(c);
        if (std::isalpha(byte) || c == '_') {
            const auto begin = position_++;
            while (position_ < source_.size()) {
                const auto next = static_cast<unsigned char>(source_[position_]);
                if (!(std::isalnum(next) || source_[position_] == '_')) break;
                ++position_;
            }
            std::string text(source_.substr(begin, position_ - begin));
            token_ = {text == "lambda" ? TokenKind::lambda : TokenKind::identifier, std::move(text)};
            return;
        }
        ++position_;
        token_ = {TokenKind::invalid, std::string(1, c)};
    }

    std::optional<LambdaTerm> parse_term(std::size_t depth) {
        if (depth > 256) return std::nullopt;
        if (token_.kind == TokenKind::lambda) {
            advance();
            if (token_.kind != TokenKind::identifier) return std::nullopt;
            std::string binder = token_.text;
            advance();
            if (token_.kind != TokenKind::dot) return std::nullopt;
            advance();
            auto body = parse_term(depth + 1);
            if (!body) return std::nullopt;
            return LambdaTerm{LambdaTerm::Kind::abstraction, std::move(binder), {std::move(*body)}};
        }
        return parse_application(depth);
    }

    std::optional<LambdaTerm> parse_application(std::size_t depth) {
        std::vector<LambdaTerm> terms;
        while (token_.kind == TokenKind::identifier || token_.kind == TokenKind::left) {
            auto atom = parse_atom(depth);
            if (!atom) return std::nullopt;
            terms.push_back(std::move(*atom));
        }
        if (terms.empty()) return std::nullopt;
        if (terms.size() == 1) return std::move(terms.front());
        return LambdaTerm{LambdaTerm::Kind::application, {}, std::move(terms)};
    }

    std::optional<LambdaTerm> parse_atom(std::size_t depth) {
        if (token_.kind == TokenKind::identifier) {
            LambdaTerm term{LambdaTerm::Kind::variable, token_.text, {}};
            advance();
            return term;
        }
        if (token_.kind == TokenKind::left) {
            advance();
            auto term = parse_term(depth + 1);
            if (!term || token_.kind != TokenKind::right) return std::nullopt;
            advance();
            return term;
        }
        return std::nullopt;
    }

    std::string_view source_;
    std::size_t position_{};
    Token token_;
};

inline bool lambda_term_contains_name(const LambdaTerm& term, std::string_view name) {
    if (term.name == name) return true;
    return std::any_of(term.children.begin(), term.children.end(), [&](const LambdaTerm& child) {
        return lambda_term_contains_name(child, name);
    });
}

inline void alpha_rename_outer_occurrences(LambdaTerm& term,
                                           std::string_view old_name,
                                           std::string_view fresh_name,
                                           bool shadowed = false) {
    if (term.kind == LambdaTerm::Kind::variable) {
        if (!shadowed && term.name == old_name) term.name = fresh_name;
        return;
    }
    if (term.kind == LambdaTerm::Kind::abstraction) {
        const bool nested_shadow = shadowed || term.name == old_name;
        alpha_rename_outer_occurrences(term.children.front(), old_name, fresh_name, nested_shadow);
        return;
    }
    for (auto& child : term.children) alpha_rename_outer_occurrences(child, old_name, fresh_name, shadowed);
}

inline std::string canonical_lambda_term(const LambdaTerm& term, bool in_application = false) {
    if (term.kind == LambdaTerm::Kind::variable) return term.name;
    if (term.kind == LambdaTerm::Kind::abstraction) {
        std::string result = "lambda " + term.name + ". " + canonical_lambda_term(term.children.front());
        return in_application ? "(" + result + ")" : result;
    }
    std::string result;
    for (const auto& child : term.children) {
        if (!result.empty()) result.push_back(' ');
        result += canonical_lambda_term(child, true);
    }
    return in_application ? "(" + result + ")" : result;
}

inline std::optional<Operand> LightRuntime::try_realize(const LightDefinition& definition,
                                                         const std::vector<Operand>& operands,
                                                         std::string& note) {
    const auto code = definition.code;
    const auto number = [&operands](std::size_t index) -> std::optional<double> {
        return index < operands.size() && operands[index].numeric()
            ? std::optional<double>{operands[index].as_number()} : std::nullopt;
    };
    const auto binary_numbers = [&]() -> std::optional<std::pair<double, double>> {
        const auto a = number(0);
        const auto b = number(1);
        return a && b ? std::optional<std::pair<double, double>>{{*a, *b}} : std::nullopt;
    };

    if (code == "divinand") {
        const auto* operations = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (!operations || operations->size() > 64) {
            note = "MY LIGHT requires one exact typed whole and a bounded finite route of Light operation names";
            return std::nullopt;
        }
        if (std::holds_alternative<ExpressionRoute>(operands[0].body)) {
            // A generic Operand never fabricates the measured-bit ancestry of a
            // whole.  Prior ExpressionRoutes remain valid authored associations,
            // but applying their values belongs to the whole-self layer where
            // the prior ledger and its exact associations are available.
            note = "MY LIGHT retained the supplied ExpressionRoute and operation route symbolically; generic replay cannot invent the referenced whole's measured-bit ancestry";
            return std::nullopt;
        }
        Operand current = operands[0];
        for (const auto& operation_name : *operations) {
            const auto* operation = find_light_by_code(operation_name);
            if (!operation) operation = find_light_by_self_number(operation_name);
            if (!operation || operation->minimum_operands != 1 ||
                operation->maximum_operands != 1 || operation->code == "divinand") {
                note = "MY LIGHT route requires every named step to be a present unary Light operation";
                return std::nullopt;
            }
            std::string step_note;
            auto derived = try_realize(*operation, {current}, step_note);
            if (!derived) {
                note = "MY LIGHT retained its source whole and finite route, but a named unary step was incompatible with the current exact typed view";
                return std::nullopt;
            }
            current = std::move(*derived);
        }
        note = "divinand carrier retains the exact supplied typed whole and finite unary Light route in this Expression; RESULT is their exact sequential derivation";
        return current;
    }
    if (code == "sub" || code == "add") {
        if (const auto values = binary_numbers()) {
            return Operand::number(code == "add" ? values->first + values->second : values->first - values->second);
        }
        if (const auto* a = std::get_if<Vec2>(&operands[0].body)) {
            if (const auto* b = std::get_if<Vec2>(&operands[1].body)) return Operand::point(code == "add" ? *a + *b : *a - *b);
        }
        if (const auto* a = std::get_if<Vec3>(&operands[0].body)) {
            if (const auto* b = std::get_if<Vec3>(&operands[1].body)) {
                return Operand::point(code == "add" ? *a + *b : Vec3{a->x - b->x, a->y - b->y, a->z - b->z});
            }
        }
        if (const auto* a = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body)) {
            if (const auto* b = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body); b && a->size() == b->size()) {
                NumberList result(a->size());
                for (std::size_t i = 0; i < result.size(); ++i) result[i] = code == "add" ? (*a)[i] + (*b)[i] : (*a)[i] - (*b)[i];
                return Operand::numbers(std::move(result));
            }
        }
    }
    if (code == "mul" || code == "div") {
        if (const auto values = binary_numbers()) {
            if (code == "div" && values->second == 0.0) {
                note = "division by zero remains symbolic";
                return std::nullopt;
            }
            return Operand::number(code == "mul" ? values->first * values->second : values->first / values->second);
        }
        const auto scalar = number(1);
        if (scalar && !(code == "div" && *scalar == 0.0)) {
            const auto factor = code == "mul" ? *scalar : 1.0 / *scalar;
            if (const auto* point = std::get_if<Vec2>(&operands[0].body)) return Operand::point(*point * factor);
            if (const auto* point = std::get_if<Vec3>(&operands[0].body)) return Operand::point(*point * factor);
            if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body)) {
                auto result = *values;
                for (auto& value : result) value *= factor;
                return Operand::numbers(std::move(result));
            }
        }
    }
    if (code == "pow") {
        if (const auto values = binary_numbers()) {
            const auto result = std::pow(values->first, values->second);
            if (std::isfinite(result)) return Operand::number(result);
        }
    }
    if (code == "is_empty") {
        if (const auto cardinality = finite_carrier_cardinality(operands[0])) {
            note = "ZF empty-set test on the exact finite carrier supplied by the typed whole view";
            return Operand::truth(*cardinality == 0);
        }
        note = "EMPTISM requires one well-formed finite carrier; an arbitrary scalar is not silently treated as a set";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "exclusive_or") {
        bool a{}, b{};
        if (truth_operand(operands[0], a) && truth_operand(operands[1], b)) return Operand::truth(a != b);
    }
    if (code == "bottom") {
        if (const auto* domain = std::get_if<TermValue>(&operands[0].body);
            domain && domain->operation == "singleton_pointed_domain" &&
            domain->arguments == NameList{"bottom"}) {
            note = "domain-tagged bottom of the exact singleton pointed domain reconstructed from a published version-1 bottom value";
            return Operand::term(TermValue{"bottom", {"bottom"}});
        }
        const auto* domain = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto poset = domain ? finite_poset_view(*domain) : std::nullopt;
        if (poset) {
            for (std::size_t candidate = 0; candidate < poset->members.size(); ++candidate) {
                bool least = true;
                for (std::size_t member = 0; member < poset->members.size(); ++member)
                    least = least && poset->leq(candidate, member);
                if (least) {
                    note = "domain-tagged bottom: the returned term names the unique member below every member of the exact supplied finite pointed domain; the enclosing expression retains that domain";
                    return Operand::term(TermValue{"bottom", {poset->members[candidate]}});
                }
            }
        }
        note = "NULLISM requires one exact nonempty finite partial order with a least member";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "zero") return Operand::integer(0);
    if (code == "heyting_not") {
        const auto* frame = std::get_if<GraphValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* proposition = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (frame && proposition && finite_graph_whole(*frame) && frame->vertices.size() <= 65536) {
            std::unordered_map<std::string, std::size_t> index;
            index.reserve(frame->vertices.size());
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < frame->vertices.size(); ++i) index.emplace(frame->vertices[i], i);
            std::vector<std::vector<std::size_t>> forward(frame->vertices.size()), reverse(frame->vertices.size());
            std::vector<std::size_t> indegree(frame->vertices.size());
            for (const auto& edge : frame->edges) {
                const auto source = index.at(edge.source), target = index.at(edge.target);
                if (source == target) continue;
                forward[source].push_back(target); reverse[target].push_back(source); ++indegree[target];
            }
            std::queue<std::size_t> acyclic;
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < indegree.size(); ++i) if (indegree[i] == 0) acyclic.push(i);
            std::size_t visited{};
            while (!acyclic.empty()) {
                const auto source = acyclic.front(); acyclic.pop(); ++visited;
                for (const auto target : forward[source]) if (--indegree[target] == 0) acyclic.push(target);
            }
            if (visited != frame->vertices.size()) {
                note = "finite Heyting frame must be a partial order; a directed cycle was supplied";
                return std::nullopt;
            }
            std::vector<bool> in_proposition(frame->vertices.size(), false);
            for (const auto& member : *proposition) {
                const auto found = index.find(member);
                if (found == index.end() || in_proposition[found->second]) {
                    note = "finite Heyting proposition must be a unique subset of the supplied frame";
                    return std::nullopt;
                }
                in_proposition[found->second] = true;
            }
            std::queue<std::size_t> upward;
            std::vector<bool> upward_reached = in_proposition;
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < in_proposition.size(); ++i) if (in_proposition[i]) upward.push(i);
            while (!upward.empty()) {
                const auto source = upward.front(); upward.pop();
                for (const auto target : forward[source]) if (!upward_reached[target]) {
                    upward_reached[target] = true; upward.push(target);
                }
            }
            if (upward_reached != in_proposition) {
                note = "finite Heyting proposition must be an upward-closed set";
                return std::nullopt;
            }
            std::queue<std::size_t> reaches_proposition;
            std::vector<bool> can_reach = in_proposition;
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < in_proposition.size(); ++i) if (in_proposition[i]) reaches_proposition.push(i);
            while (!reaches_proposition.empty()) {
                const auto target = reaches_proposition.front(); reaches_proposition.pop();
                for (const auto source : reverse[target]) if (!can_reach[source]) {
                    can_reach[source] = true; reaches_proposition.push(source);
                }
            }
            NameList pseudocomplement;
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < frame->vertices.size(); ++i)
                if (!can_reach[i]) pseudocomplement.push_back(frame->vertices[i]);
            note = "finite Heyting pseudocomplement: exactly the worlds whose upward cones are disjoint from P";
            return Operand::names(std::move(pseudocomplement));
        }
    }
    if (code == "rule30") {
        bool left{}, center{}, right{};
        if (truth_operand(operands[0], left) && truth_operand(operands[1], center) && truth_operand(operands[2], right)) {
            const unsigned pattern = (left ? 4u : 0u) | (center ? 2u : 0u) | (right ? 1u : 0u);
            return Operand::truth(((30u >> pattern) & 1u) != 0u);
        }
    }
    if (code == "delete_vertex") {
        const auto* graph = std::get_if<GraphValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* vertex = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[1].body);
        if (graph && vertex) {
            GraphValue result = *graph;
            std::erase(result.vertices, *vertex);
            std::erase_if(result.edges, [&](const GraphEdge& edge) { return edge.source == *vertex || edge.target == *vertex; });
            return Operand::graph(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "converse") {
        if (const auto* relation = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&operands[0].body)) {
            RelationValue result = *relation;
            for (auto& pair : result.pairs) std::swap(pair.first, pair.second);
            return Operand::relation(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "minimax_loss") {
        if (const auto* matrix = std::get_if<Matrix>(&operands[0].body); matrix && matrix->valid() && matrix->rows && matrix->columns) {
            double best = (std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity)();
            for (std::size_t row = 0; row < matrix->rows; ++row) {
                double worst = -(std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity)();
                for (std::size_t column = 0; column < matrix->columns; ++column) worst = (std::max)(worst, matrix->at(row, column));
                best = (std::min)(best, worst);
            }
            return Operand::number(best);
        }
    }
    if (code == "recip_inf") {
        if (const auto value = number(0); value && !std::isnan(*value)) {
            if (std::isinf(*value)) return Operand::complexes({{0.0, 0.0}, {1.0, 0.0}});
            return Operand::complexes({{1.0, 0.0}, {*value, 0.0}});
        }
        if (const auto* homogeneous = std::get_if<ComplexList>(&operands[0].body);
            homogeneous && homogeneous->size() == 2 &&
            std::isfinite((*homogeneous)[0].real()) && std::isfinite((*homogeneous)[0].imag()) &&
            std::isfinite((*homogeneous)[1].real()) && std::isfinite((*homogeneous)[1].imag()) &&
            ((*homogeneous)[0] != std::complex<double>{} || (*homogeneous)[1] != std::complex<double>{})) {
            return Operand::complexes({(*homogeneous)[1], (*homogeneous)[0]});
        }
    }
    if (code == "forward_diff") {
        const auto* sequence = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        std::int64_t index{};
        if (sequence && integral_operand(operands[1], index) && index >= 0 && static_cast<std::size_t>(index + 1) < sequence->size()) {
            return Operand::number((*sequence)[static_cast<std::size_t>(index + 1)] - (*sequence)[static_cast<std::size_t>(index)]);
        }
    }
    if (code == "diagonal") {
        if (const auto value = number(0)) return Operand::numbers({*value, *value});
        if (const auto* value = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[0].body)) return Operand::names({*value, *value});
    }
    if (code == "luk_or") {
        if (const auto values = binary_numbers(); values && std::isfinite(values->first) && std::isfinite(values->second) &&
            values->first >= 0.0 && values->first <= 1.0 && values->second >= 0.0 && values->second <= 1.0) {
            note = "bounded Lukasiewicz t-conorm min(1,a+b) on two supplied membership degrees";
            return Operand::number((std::min)(1.0, values->first + values->second));
        }
        note = "LOVELY requires two finite membership degrees in [0,1]";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "aitken") {
        const auto a = number(0), b = number(1), c = number(2);
        if (a && b && c) {
            const auto denominator = *c - 2.0 * *b + *a;
            if (denominator != 0.0) return Operand::number(*a - (*b - *a) * (*b - *a) / denominator);
        }
    }
    if (code == "discrete_partition") {
        if (const auto* names = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[0].body)) {
            RelationValue result;
            for (const auto& name : *names) result.pairs.emplace_back(name, name);
            return Operand::relation(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "bayes") {
        const auto* prior = std::get_if<ProbabilityValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* likelihood = std::get_if<ProbabilityValue>(&operands[1].body);
        const bool finite_likelihood = likelihood && likelihood->outcomes.size() == likelihood->weights.size() &&
            std::all_of(likelihood->weights.begin(), likelihood->weights.end(), [](double weight) {
                return std::isfinite(weight) && weight >= 0.0 && weight <= 1.0;
            });
        if (prior && likelihood && prior->outcomes == likelihood->outcomes &&
            normalized_probability(*prior) && finite_likelihood) {
            ProbabilityValue posterior{prior->outcomes, NumberList(prior->weights.size())};
            double evidence = 0.0;
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < posterior.weights.size(); ++i) evidence += posterior.weights[i] = prior->weights[i] * likelihood->weights[i];
            if (evidence > 0.0) {
                for (auto& weight : posterior.weights) weight /= evidence;
                note = "Bayes update: the normalized posterior is proportional to the supplied normalized prior times likelihood";
                return Operand::probability(std::move(posterior));
            }
        }
        note = "EDUCATION requires a normalized finite prior, matching [0,1] likelihoods, and positive evidence";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "reduce_free") {
        if (const auto* word = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[0].body)) {
            std::string result;
            for (const char letter : *word) {
                if (!result.empty() && std::isalpha(static_cast<unsigned char>(letter)) &&
                    std::tolower(static_cast<unsigned char>(result.back())) == std::tolower(static_cast<unsigned char>(letter)) &&
                    std::isupper(static_cast<unsigned char>(result.back())) != std::isupper(static_cast<unsigned char>(letter))) result.pop_back();
                else result.push_back(letter);
            }
            return Operand::text(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "nearest_decode") {
        const auto* words = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* received = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[1].body);
        const auto binary_word = [](const std::string& word) {
            return !word.empty() && word.size() <= 4096 &&
                   std::all_of(word.begin(), word.end(), [](char bit) { return bit == '0' || bit == '1'; });
        };
        if (words && received && !words->empty() && binary_word(*received)) {
            auto codewords = *words;
            std::sort(codewords.begin(), codewords.end());
            if (std::adjacent_find(codewords.begin(), codewords.end()) != codewords.end() ||
                !std::all_of(codewords.begin(), codewords.end(), [&](const std::string& word) {
                    return binary_word(word) && word.size() == received->size();
                })) {
                note = "RESILIENCE requires distinct fixed-length binary codewords matching the received word";
                return std::nullopt;
            }
            const auto distance = [received](const std::string& word) {
                return static_cast<std::size_t>(std::inner_product(
                    word.begin(), word.end(), received->begin(), std::size_t{}, std::plus<>{}, std::not_equal_to<>{}));
            };
            const auto decoded = std::min_element(codewords.begin(), codewords.end(), [&](const auto& left, const auto& right) {
                const auto left_distance = distance(left), right_distance = distance(right);
                return left_distance != right_distance ? left_distance < right_distance : left < right;
            });
            note = "nearest fixed-length binary codeword by Hamming distance; lexicographic order resolves an exact tie deterministically";
            return Operand::text(*decoded);
        }
        note = "RESILIENCE requires a nonempty finite binary code and one same-length received word";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "huber") {
        if (const auto values = binary_numbers(); values && values->second > 0.0) {
            const auto magnitude = std::abs(values->first);
            return Operand::number(magnitude <= values->second ? 0.5 * magnitude * magnitude
                                                               : values->second * (magnitude - 0.5 * values->second));
        }
    }
    if (code == "mix") {
        const auto* choice = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        const auto reorder = [choice](const auto& values) -> std::optional<std::decay_t<decltype(values)>> {
            using List = std::decay_t<decltype(values)>;
            if (!choice || choice->size() != values.size()) return std::nullopt;
            std::vector<bool> used(values.size(), false); List result; result.reserve(values.size());
            for (const auto raw : *choice) {
                if (raw < 0.0 || std::floor(raw) != raw || raw >= static_cast<double>(values.size())) return std::nullopt;
                const auto index = static_cast<std::size_t>(raw);
                if (used[index]) return std::nullopt;
                used[index] = true; result.push_back(values[index]);
            }
            return result;
        };
        if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body)) {
            if (auto result = reorder(*values)) return Operand::numbers(std::move(*result));
        }
        if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[0].body)) {
            if (auto result = reorder(*values)) return Operand::names(std::move(*result));
        }
        std::int64_t seed{};
        if (integral_operand(operands[1], seed)) {
            std::mt19937_64 generator(static_cast<std::uint64_t>(seed));
            const auto fisher_yates = [&generator](auto values) {
                for (std::size_t remaining = values.size(); remaining > 1; --remaining) {
                    const auto bound = static_cast<std::uint64_t>(remaining);
                    const auto rejection_floor = (std::uint64_t{0} - bound) % bound;
                    std::uint64_t draw{};
                    do { draw = generator(); } while (draw < rejection_floor);
                    std::swap(values[remaining - 1], values[static_cast<std::size_t>(draw % bound)]);
                }
                return values;
            };
            if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body)) return Operand::numbers(fisher_yates(*values));
            if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[0].body)) return Operand::names(fisher_yates(*values));
        }
    }
    if (code == "l_system_step") {
        const auto* word = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* rules = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&operands[1].body);
        if (word && rules) {
            std::string result;
            for (const char symbol : *word) {
                const std::string key(1, symbol);
                const auto rule = std::find_if(rules->pairs.begin(), rules->pairs.end(), [&](const auto& pair) { return pair.first == key; });
                result += rule == rules->pairs.end() ? key : rule->second;
            }
            return Operand::text(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "delay_k") {
        const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        std::int64_t delay{};
        const auto fill = number(2);
        if (values && integral_operand(operands[1], delay) && delay >= 0 && fill) {
            NumberList result(values->size(), *fill);
            const auto amount = (std::min)(static_cast<std::size_t>(delay), values->size());
            std::copy(values->begin(), values->end() - amount, result.begin() + amount);
            return Operand::numbers(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "kl_div") {
        const auto* p = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* q = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (p && q && p->size() == q->size() && normalized_weights(*p) && normalized_weights(*q)) {
            double result = 0.0;
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < p->size(); ++i) {
                if ((*p)[i] > 0.0 && (*q)[i] == 0.0) {
                    note = "NOVELTY has infinite KL divergence because q assigns zero weight where p is positive; the finite operand domain does not encode +infinity";
                    return std::nullopt;
                }
                if ((*p)[i] > 0.0) result += (*p)[i] * std::log((*p)[i] / (*q)[i]);
            }
            note = "finite Kullback-Leibler divergence sum p log(p/q) on two normalized distributions with shared positions";
            return Operand::number(result);
        }
        note = "NOVELTY requires two same-extent normalized finite nonnegative distributions";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "reciprocal") {
        if (const auto value = number(0); value && *value != 0.0) return Operand::number(1.0 / *value);
    }
    if (code == "log_spiral") {
        const auto a = number(0), b = number(1), theta = number(2);
        if (a && b && theta) return Operand::point(logarithmic_spiral(*a, *b, *theta));
    }
    if (code == "eval_at") {
        const auto* finite_function = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* point = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[1].body);
        if (finite_function && point && !point->empty()) {
            std::map<std::string, std::string> function;
            for (const auto& [input, output] : finite_function->pairs) {
                if (input.empty() || output.empty() || !function.emplace(input, output).second) {
                    note = "PRESENTLY requires a finite function with one exact output for each supplied input";
                    return std::nullopt;
                }
            }
            const auto found = function.find(*point);
            if (found != function.end()) {
                note = "actual finite function evaluation at the supplied domain member";
                return Operand::text(found->second);
            }
            note = "evaluation point is outside the finite function's declared domain";
            return std::nullopt;
        }
    }
    if (code == "dft") {
        if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body); values && values->size() <= 4096) {
            ComplexList result(values->size());
            for (std::size_t k = 0; k < values->size(); ++k) {
                for (std::size_t n = 0; n < values->size(); ++n) {
                    result[k] += (*values)[n] * std::polar(1.0, -2.0 * pi * static_cast<double>(k * n) / static_cast<double>(values->size()));
                }
            }
            return Operand::complexes(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "group") return operands[0];
    if (code == "gossip_step") {
        const auto* weights = std::get_if<Matrix>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (weights && values && weights->valid() && weights->rows != 0 && weights->rows == weights->columns &&
            weights->columns == values->size() && weights->rows <= 256 &&
            std::all_of(values->begin(), values->end(), [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); })) {
            bool stochastic = true;
            for (std::size_t row = 0; row < weights->rows; ++row) {
                double row_sum = 0.0;
                for (std::size_t column = 0; column < weights->columns; ++column) {
                    const auto weight = weights->at(row, column);
                    stochastic = stochastic && std::isfinite(weight) && weight >= 0.0;
                    row_sum += weight;
                }
                stochastic = stochastic && std::abs(row_sum - 1.0) <= 1e-10 * (std::max)(std::size_t{1}, weights->columns);
            }
            if (!stochastic) {
                note = "PUBLICITY requires a finite nonnegative row-stochastic gossip matrix";
                return std::nullopt;
            }
            NumberList result(weights->rows, 0.0);
            for (std::size_t row = 0; row < weights->rows; ++row)
                for (std::size_t column = 0; column < weights->columns; ++column)
                    result[row] += weights->at(row, column) * (*values)[column];
            note = "one bounded gossip-consensus update Wv; each new value is the row-defined convex association of supplied values";
            return Operand::numbers(std::move(result));
        }
        note = "PUBLICITY requires a square row-stochastic matrix and a matching finite value family (extent at most 256)";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "hill_diversity") {
        const auto* weights = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto order = number(1);
        if (weights && order && !weights->empty() && std::isfinite(*order) && *order >= 0.0 &&
            std::all_of(weights->begin(), weights->end(), [](double weight) { return std::isfinite(weight) && weight >= 0.0; })) {
            const auto total = std::accumulate(weights->begin(), weights->end(), 0.0);
            if (total > 0.0) {
                if (std::abs(*order - 1.0) < 1e-12) {
                    double entropy = 0.0;
                    for (const auto weight : *weights) if (weight > 0.0) { const auto p = weight / total; entropy -= p * std::log(p); }
                    note = "Hill diversity of order one: exp of Shannon entropy after exact finite normalization";
                    return Operand::number(std::exp(entropy));
                }
                double sum = 0.0;
                for (const auto weight : *weights) if (weight > 0.0) sum += std::pow(weight / total, *order);
                if (sum > 0.0) {
                    note = "Hill diversity effective count for the supplied nonnegative weights and finite order";
                    return Operand::number(std::pow(sum, 1.0 / (1.0 - *order)));
                }
            }
        }
        note = "DIVERSITY requires a nonzero finite nonnegative weight family and a finite order q >= 0";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "offspring_pgf") {
        const auto* probabilities = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto z = number(1);
        if (probabilities && z) {
            double result = 0.0;
            for (auto cursor = probabilities->rbegin(); cursor != probabilities->rend(); ++cursor) result = result * *z + *cursor;
            return Operand::number(result);
        }
    }
    if (code == "cyclic_shift") {
        std::int64_t amount{};
        if (integral_operand(operands[1], amount)) {
            if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body)) return Operand::numbers(cyclically_shifted(*values, amount));
            if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[0].body)) return Operand::names(cyclically_shifted(*values, amount));
            if (const auto* value = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[0].body)) {
                std::vector<char> letters(value->begin(), value->end());
                const auto shifted = cyclically_shifted(letters, amount);
                return Operand::text(std::string(shifted.begin(), shifted.end()));
            }
        }
    }
    if (code == "replicator_rhs") {
        const auto* payoff = std::get_if<Matrix>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* weights = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (payoff && weights && payoff->valid() && payoff->rows == payoff->columns && payoff->rows == weights->size()) {
            NumberList fitness(weights->size(), 0.0), result(weights->size(), 0.0);
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < weights->size(); ++i)
                for (std::size_t j = 0; j < weights->size(); ++j) fitness[i] += payoff->at(i, j) * (*weights)[j];
            const auto mean = std::inner_product(weights->begin(), weights->end(), fitness.begin(), 0.0);
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < weights->size(); ++i) result[i] = (*weights)[i] * (fitness[i] - mean);
            return Operand::numbers(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "coboundary") {
        const auto* path = std::get_if<TermValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* path_values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (path && path_values && path->operation == "oriented_path_graph" &&
            path->arguments.size() == 1) {
            std::size_t declared_vertices{};
            const auto& extent_text = path->arguments.front();
            const auto parsed_extent = std::from_chars(
                extent_text.data(), extent_text.data() + extent_text.size(), declared_vertices);
            if (parsed_extent.ec == std::errc{} && parsed_extent.ptr == extent_text.data() + extent_text.size() &&
                declared_vertices == path_values->size() &&
                std::all_of(path_values->begin(), path_values->end(),
                            [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); })) {
                NumberList result(path_values->size() > 1 ? path_values->size() - 1 : 0);
                for (std::size_t i = 0; i < result.size(); ++i)
                    result[i] = (*path_values)[i + 1] - (*path_values)[i];
                note = "oriented coboundary on the exact consecutive path graph reconstructed from a published version-1 vertex-value sequence";
                return Operand::numbers(std::move(result));
            }
            note = "published version-1 TENSIONS path extent disagrees with its exact finite vertex-value sequence";
            return std::nullopt;
        }
        const auto* graph = std::get_if<GraphValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (graph && values && finite_graph_whole(*graph) &&
            values->size() == graph->vertices.size() &&
            std::all_of(values->begin(), values->end(),
                        [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); })) {
            std::unordered_map<std::string, std::size_t> index;
            index.reserve(graph->vertices.size());
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < graph->vertices.size(); ++i)
                index.emplace(graph->vertices[i], i);
            NumberList result; result.reserve(graph->edges.size());
            for (const auto& edge : graph->edges)
                result.push_back((*values)[index.at(edge.target)] -
                                 (*values)[index.at(edge.source)]);
            note = "oriented finite-graph coboundary: one exact target-minus-source difference in supplied edge order";
            return Operand::numbers(std::move(result));
        }
        note = "TENSIONS requires one finite oriented graph and one finite value for every vertex";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "givens_rotation") {
        if (const auto values = binary_numbers()) {
            const auto rotation = givens_rotation(values->first, values->second);
            return Operand::numbers(NumberList(rotation.begin(), rotation.end()));
        }
    }
    if (code == "jain_fairness") {
        if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body); values && !values->empty()) {
            const auto sum = std::accumulate(values->begin(), values->end(), 0.0);
            const auto squares = std::inner_product(values->begin(), values->end(), values->begin(), 0.0);
            if (squares > 0.0) return Operand::number(sum * sum / (static_cast<double>(values->size()) * squares));
        }
    }
    if (code == "sinkhorn_step") {
        if (const auto* input = std::get_if<Matrix>(&operands[0].body); input && input->valid() &&
            input->rows != 0 && input->columns != 0 && input->values.size() <= 65536 &&
            std::all_of(input->values.begin(), input->values.end(), [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value) && value > 0.0; })) {
            Matrix result = *input;
            for (std::size_t row = 0; row < result.rows; ++row) {
                double sum = 0.0;
                for (std::size_t column = 0; column < result.columns; ++column) sum += result.values[row * result.columns + column];
                if (sum > 0.0) for (std::size_t column = 0; column < result.columns; ++column) result.values[row * result.columns + column] /= sum;
            }
            for (std::size_t column = 0; column < result.columns; ++column) {
                double sum = 0.0;
                for (std::size_t row = 0; row < result.rows; ++row) sum += result.values[row * result.columns + column];
                if (sum > 0.0) for (std::size_t row = 0; row < result.rows; ++row) result.values[row * result.columns + column] /= sum;
            }
            note = "one Sinkhorn alternating scaling step: normalize every row, then every column, on a strictly positive finite matrix";
            return Operand::matrix(std::move(result));
        }
        note = "EQUALINS requires a nonempty strictly positive finite matrix";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "pareto_front") {
        if (const auto* candidates = std::get_if<Matrix>(&operands[0].body); candidates && candidates->valid()) {
            NumberList front;
            for (std::size_t row = 0; row < candidates->rows; ++row) {
                bool dominated = false;
                for (std::size_t other = 0; other < candidates->rows && !dominated; ++other) if (other != row) {
                    bool never_worse = true, strictly_better = false;
                    for (std::size_t column = 0; column < candidates->columns; ++column) {
                        never_worse = never_worse && candidates->at(other, column) <= candidates->at(row, column);
                        strictly_better = strictly_better || candidates->at(other, column) < candidates->at(row, column);
                    }
                    dominated = never_worse && strictly_better;
                }
                if (!dominated) front.push_back(static_cast<double>(row));
            }
            return Operand::numbers(std::move(front));
        }
    }
    if (code == "convex_hull") {
        if (const auto* points = std::get_if<Point2List>(&operands[0].body)) return Operand::points(finite_convex_hull(*points));
    }
    if (code == "isotonic_fit") {
        const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* order = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (values && order && !values->empty() && values->size() == order->size() &&
            std::all_of(values->begin(), values->end(), [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); })) {
            std::unordered_set<std::string> positions;
            if (!std::all_of(order->begin(), order->end(), [&](const std::string& position) {
                    return !position.empty() && positions.insert(position).second;
                })) {
                note = "RESPECT requires a unique named finite chain order";
                return std::nullopt;
            }
            struct Block { double sum; std::size_t count; };
            std::vector<Block> blocks;
            for (const auto value : *values) {
                blocks.push_back({value, 1});
                while (blocks.size() >= 2) {
                    const auto last = blocks.back().sum / static_cast<double>(blocks.back().count);
                    const auto prior = blocks[blocks.size() - 2].sum / static_cast<double>(blocks[blocks.size() - 2].count);
                    if (prior <= last) break;
                    const auto merged = Block{blocks[blocks.size() - 2].sum + blocks.back().sum,
                                              blocks[blocks.size() - 2].count + blocks.back().count};
                    blocks.pop_back(); blocks.back() = merged;
                }
            }
            NumberList result; result.reserve(values->size());
            for (const auto& block : blocks) result.insert(result.end(), block.count, block.sum / static_cast<double>(block.count));
            note = "pool-adjacent-violators isotonic least-squares fit in the exact supplied named chain order";
            return Operand::numbers(std::move(result));
        }
        note = "RESPECT requires one finite value for every unique member of its supplied chain order";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "conjugate") {
        const auto* group_element = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* value = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[1].body);
        if (group_element && value && std::all_of(group_element->begin(), group_element->end(), [](unsigned char letter) { return std::isalpha(letter) != 0; }) &&
            std::all_of(value->begin(), value->end(), [](unsigned char letter) { return std::isalpha(letter) != 0; })) {
            std::string inverse;
            inverse.reserve(group_element->size());
            for (auto cursor = group_element->rbegin(); cursor != group_element->rend(); ++cursor)
                inverse.push_back(std::islower(static_cast<unsigned char>(*cursor)) ? static_cast<char>(std::toupper(static_cast<unsigned char>(*cursor)))
                                                                                  : static_cast<char>(std::tolower(static_cast<unsigned char>(*cursor))));
            std::string word = *group_element + *value + inverse;
            std::string reduced;
            for (const char letter : word) {
                if (!reduced.empty() && std::tolower(static_cast<unsigned char>(reduced.back())) == std::tolower(static_cast<unsigned char>(letter)) &&
                    std::isupper(static_cast<unsigned char>(reduced.back())) != std::isupper(static_cast<unsigned char>(letter))) reduced.pop_back();
                else reduced.push_back(letter);
            }
            return Operand::text(std::move(reduced));
        }
    }
    if (code == "local_maxima") {
        const auto* path = std::get_if<TermValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* path_field = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (path && path_field && path->operation == "undirected_path_graph" &&
            path->arguments.size() == 1) {
            std::size_t declared_vertices{};
            const auto& extent_text = path->arguments.front();
            const auto parsed_extent = std::from_chars(
                extent_text.data(), extent_text.data() + extent_text.size(), declared_vertices);
            if (parsed_extent.ec == std::errc{} && parsed_extent.ptr == extent_text.data() + extent_text.size() &&
                declared_vertices == path_field->size() &&
                std::all_of(path_field->begin(), path_field->end(),
                            [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); })) {
                NameList maxima;
                for (std::size_t i = 0; i < path_field->size(); ++i) {
                    const bool no_lower_than_left = i == 0 || (*path_field)[i] >= (*path_field)[i - 1];
                    const bool no_lower_than_right = i + 1 == path_field->size() || (*path_field)[i] >= (*path_field)[i + 1];
                    if (no_lower_than_left && no_lower_than_right)
                        maxima.push_back("v" + std::to_string(i));
                }
                note = "finite path-graph local maxima reconstructed from a published version-1 sample sequence, with current >= plateau handling";
                return Operand::names(std::move(maxima));
            }
            note = "published version-1 CREST path extent disagrees with its exact finite scalar field";
            return std::nullopt;
        }
        const auto* graph = std::get_if<GraphValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* field = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (graph && field && finite_graph_whole(*graph) && field->size() == graph->vertices.size() &&
            std::all_of(field->begin(), field->end(), [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); })) {
            std::unordered_map<std::string, std::size_t> index;
            index.reserve(graph->vertices.size());
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < graph->vertices.size(); ++i) index.emplace(graph->vertices[i], i);
            std::vector<std::vector<std::size_t>> neighbors(graph->vertices.size());
            for (const auto& edge : graph->edges) if (edge.source != edge.target) {
                const auto source = index.at(edge.source), target = index.at(edge.target);
                neighbors[source].push_back(target); neighbors[target].push_back(source);
            }
            NameList maxima;
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < graph->vertices.size(); ++i) {
                const bool no_lower_than_neighbors = std::all_of(neighbors[i].begin(), neighbors[i].end(),
                    [&](std::size_t neighbor) { return (*field)[i] >= (*field)[neighbor]; });
                if (no_lower_than_neighbors) maxima.push_back(graph->vertices[i]);
            }
            note = "finite graph local maxima use >= on every adjacency; each vertex of a top plateau is returned exactly when none of its adjacent vertices has a greater field value";
            return Operand::names(std::move(maxima));
        }
    }
    if (code == "rule_of_succession") {
        std::int64_t successes{}, trials{};
        if (integral_operand(operands[0], successes) && integral_operand(operands[1], trials) &&
            successes >= 0 && trials >= successes && trials <= 9'007'199'254'740'989ll) {
            note = "Laplace rule of succession on exact finite event counts: (successes+1)/(trials+2)";
            return Operand::number((static_cast<double>(successes) + 1.0) /
                                   (static_cast<double>(trials) + 2.0));
        }
        note = "WISE requires exact nonnegative integer counts with successes <= trials";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "vector_norm") {
        if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body)) return Operand::number(std::sqrt(std::inner_product(values->begin(), values->end(), values->begin(), 0.0)));
        if (const auto* value = std::get_if<Vec2>(&operands[0].body)) return Operand::number(length(*value));
        if (const auto* value = std::get_if<Vec3>(&operands[0].body)) return Operand::number(length(*value));
    }
    if (code == "highest_bid") {
        if (const auto* bids = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body); bids && !bids->empty()) return Operand::number(*(std::max_element)(bids->begin(), bids->end()));
    }
    if (code == "generating_poly") {
        const auto* coefficients = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto z = number(1);
        if (coefficients && z) {
            double result = 0.0;
            for (auto cursor = coefficients->rbegin(); cursor != coefficients->rend(); ++cursor) result = result * *z + *cursor;
            return Operand::number(result);
        }
    }
    if (code == "kleene_not") {
        bool value{};
        if (truth_operand(operands[0], value)) return Operand::truth(!value);
        if (std::holds_alternative<std::monostate>(operands[0].body)) return Operand{};
    }
    if (code == "cardinality") {
        if (const auto count = finite_carrier_cardinality(operands[0]);
            count && *count <= static_cast<std::size_t>((std::numeric_limits<std::int64_t>::max)())) {
            note = "finite cardinality of the exact carrier; repeated representations of one member count once";
            return Operand::integer(static_cast<std::int64_t>(*count));
        }
        note = "SIZE requires a well-formed finite carrier whose cardinality is representable";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "spin") {
        const auto* classes = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* subclasses = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[1].body);
        std::int64_t turn{};
        if (classes && subclasses && integral_operand(operands[2], turn)) {
            auto rotated_classes = cyclically_shifted(*classes, turn);
            auto rotated_subclasses = cyclically_shifted(*subclasses, -turn);
            NameList result; result.reserve(rotated_classes.size() + rotated_subclasses.size());
            result.insert(result.end(), rotated_classes.begin(), rotated_classes.end());
            result.insert(result.end(), rotated_subclasses.begin(), rotated_subclasses.end());
            note = "exact finite Spin: classes turn forward, subclasses counter-turn";
            return Operand::names(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "median3") {
        const auto a = number(0), b = number(1), c = number(2);
        if (a && b && c) return Operand::number(*a + *b + *c - (std::min)({*a, *b, *c}) - (std::max)({*a, *b, *c}));
    }
    if (code == "decibel") {
        const auto values = binary_numbers();
        if (values && values->first > 0.0 && values->second > 0.0) return Operand::number(10.0 * std::log10(values->first / values->second));
    }
    if (code == "dtw_path") {
        const auto* a = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* b = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (a && b && !a->empty() && !b->empty() && a->size() * b->size() <= 1'000'000) {
            const auto width = b->size() + 1;
            NumberList cost((a->size() + 1) * width, (std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity)());
            cost[0] = 0.0;
            for (std::size_t i = 1; i <= a->size(); ++i) for (std::size_t j = 1; j <= b->size(); ++j) {
                cost[i * width + j] = std::abs((*a)[i - 1] - (*b)[j - 1]) +
                    (std::min)({cost[(i - 1) * width + j], cost[i * width + j - 1], cost[(i - 1) * width + j - 1]});
            }
            Point2List path;
            for (std::size_t i = a->size(), j = b->size(); i && j;) {
                path.push_back({static_cast<double>(i - 1), static_cast<double>(j - 1)});
                const auto diagonal = cost[(i - 1) * width + j - 1];
                const auto vertical = cost[(i - 1) * width + j];
                const auto horizontal = cost[i * width + j - 1];
                if (diagonal <= vertical && diagonal <= horizontal) { --i; --j; }
                else if (vertical <= horizontal) --i;
                else --j;
            }
            std::reverse(path.begin(), path.end());
            return Operand::points(std::move(path));
        }
    }
    if (code == "doubling_map") {
        if (const auto value = number(0)) return Operand::number(std::fmod(2.0 * *value, 1.0) + (std::fmod(2.0 * *value, 1.0) < 0.0 ? 1.0 : 0.0));
    }
    if (code == "alpha_rename") {
        const auto* term = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* old_name = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[1].body);
        const auto* fresh_name = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[2].body);
        const auto valid_identifier = [](const std::string& name) {
            return !name.empty() && (std::isalpha(static_cast<unsigned char>(name.front())) || name.front() == '_') &&
                   std::all_of(name.begin() + 1, name.end(), [](unsigned char c) { return std::isalnum(c) || c == '_'; });
        };
        if (term && term->size() <= 65536 && old_name && fresh_name && old_name != fresh_name &&
            valid_identifier(*old_name) && valid_identifier(*fresh_name)) {
            auto syntax = FiniteLambdaParser(*term).parse();
            if (syntax && syntax->kind == LambdaTerm::Kind::abstraction && syntax->name == *old_name &&
                !lambda_term_contains_name(syntax->children.front(), *fresh_name)) {
                syntax->name = *fresh_name;
                alpha_rename_outer_occurrences(syntax->children.front(), *old_name, *fresh_name);
                note = "capture-avoiding alpha-conversion of the supplied outer lambda binder; nested shadowing remains intact";
                return Operand::text(canonical_lambda_term(*syntax));
            }
        }
        note = "NAMA requires a parsed finite lambda term whose outer binder matches old_name and whose genuinely fresh name occurs nowhere in that body";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "face_map") {
        const auto* simplex = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[0].body);
        std::int64_t index{};
        if (simplex && integral_operand(operands[1], index) && index >= 0 && static_cast<std::size_t>(index) < simplex->size()) {
            auto face = *simplex; face.erase(face.begin() + index); return Operand::names(std::move(face));
        }
    }
    if (code == "reverse") {
        if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body)) { auto result = *values; std::reverse(result.begin(), result.end()); return Operand::numbers(std::move(result)); }
        if (const auto* values = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[0].body)) { auto result = *values; std::reverse(result.begin(), result.end()); return Operand::names(std::move(result)); }
        if (const auto* value = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[0].body)) { auto result = *value; std::reverse(result.begin(), result.end()); return Operand::text(std::move(result)); }
    }
    if (code == "expected_loss") {
        const auto* losses = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* probabilities = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (losses && probabilities && losses->size() == probabilities->size() && normalized_weights(*probabilities) &&
            std::all_of(losses->begin(), losses->end(), [](double loss) { return std::isfinite(loss) && loss >= 0.0; })) {
            note = "actuarial expected loss: finite loss-probability inner product on one normalized outcome family";
            return Operand::number(std::inner_product(losses->begin(), losses->end(), probabilities->begin(), 0.0));
        }
        note = "DAMAGE requires matching finite nonnegative losses and a normalized nonnegative probability family";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "filtration_at") {
        const auto* names = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        const auto threshold = number(2);
        if (names && values && threshold && names->size() == values->size()) {
            NameList result;
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < names->size(); ++i) if ((*values)[i] <= *threshold) result.push_back((*names)[i]);
            return Operand::names(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "borda_count") {
        if (const auto* rankings = std::get_if<Matrix>(&operands[0].body); rankings && rankings->valid() &&
            rankings->rows != 0 && rankings->columns != 0 && rankings->values.size() <= 65536) {
            bool strict_rankings = true;
            for (std::size_t row = 0; row < rankings->rows; ++row) {
                std::vector<bool> seen(rankings->columns, false);
                for (std::size_t candidate = 0; candidate < rankings->columns; ++candidate) {
                    const auto rank = rankings->at(row, candidate);
                    if (!std::isfinite(rank) || std::floor(rank) != rank || rank < 1.0 ||
                        rank > static_cast<double>(rankings->columns) || seen[static_cast<std::size_t>(rank) - 1]) {
                        strict_rankings = false;
                        break;
                    }
                    seen[static_cast<std::size_t>(rank) - 1] = true;
                }
                if (!strict_rankings) break;
            }
            if (!strict_rankings) {
                note = "COURTAGE requires every voter row to be a strict permutation of ranks 1 through the candidate extent";
                return std::nullopt;
            }
            NumberList scores(rankings->columns, 0.0);
            for (std::size_t row = 0; row < rankings->rows; ++row)
                for (std::size_t column = 0; column < rankings->columns; ++column)
                    scores[column] += static_cast<double>(rankings->columns) - rankings->at(row, column);
            note = "Borda aggregation: each strict rank r contributes candidate_extent-r points";
            return Operand::numbers(std::move(scores));
        }
        note = "COURTAGE requires a nonempty finite voter-by-candidate ranking matrix";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "eventually") {
        const auto* trace = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto threshold = number(1);
        if (trace && threshold) return Operand::truth(std::any_of(trace->begin(), trace->end(), [&](double value) { return value >= *threshold; }));
    }
    if (code == "poisson_birth") {
        const auto rate = number(0), time = number(1);
        std::int64_t count{};
        if (rate && time && *rate >= 0.0 && *time >= 0.0 && integral_operand(operands[2], count) && count >= 0) {
            const auto mean = *rate * *time;
            return Operand::number(std::exp(-mean + static_cast<double>(count) * std::log(mean == 0.0 ? 1.0 : mean) - std::lgamma(static_cast<double>(count) + 1.0)) * (mean == 0.0 && count > 0 ? 0.0 : 1.0));
        }
    }
    if (code == "outage_probability") {
        if (const auto reliability = number(0); reliability && *reliability >= 0.0 && *reliability <= 1.0) return Operand::number(1.0 - *reliability);
        if (const auto* reliabilities = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body)) {
            double available = 1.0;
            for (const auto value : *reliabilities) { if (value < 0.0 || value > 1.0) return std::nullopt; available *= value; }
            return Operand::number(1.0 - available);
        }
    }
    if (code == "fold_all") {
        const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* combine = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[1].body);
        const auto unit = number(2);
        if (values && combine && unit && std::isfinite(*unit) &&
            std::all_of(values->begin(), values->end(), [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); }) &&
            ((*combine == "add" && *unit == 0.0) || (*combine == "mul" && *unit == 1.0))) {
            double result = *unit;
            for (const auto value : *values) {
                if (*combine == "add") result += value;
                else result *= value;
                if (!std::isfinite(result)) {
                    note = "ALLAGE finite monoid fold overflowed the representable scalar domain";
                    return std::nullopt;
                }
            }
            note = *combine == "add"
                ? "finite fold in the additive real monoid with its actual neutral element 0"
                : "finite fold in the multiplicative real monoid with its actual neutral element 1";
            return Operand::number(result);
        }
        note = "ALLAGE requires finite scalars and an actual supported monoid neutral element: add/0 or mul/1";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "surreal_cut") {
        const auto* left = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* right = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (left && right) {
            const auto lower = left->empty() ? -(std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity)() : *(std::max_element)(left->begin(), left->end());
            const auto upper = right->empty() ? (std::numeric_limits<double>::infinity)() : *(std::min_element)(right->begin(), right->end());
            const bool finite_sides = std::all_of(left->begin(), left->end(), [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); }) &&
                                      std::all_of(right->begin(), right->end(), [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); });
            const bool valid_cut = finite_sides && std::all_of(left->begin(), left->end(), [&](double l) {
                return std::all_of(right->begin(), right->end(), [&](double r) { return l < r; });
            });
            if (valid_cut && lower < upper) {
                if (!std::isfinite(lower) && !std::isfinite(upper)) return Operand::number(0.0);
                if (!std::isfinite(lower)) return Operand::number(std::ceil(upper) - 1.0);
                if (!std::isfinite(upper)) return Operand::number(std::floor(lower) + 1.0);
                for (unsigned exponent = 0; exponent <= 52; ++exponent) {
                    const auto denominator = std::uint64_t{1} << exponent;
                    const auto scaled_lower = static_cast<long double>(lower) * static_cast<long double>(denominator);
                    const auto scaled_upper = static_cast<long double>(upper) * static_cast<long double>(denominator);
                    if (scaled_lower < static_cast<long double>((std::numeric_limits<std::int64_t>::min)()) ||
                        scaled_upper > static_cast<long double>((std::numeric_limits<std::int64_t>::max)())) break;
                    const auto first = static_cast<std::int64_t>(std::floor(scaled_lower)) + 1;
                    const auto last = static_cast<std::int64_t>(std::ceil(scaled_upper)) - 1;
                    if (first > last) continue;
                    const auto nearest_zero = first > 0 ? first : last < 0 ? last : std::int64_t{0};
                    static constexpr std::array<int, 5> offsets{0, -1, 1, -2, 2};
                    for (const int offset : offsets) {
                        const auto numerator = nearest_zero + offset;
                        if (numerator < first || numerator > last || (exponent > 0 && (numerator & 1) == 0)) continue;
                        return Operand::number(static_cast<double>(numerator) / static_cast<double>(denominator));
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    if (code == "operad_substitute") {
        const auto* tree = std::get_if<OperadTreeValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* substitutions = std::get_if<OperadSubstitutions>(&operands[1].body);
        if (tree && substitutions && tree->valid()) {
            bool valid = true;
            std::size_t projected = tree->labels.size();
            for (const auto& graft : substitutions->grafts) {
                valid = valid && !graft.slot.empty() && graft.tree.valid();
                if (graft.tree.valid()) projected += graft.tree.labels.size() - 1;
            }
            if (!valid || projected > 100000) return std::nullopt;
            OperadTreeValue result;
            std::vector<std::size_t> original_to_output(tree->labels.size());
            for (std::size_t node = 0; node < tree->labels.size(); ++node) {
                const auto graft = std::find_if(substitutions->grafts.begin(), substitutions->grafts.end(), [&](const OperadGraft& value) { return value.slot == tree->labels[node]; });
                const bool has_children = std::find(tree->parents.begin(), tree->parents.end(), static_cast<std::int64_t>(node)) != tree->parents.end();
                const auto output_parent = tree->parents[node] < 0 ? std::int64_t{-1} : static_cast<std::int64_t>(original_to_output[static_cast<std::size_t>(tree->parents[node])]);
                if (graft == substitutions->grafts.end()) {
                    original_to_output[node] = result.labels.size();
                    result.labels.push_back(tree->labels[node]);
                    result.parents.push_back(output_parent);
                } else {
                    if (has_children) { note = "operadic graft slots must be leaves in the bounded tree domain"; return std::nullopt; }
                    const auto base = result.labels.size();
                    original_to_output[node] = base;
                    for (std::size_t local = 0; local < graft->tree.labels.size(); ++local) {
                        result.labels.push_back(graft->tree.labels[local]);
                        result.parents.push_back(local == 0 ? output_parent : static_cast<std::int64_t>(base + static_cast<std::size_t>(graft->tree.parents[local])));
                    }
                }
            }
            if (result.valid()) return Operand::operad_tree(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "growth" || code == "iterate") {
        const auto* operation = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[0].body);
        std::int64_t count{};
        if (operation && integral_operand(operands[1], count) && count >= 0 && count <= 1024) {
            const auto* repeated = find_light_by_code(*operation);
            if (repeated && repeated->minimum_operands <= 1 && repeated->maximum_operands >= 1 && *operation != code) {
                Operand current = operands[2];
                for (std::int64_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
                    auto step = invoke(*operation, {current});
                    if (!step.exact()) { note = "bounded repetition reached a symbolic remainder"; return std::nullopt; }
                    current = *step.value;
                }
                note = "exact bounded Light repetition";
                return current;
            }
        }
    }
    if (code == "prim_rec") {
        const auto* step_code = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[1].body);
        std::int64_t count{};
        if (step_code && integral_operand(operands[2], count) && count >= 0 && count <= 1024) {
            const auto* step_definition = find_light_by_code(*step_code);
            if (step_definition && *step_code != code) {
                Operand current = operands[0];
                for (std::int64_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
                    std::vector<Operand> call;
                    if (step_definition->minimum_operands <= 2 && step_definition->maximum_operands >= 2) call = {Operand::integer(i), current};
                    else if (step_definition->minimum_operands <= 1 && step_definition->maximum_operands >= 1) call = {current};
                    else return std::nullopt;
                    auto step = invoke(*step_code, std::move(call));
                    if (!step.exact()) { note = "primitive recursion reached a symbolic remainder"; return std::nullopt; }
                    current = *step.value;
                }
                note = "exact bounded primitive recursion";
                return current;
            }
        }
    }

    if (code == "both") {
        if (const auto* evidence = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[0].body)) {
            const bool true_evidence = std::find(evidence->begin(), evidence->end(), "true") != evidence->end();
            const bool false_evidence = std::find(evidence->begin(), evidence->end(), "false") != evidence->end();
            return Operand::truth(true_evidence && false_evidence);
        }
        if (std::holds_alternative<bool>(operands[0].body) || std::holds_alternative<std::monostate>(operands[0].body)) return Operand::truth(false);
    }
    if (code == "box_all") {
        const auto* relation = std::get_if<GraphValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* predicate = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[1].body);
        const auto* world = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[2].body);
        if (relation && predicate && world) {
            for (const auto& edge : relation->edges)
                if (edge.source == *world && std::find(predicate->begin(), predicate->end(), edge.target) == predicate->end()) return Operand::truth(false);
            return Operand::truth(true);
        }
    }
    if (code == "compose") {
        const auto* g = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* f = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&operands[1].body);
        if (g && f) {
            RelationValue result;
            for (const auto& first : f->pairs) for (const auto& second : g->pairs)
                if (first.second == second.first) result.pairs.emplace_back(first.first, second.second);
            std::sort(result.pairs.begin(), result.pairs.end());
            result.pairs.erase(std::unique(result.pairs.begin(), result.pairs.end()), result.pairs.end());
            return Operand::relation(std::move(result));
        }
    }
    if (code == "term") {
        const auto* operation = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* arguments = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (operation && arguments && !operation->empty()) return Operand::term(TermValue{*operation, *arguments});
    }
    if (code == "action_prefix") {
        const auto* action = std::get_if<std::string>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* process = std::get_if<NameList>(&operands[1].body);
        if (action && process && !action->empty() && !process->empty() && process->size() <= 65535 &&
            std::all_of(process->begin(), process->end(), [](const std::string& body) { return !body.empty(); })) {
            NameList ordered_arguments; ordered_arguments.reserve(process->size() + 1);
            ordered_arguments.push_back(*action);
            ordered_arguments.insert(ordered_arguments.end(), process->begin(), process->end());
            note = "mCRL2-style action-prefix constructor: one action is retained separately at the head of the ordered process body";
            return Operand::term(TermValue{"action_prefix", std::move(ordered_arguments)});
        }
        note = "COMMANDSEA requires one named action and one nonempty finite ordered process body";
        return std::nullopt;
    }
    if (code == "erode") {
        const auto* shape = std::get_if<Point2List>(&operands[0].body);
        const auto* element = std::get_if<Point2List>(&operands[1].body);
        if (shape && element && !element->empty() && shape->size() * element->size() <= 1'000'000) {
            const auto equal = [](Vec2 a, Vec2 b) { return std::abs(a.x - b.x) <= 1e-9 && std::abs(a.y - b.y) <= 1e-9; };
            Point2List candidates;
            for (const auto a : *shape) for (const auto b : *element) candidates.push_back(a - b);
            Point2List result;
            for (const auto candidate : candidates) {
                const bool contained = std::all_of(element->begin(), element->end(), [&](Vec2 b) {
                    const auto wanted = candidate + b;
