    if (code == "erode") return make({{"shape", Operand::points(Point2List{{0, 0}, {1, 0}, {2, 0}})}, {"structuring element", Operand::points(Point2List{{0, 0}, {1, 0}})}});
    if (code == "shapley") return make({{"player", Operand::integer(0)}, {"coalition values", Operand::numbers({0, 1, 2, 4})}});
    if (code == "discrete_partition") return make({{"selves", Operand::names({"a", "b", "c"})}});
    if (code == "bayes") return make({{"prior", Operand::probability({{"a", "b"}, {0.6, 0.4}})}, {"likelihood", Operand::probability({{"a", "b"}, {0.8, 0.2}})}});
    if (code == "reduce_free") return make({{"word", Operand::text("abBAc")}});
    if (code == "nearest_decode") return make({{"code", Operand::names({"000", "111"})}, {"received", Operand::text("110")}});
    if (code == "snell") return make({{"gain", Operand::matrix({2, 2, {1, 2, 3, 1}})}, {"kernel", Operand::matrix({2, 2, {0.8, 0.2, 0.1, 0.9}})}});
    if (code == "huber") return make({{"error", Operand::number(2.0)}, {"delta", Operand::number(1.0)}});
    if (code == "covers") return make({{"finite order", Operand::relation({{{"a", "a"}, {"b", "b"}, {"c", "c"}, {"a", "b"}, {"b", "c"}, {"a", "c"}}})}});
    if (code == "concept_close") return make({{"context", Operand::relation({{{"o1", "warm"}, {"o1", "bright"}, {"o2", "warm"}}})}, {"objects", Operand::names({"o1"})}});
    if (code == "mix") return make({{"values", Operand::names({"a", "b", "c"})}, {"chosen order", Operand::numbers({2, 0, 1})}});
    if (code == "cyclic_shift") return make({{"values", Operand::names({"a", "b", "c"})}, {"turn", Operand::integer(1)}});
    if (code == "lyap_residual") return make({{"A", Operand::matrix({2, 2, {0.5, 0, 0, 0.25}})}, {"P", Operand::matrix({2, 2, {1, 0, 0, 1}})}});
    if (code == "l_system_step") return make({{"word", Operand::text("AB")}, {"rules", Operand::relation({{{"A", "AB"}, {"B", "A"}}})}});
    if (code == "exact_cover") return make({{"incidence", Operand::matrix({3, 3, {1, 0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 0, 1, 0}})}});
    if (code == "delay_k") return make({{"sequence", Operand::numbers({1, 2, 3})}, {"delay", Operand::integer(1)}, {"fill", Operand::number(0)}});
    if (code == "kl_div") return make({{"p", Operand::numbers({0.5, 0.5})}, {"q", Operand::numbers({0.25, 0.75})}});
    if (code == "log_spiral") return make({{"scale", Operand::number(1)}, {"growth", Operand::number(0.1)}, {"angle", Operand::number(pi)}});
    if (code == "bellman_opt") return make({{"values", Operand::numbers({2, 3})}, {"model", Operand::matrix({2, 3, {1, 0.5, 0.5, 0, 0.25, 0.75}})}});
    if (code == "eval_at") return make({
        {"finite function", Operand::relation({{{"now", "4"}, {"later", "8"}}})},
        {"domain member", Operand::text("now")}
    });
    if (code == "dft") return make({{"signal", Operand::numbers({1, 0, -1, 0})}});
    if (code == "group") return make({{"expression", Operand::expression(0)}});
    if (code == "voronoi") return make({{"sites", Operand::points(Point2List{{-1, 0}, {1, 0}, {0, 2}})}});
    if (code == "gossip_step") return make({{"weights", Operand::matrix({2, 2, {0.5, 0.5, 0.5, 0.5}})}, {"values", Operand::numbers({0, 2})}});
    if (code == "hill_diversity") return make({{"weights", Operand::numbers({1, 1, 2})}, {"order", Operand::number(1)}});
    if (code == "maxplus_mv") return make({{"matrix", Operand::matrix({2, 2, {0, 1, 2, 0}})}, {"vector", Operand::numbers({3, 4})}});
    if (code == "safe_gfp") return make({{"graph", Operand::graph({{"a", "b", "c"}, {{"a", "b", 1}, {"b", "b", 1}, {"c", "a", 1}}})}, {"safe region", Operand::names({"a", "b"})}});
    if (code == "offspring_pgf") return make({{"probabilities", Operand::numbers({0.2, 0.5, 0.3})}, {"z", Operand::number(0.75)}});
    if (code == "hutchinson") return make({{"shape", Operand::points(Point2List{{0, 0}, {1, 0}, {0, 1}})}, {"affine maps", Operand::matrix({2, 6, {0.5, 0, 0, 0.5, 0, 0, 0.5, 0, 0, 0.5, 1, 0}})}});
    if (code == "right_adjoint") return make({
        {"source poset", Operand::relation({{{"a0", "a0"}, {"a1", "a1"}, {"a2", "a2"}, {"a3", "a3"},
                                               {"a0", "a1"}, {"a0", "a2"}, {"a0", "a3"},
                                               {"a1", "a2"}, {"a1", "a3"}, {"a2", "a3"}}})},
        {"target poset", Operand::relation({{{"b0", "b0"}, {"b1", "b1"}, {"b2", "b2"}, {"b3", "b3"},
                                               {"b0", "b1"}, {"b0", "b2"}, {"b0", "b3"},
                                               {"b1", "b2"}, {"b1", "b3"}, {"b2", "b3"}}})},
        {"monotone map", Operand::relation({{{"a0", "b0"}, {"a1", "b1"}, {"a2", "b1"}, {"a3", "b3"}}})},
        {"target", Operand::text("b1")}
    });
    if (code == "ols") return make({{"design", Operand::matrix({3, 2, {1, 0, 1, 1, 1, 2}})}, {"response", Operand::numbers({1, 3, 5})}});
    if (code == "operad_substitute") return make({
        {"tree", Operand::operad_tree(OperadTreeValue{{"root", "slot"}, {-1, 0}})},
        {"grafts", Operand::operad_substitutions(OperadSubstitutions{{OperadGraft{"slot", OperadTreeValue{{"branch", "leaf"}, {-1, 0}}}}})}
    });
    if (code == "prim_rec") return make({{"base", Operand::number(0.125)}, {"step", Operand::text("doubling_map")}, {"count", Operand::integer(2)}});
    if (code == "prox") return make({{"objective", Operand::text("l1")}, {"lambda", Operand::number(0.5)}, {"value", Operand::number(2)}});
    if (code == "replicator_rhs") return make({{"payoff", Operand::matrix({2, 2, {1, 0, 0, 2}})}, {"weights", Operand::numbers({0.5, 0.5})}});
    if (code == "coboundary") return make({
        {"oriented graph", Operand::graph({{"a", "b", "c"}, {{"a", "b", 1.0}, {"b", "c", 1.0}}})},
        {"vertex values", Operand::numbers({1, 4, 9})}
    });
    if (code == "union_sets") return make({{"partition", Operand::relation({{{"a", "a"}, {"b", "b"}}})}, {"a", Operand::text("a")}, {"b", Operand::text("b")}});
    if (code == "cut_rule") return make({{"left proof", Operand::relation({{{"Gamma", "P"}}})}, {"right proof", Operand::relation({{{"P", "Delta"}}})}, {"formula", Operand::text("P")}});
    if (code == "givens_rotation") return make({{"a", Operand::number(3)}, {"b", Operand::number(4)}});
    if (code == "jain_fairness") return make({{"allocations", Operand::numbers({1, 2, 3})}});
    if (code == "sinkhorn_step") return make({{"positive matrix", Operand::matrix({2, 2, {1, 2, 3, 4}})}});
    if (code == "pareto_front") return make({{"candidates", Operand::matrix({3, 2, {1, 3, 2, 2, 3, 1}})}});
    if (code == "involute") return make({{"value", Operand::complexes({{1, 2}, {3, -1}})}});
    if (code == "astar_path") return make({{"graph", Operand::graph({{"a", "b", "c"}, {{"a", "b", 1}, {"b", "c", 1}, {"a", "c", 3}}})}, {"start", Operand::text("a")}, {"goal", Operand::text("c")}, {"heuristic", Operand::numbers({2, 1, 0})}});
    if (code == "kernel") return make({{"matrix", Operand::matrix({1, 2, {1, 1}})}});
    if (code == "np_test") return make({{"sample", Operand::numbers({0, 1, 1})}, {"likelihood 0", Operand::numbers({0.7, 0.3})}, {"likelihood 1", Operand::numbers({0.2, 0.8})}, {"threshold", Operand::number(1)}});
    if (code == "conjugate") return make({{"group element", Operand::text("a")}, {"value", Operand::text("b")}});
    if (code == "convex_hull") return make({{"points", Operand::points(Point2List{{0, 0}, {1, 0}, {0, 1}, {0.2, 0.2}})}});
    if (code == "isotonic_fit") return make({{"values", Operand::numbers({3, 1, 2})}, {"order", Operand::names({"a", "b", "c"})}});
    if (code == "dempster_combine") return make({
        {"declared discernment frame", Operand::names({"a", "b"})},
        {"evidence one", Operand::probability({{"a", "a|b"}, {0.7, 0.3}})},
        {"evidence two", Operand::probability({{"a", "b"}, {0.6, 0.4}})}
    });
    if (code == "local_maxima") return make({
        {"graph", Operand::graph({{"a", "b", "c", "d", "e"}, {{"a", "b", 1}, {"b", "c", 1}, {"c", "d", 1}, {"d", "e", 1}}})},
        {"scalar field", Operand::numbers({1, 3, 2, 4, 1})}
    });
    if (code == "rule_of_succession") return make({{"successes", Operand::integer(3)}, {"trials", Operand::integer(5)}});
    if (code == "vector_norm") return make({{"vector", Operand::numbers({3, 4})}});
    if (code == "preimage") return make({{"function", Operand::relation({{{"a", "x"}, {"b", "y"}, {"c", "x"}}})}, {"target", Operand::names({"x"})}});
    if (code == "spectral_bisect") return make({{"graph", Operand::graph({{"a", "b", "c", "d"}, {{"a", "b", 1}, {"b", "c", 0.1}, {"c", "d", 1}}})}});
    if (code == "highest_bid") return make({{"bids", Operand::numbers({2, 9, 5})}});
    if (code == "some_satisfy") return make({{"values", Operand::numbers({-1, 0, 2})}, {"predicate", Operand::text("positive")}});
    if (code == "generating_poly") return make({{"coefficients", Operand::numbers({1, 2, 1})}, {"z", Operand::number(2)}});
    if (code == "up_closure") return make({{"order", Operand::relation({{{"a", "b"}, {"b", "c"}}})}, {"seed", Operand::names({"a"})}});
    if (code == "cardinality") return make({{"finite carrier", Operand::names({"a", "b", "a", "c"})}});
    if (code == "spin") return make({{"classes", Operand::names({"REALITY", "INTIMACY", "FUSING"})}, {"subclasses", Operand::names({"INFINITY", "CARE", "SPIRALLY"})}, {"turn", Operand::integer(1)}});
    if (code == "median3") return make({{"a", Operand::number(7)}, {"b", Operand::number(2)}, {"c", Operand::number(4)}});
    if (code == "mahalanobis") return make({{"x", Operand::numbers({2, 1})}, {"mean", Operand::numbers({0, 0})}, {"covariance", Operand::matrix({2, 2, {2, 0, 0, 1}})}});
    if (code == "free_module") return make({{"ring", Operand::text("Z")}, {"basis", Operand::names({"e1", "e2"})}});
    if (code == "decibel") return make({{"power", Operand::number(10)}, {"reference", Operand::number(1)}});
    if (code == "dtw_path") return make({{"left signal", Operand::numbers({1, 2, 3})}, {"right signal", Operand::numbers({1, 1.5, 3})}});
    if (code == "doubling_map") return make({{"position", Operand::number(0.375)}});
    if (code == "inclusion_exclusion") return make({{"set incidence", Operand::matrix({2, 3, {1, 1, 0, 0, 1, 1}})}});
    if (code == "alpha_rename") return make({{"term", Operand::text("lambda x. x")}, {"old name", Operand::text("x")}, {"fresh name", Operand::text("y")}});
    if (code == "holonomy_product") return make({
        {"closed edge loop", Operand::names({"a", "b", "a"})},
        {"ordered transports", Operand::matrix({2, 4, {0, -1, 1, 0, 0, -1, 1, 0}})}
    });
    if (code == "face_map") return make({{"simplex", Operand::names({"a", "b", "c"})}, {"face", Operand::integer(1)}});
    if (code == "reverse") return make({{"authored order", Operand::names({"a", "b", "c"})}});
    if (code == "stable_match") return make({{"preferences A", Operand::matrix({2, 2, {0, 1, 1, 0}})}, {"preferences B", Operand::matrix({2, 2, {0, 1, 1, 0}})}});
    if (code == "expected_loss") return make({{"losses", Operand::numbers({0, 10})}, {"probabilities", Operand::numbers({0.8, 0.2})}});
    if (code == "filtration_at") return make({{"complex", Operand::names({"v0", "e0", "f0"})}, {"values", Operand::numbers({0, 1, 2})}, {"threshold", Operand::number(1)}});
    if (code == "borda_count") return make({{"rankings", Operand::matrix({2, 3, {1, 2, 3, 2, 1, 3}})}});
    if (code == "eventually") return make({{"trace", Operand::numbers({0, 0.5, 2})}, {"predicate threshold", Operand::number(1)}});
    if (code == "poisson_birth") return make({{"rate", Operand::number(2)}, {"time", Operand::number(1)}, {"count", Operand::integer(2)}});
    if (code == "homology") return make({{"boundary k", Operand::matrix({1, 2, {1, 1}})}, {"boundary next", Operand::matrix({2, 1, {1, 1}})}});
    if (code == "outage_probability") return make({{"reliability", Operand::number(0.95)}});
    if (code == "fold_all") return make({{"values", Operand::numbers({1, 2, 3})}, {"combine", Operand::text("add")}, {"unit", Operand::number(0)}});
    if (code == "surreal_cut") return make({{"left", Operand::numbers({0})}, {"right", Operand::numbers({3})}});
    if (code == "sheaf_glue") return make({
        {"finite cover", Operand::relation({{{"U", "a"}, {"U", "b"}, {"V", "b"}, {"V", "c"}}})},
        {"local sections", Operand::relation({{{"U|a", "red"}, {"U|b", "gold"}, {"V|b", "gold"}, {"V|c", "blue"}}})}
    });
    throw std::logic_error("finite fixture missing for self number: " + std::string(unit));
}

inline std::vector<OperandDesignation> operator_fixture(const AuthoredWorld& world, std::string_view unit) {
    if (!world.find_unit(unit)) throw std::invalid_argument("fixture self number has no authored body: " + std::string(unit));
    return operator_fixture(unit);
}

inline AuthoredInvocation exercise_operator(const AuthoredWorld& world,
                                            LightRuntime& runtime,
                                            std::string_view unit,
                                            std::string consumer = "OPERATIONS lab",
                                            std::string purpose = "bounded one-operator finite exercise") {
    auto answer = invoke_authored_light(world, runtime, unit, operator_fixture(world, unit),
                                        std::move(consumer), std::move(purpose));
    if (!answer.invocation.exact()) throw std::logic_error("finite fixture did not realize self number: " + std::string(unit));
    return answer;
}

inline bool has_present_finite_executor(std::string_view code) noexcept {
    static constexpr std::string_view realized[]{
        "divinand", "sub", "add", "mul", "div", "pow", "is_empty", "exclusive_or", "bottom", "zero",
        "heyting_not", "rule30", "delete_vertex", "converse", "minimax_loss", "recip_inf", "forward_diff",
        "diagonal", "luk_or", "iterate", "aitken", "discrete_partition", "bayes", "reduce_free", "nearest_decode",
        "huber", "mix", "l_system_step", "delay_k", "kl_div", "reciprocal", "log_spiral", "eval_at", "dft",
        "group", "gossip_step", "hill_diversity", "offspring_pgf", "cyclic_shift", "replicator_rhs", "coboundary",
        "givens_rotation", "jain_fairness", "sinkhorn_step", "pareto_front", "conjugate", "convex_hull",
        "isotonic_fit", "local_maxima", "growth", "rule_of_succession", "vector_norm", "highest_bid",
        "generating_poly", "kleene_not", "cardinality", "spin", "median3", "decibel", "dtw_path", "doubling_map",
        "alpha_rename", "face_map", "reverse", "expected_loss", "filtration_at", "borda_count", "eventually",
        "poisson_birth", "outage_probability", "fold_all", "surreal_cut", "operad_substitute", "prim_rec",
        "both", "box_all", "compose", "term", "action_prefix", "erode", "shapley", "snell", "covers",
        "concept_close", "lyap_residual", "exact_cover", "bellman_opt", "voronoi", "maxplus_mv", "safe_gfp",
        "hutchinson", "right_adjoint", "ols", "prox", "union_sets", "cut_rule", "involute", "astar_path",
        "kernel", "np_test", "dempster_combine", "preimage", "spectral_bisect", "some_satisfy", "up_closure",
        "mahalanobis", "free_module", "inclusion_exclusion", "holonomy_product", "stable_match", "homology",
        "sheaf_glue"
    };
    return std::find(std::begin(realized), std::end(realized), code) != std::end(realized);
}

inline std::string_view integration_target_for(const LightDefinition& definition) noexcept {
    if (definition.unit == "MY LIGHT") return "APP | shared authored world | every source body";
    if (definition.branch == "NIHILISM") return "SUPPORT | EDITOR | graph and boundary commands";
    if (definition.branch == "REALITY") return "SUPPORT | APP | composition and live change";
    if (definition.branch == "INTIMACY") return "SUPPORT | EDITOR | relation, inference, care, and recovery domains";
    if (definition.branch == "FUSING") return "SUPPORT | both FRACTALIZERS | time, signal, mixture, and geometry";
    if (definition.branch == "DESIGNING") return "both FRACTALIZERS | RENDERER | layout, safety, and generated form";
    if (definition.branch == "METHODOLOGIES") return "SUPPORT | EDITOR | recursive language and numerical method";
    if (definition.branch == "PURPOSE") return "EDITOR | both FRACTALIZERS | search, fit, and chosen result";
    if (definition.branch == "GROWING") return "SUPPORT | both FRACTALIZERS | bounded evolution and measurement";
    if (definition.branch == "UNIVERSING") return "both FRACTALIZERS | RENDERER | spatial, media, and naming transforms";
    return "EDITOR | SUPPORT | time, order, recovery, and whole-work combination";
}

struct OperatorCapability {
    std::size_t catalog_index{};
    std::string_view self_number;
    std::string_view code;
    std::string_view operand_form;
    std::string_view mathematical_domain;
    std::string_view integration_targets;
    std::string_view evolution_route;
    bool present_finite_executor{};
    bool unrendered_expression{true};
    bool result_can_be_operand{true};
};

inline const std::array<OperatorCapability, light_catalog.size()>& operator_capabilities() {
    static const auto capabilities = [] {
        std::array<OperatorCapability, light_catalog.size()> result{};
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < light_catalog.size(); ++i) {
            const auto& definition = light_catalog[i];
            result[i] = OperatorCapability{i, definition.self_number, definition.code, definition.signature,
                definition.origin, integration_target_for(definition),
                "measured whole -> typed technical view -> self-number operation -> completed declared-domain result; otherwise no whole-self formation",
                has_present_finite_executor(definition.code), true, true};
        }
        return result;
    }();
    return capabilities;
}

inline const OperatorCapability* capability_for_unit(std::string_view unit) noexcept {
    const auto* definition = find_light_by_unit(unit);
    return definition ? &operator_capabilities()[light_catalog_index(*definition)] : nullptr;
}

struct Camera2Packet {
    Vec2 center{};
    Vec2 viewport{1280.0, 720.0};
    double zoom{1.0};
};

struct Camera3Packet {
    Vec3 eye{0.0, 0.0, -760.0};
    Vec3 target{};
    Vec3 up{0.0, 1.0, 0.0};
    Vec2 viewport{1280.0, 720.0};
    double field_of_view{pi / 3.0};
    double near_plane{0.1};
    double far_plane{10000.0};
};

enum class PortalDimension : std::uint8_t { planar, spatial };

struct PortalPacket {
    std::size_t node{no_node};
    PortalDimension source{PortalDimension::planar};
    PortalDimension destination{PortalDimension::spatial};
    Vec2 position{};
    Vec2 size{360.0, 240.0};
    std::uint32_t recursion_depth{};
    bool interactive{true};
};

struct RenderPacket {
    const AuthoredWorld* world{};
    Camera2Packet planar_camera;
    Camera3Packet spatial_camera;
    std::vector<std::size_t> attention;
    std::vector<PortalPacket> portals;
    std::vector<AppliedOperation> applied_operations;
    std::uint64_t revision{};
};

inline std::string hex_bytes(std::string_view value) {
    static constexpr char digits[] = "0123456789abcdef";
    std::string result;
    result.reserve(value.size() * 2);
    for (const auto byte : value) {
        const auto part = static_cast<unsigned char>(byte);
        result.push_back(digits[part >> 4]);
        result.push_back(digits[part & 0x0f]);
    }
    return result;
}

inline std::string hex_token(std::string_view value) {
    auto result = hex_bytes(value);
    return result.empty() ? std::string{"-"} : result;
}

inline std::string canonical_number(double value) {
    const auto bits = std::bit_cast<std::uint64_t>(value);
    std::ostringstream output;
    output.imbue(std::locale::classic());
    output << std::hex << std::setfill('0') << std::setw(16) << bits;
    return output.str();
}

inline std::string canonical_operand(const Operand& operand) {
    std::ostringstream output;
    output.imbue(std::locale::classic());
    const auto write_numbers = [&output](const NumberList& values) {
        output << values.size();
        for (const auto value : values) output << ':' << canonical_number(value);
    };
    const auto write_names = [&output](const NameList& values) {
        output << values.size();
        for (const auto& value : values) output << ':' << hex_bytes(value);
    };
    std::visit([&](const auto& value) {
        using T = std::decay_t<decltype(value)>;
        if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, std::monostate>) output << 'N';
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, bool>) output << "B:" << (value ? '1' : '0');
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, std::int64_t>) output << "I:" << value;
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, double>) output << "D:" << canonical_number(value);
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, std::string>) output << "S:" << hex_bytes(value);
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, NumberList>) { output << "NL:"; write_numbers(value); }
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, NameList>) { output << "SL:"; write_names(value); }
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, ComplexList>) {
            output << "CL:" << value.size();
            for (const auto& item : value) output << ':' << canonical_number(item.real()) << ':' << canonical_number(item.imag());
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, Point2List>) {
            output << "P2L:" << value.size();
            for (const auto point : value) output << ':' << canonical_number(point.x) << ':' << canonical_number(point.y);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, Point3List>) {
            output << "P3L:" << value.size();
            for (const auto point : value) output << ':' << canonical_number(point.x) << ':' << canonical_number(point.y) << ':' << canonical_number(point.z);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, Vec2>) output << "P2:" << canonical_number(value.x) << ':' << canonical_number(value.y);
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, Vec3>) output << "P3:" << canonical_number(value.x) << ':' << canonical_number(value.y) << ':' << canonical_number(value.z);
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, Matrix>) {
            output << "MX:" << value.rows << ':' << value.columns << ':'; write_numbers(value.values);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, RelationValue>) {
            output << "RL:" << value.pairs.size();
            for (const auto& pair : value.pairs) output << ':' << hex_bytes(pair.first) << ':' << hex_bytes(pair.second);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, GraphValue>) {
            output << "GR:"; write_names(value.vertices); output << ':' << value.edges.size();
            for (const auto& edge : value.edges) output << ':' << hex_bytes(edge.source) << ':' << hex_bytes(edge.target) << ':' << canonical_number(edge.weight);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, ProbabilityValue>) {
            output << "PR:"; write_names(value.outcomes); output << ':'; write_numbers(value.weights);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, TimeValue>) output << "TM:" << canonical_number(value.seconds);
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, ResourceRoute>) output << "RS:" << hex_bytes(value.path);
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, AuthoredBodyRoute>) output << "AR:" << hex_bytes(value.route);
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, TermValue>) { output << "TR:" << hex_bytes(value.operation) << ':'; write_names(value.arguments); }
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, OperadTreeValue>) {
            output << "OT:"; write_names(value.labels); output << ':' << value.parents.size();
            for (const auto parent : value.parents) output << ':' << parent;
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, OperadSubstitutions>) {
            output << "OS:" << value.grafts.size();
            for (const auto& graft : value.grafts) {
                output << ':' << hex_bytes(graft.slot) << ':'; write_names(graft.tree.labels); output << ':' << graft.tree.parents.size();
                for (const auto parent : graft.tree.parents) output << ':' << parent;
            }
        }
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, VoronoiDiagram>) {
            output << "VO:" << value.sites.size();
            for (const auto site : value.sites) output << ':' << canonical_number(site.x) << ':' << canonical_number(site.y);
            output << ':' << value.cells.size();
            for (const auto& cell : value.cells) { output << ':' << cell.size(); for (const auto point : cell) output << ':' << canonical_number(point.x) << ':' << canonical_number(point.y); }
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, FreeModuleValue>) {
            output << "FM:" << hex_bytes(value.ring) << ':'; write_names(value.basis); output << ':'; write_numbers(value.coordinates);
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, DivinandValue>) {
            output << "DV:" << value.catalog_extent << ':'; write_names(value.units); output << ':'; write_names(value.assigned_operators);
        }
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, ExpressionRoute>) output << "EX:" << value.value;
    }, operand.body);
    return output.str();
}

inline std::string canonical_workspace_text(const AuthoredWorld& world,
                                            const LightRuntime& runtime,
                                            std::span<const AppliedOperation> applied = {},
                                            std::span<const std::size_t> attention = {}) {
    std::ostringstream output;
    output.imbue(std::locale::classic());
    output << "MILESING-LIGHT-WORKSPACE 2\n";
    output << "WORLD " << world.revision << ' ' << world.nodes.size() << ' '
           << world.relations.size() << ' ' << world.authored_order.size() << '\n';
    for (const auto& node : world.nodes) {
        if (node.catalog_index >= light_catalog.size()) throw std::invalid_argument("world node catalog route");
        const auto& definition = light_catalog[node.catalog_index];
        output << "NODE " << node.id << ' ' << node.catalog_index << ' ' << node.parent << ' '
               << canonical_number(node.planar.x) << ' ' << canonical_number(node.planar.y) << ' '
               << canonical_number(node.spatial.x) << ' ' << canonical_number(node.spatial.y) << ' ' << canonical_number(node.spatial.z) << ' '
               << canonical_number(node.extent) << ' ' << canonical_number(node.rotation) << ' '
               << node.visible << ' ' << node.locked << ' '
               << hex_token(definition.unit) << ' ' << hex_token(definition.code) << ' ' << hex_token(definition.origin) << '\n';
    }
    for (const auto& relation : world.relations) output << "RELATION " << relation.source << ' ' << relation.target << '\n';
    output << "ORDER";
    for (const auto id : world.authored_order) output << ' ' << id;
    output << '\n';
    output << "ATTENTION";
    for (const auto id : attention) output << ' ' << id;
    output << '\n';
    for (const auto& expression : runtime.expressions()) {
        if (expression.catalog_index >= light_catalog.size()) throw std::invalid_argument("expression catalog route");
        output << "EXPRESSION " << expression.route.value << ' ' << expression.catalog_index << ' '
               << expression.operands.size() << ' ' << (expression.value ? 1 : 0) << ' '
               << hex_token(expression.note) << '\n';
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < expression.operands.size(); ++i) output << "OPERAND " << i << ' ' << canonical_operand(expression.operands[i]) << '\n';
        if (expression.value) output << "RESULT " << canonical_operand(*expression.value) << '\n';
    }
    for (const auto& operation : applied) {
        output << "APPLIED " << operation.expression.value << ' ' << operation.operator_world_node << ' '
               << operation.catalog_index << ' ' << operation.operands.size() << ' '
               << hex_token(operation.consumer) << ' ' << hex_token(operation.purpose) << '\n';
        for (const auto& designation : operation.operands) {
            output << "DESIGNATION " << designation.operand_index << ' ' << hex_token(designation.role) << ' '
                   << (designation.authored_node ? std::to_string(*designation.authored_node) : "-") << ' ';
            if (designation.spatial_position) {
                output << canonical_number(designation.spatial_position->x) << ':'
                       << canonical_number(designation.spatial_position->y) << ':'
                       << canonical_number(designation.spatial_position->z);
            } else output << '-';
            output << ' ' << canonical_operand(designation.value) << '\n';
        }
    }
    output << "END\n";
    return output.str();
}

inline std::wstring utf8_to_wide(std::string_view value) {
    if (value.empty()) return {};
    if (value.size() > static_cast<std::size_t>((std::numeric_limits<int>::max)())) throw std::length_error("UTF-8 body too large");
    const auto source_size = static_cast<int>(value.size());
    const auto needed = MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, MB_ERR_INVALID_CHARS, value.data(), source_size, nullptr, 0);
    if (!needed) throw std::runtime_error("invalid UTF-8");
    std::wstring result(static_cast<std::size_t>(needed), L'\0');
    if (!MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, MB_ERR_INVALID_CHARS, value.data(), source_size, result.data(), needed)) throw std::runtime_error("UTF-8 conversion failed");
    return result;
}

inline std::string wide_to_utf8(std::wstring_view value) {
    if (value.empty()) return {};
    if (value.size() > static_cast<std::size_t>((std::numeric_limits<int>::max)())) throw std::length_error("UTF-16 body too large");
    const auto source_size = static_cast<int>(value.size());
    const auto needed = WideCharToMultiByte(CP_UTF8, WC_ERR_INVALID_CHARS, value.data(), source_size, nullptr, 0, nullptr, nullptr);
    if (!needed) throw std::runtime_error("invalid UTF-16");
    std::string result(static_cast<std::size_t>(needed), '\0');
    if (!WideCharToMultiByte(CP_UTF8, WC_ERR_INVALID_CHARS, value.data(), source_size, result.data(), needed, nullptr, nullptr)) throw std::runtime_error("UTF-16 conversion failed");
    return result;
}

struct WorkspaceParseLimits {
    std::size_t maximum_bytes{64ull * 1024ull * 1024ull};
    std::size_t maximum_lines{400000};
    std::size_t maximum_line_bytes{8ull * 1024ull * 1024ull};
    std::size_t maximum_expressions{65536};
    std::size_t maximum_applied_operations{4096};
    std::size_t maximum_collection_items{65536};
    std::size_t maximum_total_collection_items{1048576};
    std::size_t maximum_decoded_string_bytes{1024ull * 1024ull};
    std::size_t maximum_replay_work{64000000};
};

struct ParsedWorkspace {
    AuthoredWorld world{};
    LightRuntime runtime{};
    std::vector<AppliedOperation> applied_operations{};
    std::vector<std::size_t> attention{};
};

struct WorkspaceParseResult {
    std::optional<ParsedWorkspace> workspace{};
    std::string error{};
    std::size_t line{};

    explicit operator bool() const noexcept { return workspace.has_value(); }
};

namespace canonical_detail {

struct ParseFailure final : std::runtime_error {
    std::size_t line{};
    ParseFailure(std::size_t source_line, std::string message)
        : std::runtime_error(std::move(message)), line(source_line) {}
};

inline void require(bool condition, std::size_t line, std::string message) {
    if (!condition) throw ParseFailure(line, std::move(message));
}

inline bool split_canonical_spaces(std::string_view line,
                                   std::vector<std::string_view>& fields) {
    fields.clear();
    if (line.empty() || line.front() == ' ' || line.back() == ' ') return false;
    std::size_t begin = 0;
    while (begin < line.size()) {
        const auto end = line.find(' ', begin);
        const auto field = line.substr(begin, end == std::string_view::npos
            ? line.size() - begin : end - begin);
        if (field.empty()) return false;
        fields.push_back(field);
        if (end == std::string_view::npos) break;
        begin = end + 1;
    }
    return true;
}

inline bool parse_unsigned(std::string_view token, std::uint64_t& value) noexcept {
    if (token.empty() || token.front() == '+' || token.front() == '-' ||
        (token.size() > 1 && token.front() == '0')) return false;
    const auto parsed = std::from_chars(token.data(), token.data() + token.size(), value, 10);
    return parsed.ec == std::errc{} && parsed.ptr == token.data() + token.size();
}

inline bool parse_size(std::string_view token, std::size_t& value) noexcept {
    std::uint64_t parsed{};
    if (!parse_unsigned(token, parsed) || parsed > (std::numeric_limits<std::size_t>::max)()) return false;
    value = static_cast<std::size_t>(parsed);
    return true;
}

inline bool parse_signed(std::string_view token, std::int64_t& value) noexcept {
    if (token.empty() || token.front() == '+' || token == "-0" ||
        (token.size() > 1 && token.front() == '0') ||
        (token.size() > 2 && token[0] == '-' && token[1] == '0')) return false;
    const auto parsed = std::from_chars(token.data(), token.data() + token.size(), value, 10);
    return parsed.ec == std::errc{} && parsed.ptr == token.data() + token.size();
}

inline bool parse_canonical_double(std::string_view token, double& value) noexcept {
    if (token.size() != 16) return false;
    std::uint64_t bits{};
    for (const char c : token) {
        std::uint64_t digit{};
        if (c >= '0' && c <= '9') digit = static_cast<std::uint64_t>(c - '0');
        else if (c >= 'a' && c <= 'f') digit = static_cast<std::uint64_t>(c - 'a' + 10);
        else return false;
        bits = (bits << 4) | digit;
    }
    value = std::bit_cast<double>(bits);
    return true;
}

inline bool valid_utf8(std::string_view value) noexcept {
    try {
        (void)utf8_to_wide(value);
        return true;
    } catch (...) {
        return false;
    }
}

inline bool decode_hex(std::string_view token, std::string& value,
                       const WorkspaceParseLimits& limits,
                       bool dash_is_empty = false) {
    if (dash_is_empty && token == "-") {
        value.clear();
        return true;
    }
    if ((token.size() & 1u) != 0 || token.size() / 2 > limits.maximum_decoded_string_bytes) return false;
    value.clear();
    value.reserve(token.size() / 2);
    const auto digit = [](char c, unsigned char& answer) {
        if (c >= '0' && c <= '9') { answer = static_cast<unsigned char>(c - '0'); return true; }
        if (c >= 'a' && c <= 'f') { answer = static_cast<unsigned char>(c - 'a' + 10); return true; }
        return false;
    };
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < token.size(); i += 2) {
        unsigned char high{}, low{};
        if (!digit(token[i], high) || !digit(token[i + 1], low)) return false;
        value.push_back(static_cast<char>((high << 4) | low));
    }
    return valid_utf8(value);
}

class ColonFields {
public:
    explicit ColonFields(std::string_view body) : body_(body) {}

    bool next(std::string_view& field) noexcept {
        if (finished_) return false;
        const auto end = body_.find(':', position_);
        field = body_.substr(position_, end == std::string_view::npos
            ? body_.size() - position_ : end - position_);
        if (end == std::string_view::npos) finished_ = true;
        else position_ = end + 1;
        return true;
    }

    bool done() const noexcept { return finished_; }

private:
    std::string_view body_{};
    std::size_t position_{};
    bool finished_{};
};

struct OperandBudget {
    const WorkspaceParseLimits& limits;
    std::size_t total_items{};

    bool claim(std::size_t count) noexcept {
        if (count > limits.maximum_collection_items ||
            count > limits.maximum_total_collection_items - total_items) return false;
        total_items += count;
        return true;
    }
};

inline bool parse_operand(std::string_view encoded, OperandBudget& budget,
                          Operand& operand, std::string& error) {
    if (encoded == "N") {
        operand = Operand{};
        return true;
    }
    const auto separator = encoded.find(':');
    if (separator == std::string_view::npos || separator == 0) {
        error = "unknown or malformed canonical operand tag";
        return false;
    }
    const auto tag = encoded.substr(0, separator);
    ColonFields fields(encoded.substr(separator + 1));
    const auto next = [&](std::string_view& field) {
        if (!fields.next(field)) { error = "canonical operand ended before its declared fields"; return false; }
        return true;
    };
    const auto next_size = [&](std::size_t& value) {
        std::string_view field;
        if (!next(field) || !parse_size(field, value)) { error = "invalid canonical operand count"; return false; }
        return true;
    };
    const auto next_u64 = [&](std::uint64_t& value) {
        std::string_view field;
        if (!next(field) || !parse_unsigned(field, value)) { error = "invalid canonical operand extent"; return false; }
        return true;
    };
    const auto next_integer = [&](std::int64_t& value) {
        std::string_view field;
        if (!next(field) || !parse_signed(field, value)) { error = "invalid canonical operand integer"; return false; }
        return true;
    };
    const auto next_number = [&](double& value) {
        std::string_view field;
        if (!next(field) || !parse_canonical_double(field, value)) { error = "invalid canonical operand number"; return false; }
        return true;
    };
    const auto next_text = [&](std::string& value) {
        std::string_view field;
        if (!next(field) || !decode_hex(field, value, budget.limits)) { error = "invalid canonical UTF-8 hex string"; return false; }
        return true;
    };
    const auto claim = [&](std::size_t count) {
        if (!budget.claim(count)) { error = "canonical operand collection exceeds its bound"; return false; }
        return true;
    };
    const auto next_numbers = [&](NumberList& values) {
        std::size_t count{};
        if (!next_size(count) || !claim(count)) return false;
        values.clear(); values.reserve(count);
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
            double value{}; if (!next_number(value)) return false; values.push_back(value);
        }
        return true;
    };
    const auto next_names = [&](NameList& values) {
        std::size_t count{};
        if (!next_size(count) || !claim(count)) return false;
        values.clear(); values.reserve(count);
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
            std::string value; if (!next_text(value)) return false; values.push_back(std::move(value));
        }
        return true;
    };
    const auto complete = [&]() {
        if (!fields.done()) { error = "canonical operand has trailing fields"; return false; }
        return true;
    };

    if (tag == "B") {
        std::string_view field;
        if (!next(field) || (field != "0" && field != "1") || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::truth(field == "1");
        return true;
    }
    if (tag == "I") {
        std::int64_t value{}; if (!next_integer(value) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::integer(value); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "D") {
        double value{}; if (!next_number(value) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::number(value); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "S") {
        std::string value; if (!next_text(value) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::text(std::move(value)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "NL") {
        NumberList values; if (!next_numbers(values) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::numbers(std::move(values)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "SL") {
        NameList values; if (!next_names(values) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::names(std::move(values)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "CL") {
        std::size_t count{}; if (!next_size(count) || !claim(count)) return false;
        ComplexList values; values.reserve(count);
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
            double real{}, imaginary{}; if (!next_number(real) || !next_number(imaginary)) return false;
            values.emplace_back(real, imaginary);
        }
        if (!complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::complexes(std::move(values)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "P2L" || tag == "P3L") {
        std::size_t count{}; if (!next_size(count) || !claim(count)) return false;
        if (tag == "P2L") {
            Point2List values; values.reserve(count);
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
                Vec2 value{}; if (!next_number(value.x) || !next_number(value.y)) return false; values.push_back(value);
            }
            if (!complete()) return false;
            operand = Operand::points(std::move(values)); return true;
        }
        Point3List values; values.reserve(count);
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
            Vec3 value{}; if (!next_number(value.x) || !next_number(value.y) || !next_number(value.z)) return false; values.push_back(value);
        }
        if (!complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::points(std::move(values)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "P2") {
        Vec2 value{}; if (!next_number(value.x) || !next_number(value.y) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::point(value); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "P3") {
        Vec3 value{}; if (!next_number(value.x) || !next_number(value.y) || !next_number(value.z) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::point(value); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "MX") {
        std::size_t rows{}, columns{}; NumberList values;
        if (!next_size(rows) || !next_size(columns) || !next_numbers(values) || !complete()) return false;
        Matrix matrix{rows, columns, std::move(values)};
        if (rows > budget.limits.maximum_collection_items ||
            columns > budget.limits.maximum_collection_items ||
            ((rows == 0) != (columns == 0)) ||
            (rows != 0 && columns > (std::numeric_limits<std::size_t>::max)() / rows) ||
            rows * columns != matrix.values.size() || !matrix.valid()) {
            error = "canonical matrix dimensions do not exactly match its finite value body";
            return false;
        }
        operand = Operand::matrix(std::move(matrix)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "RL") {
        std::size_t count{}; if (!next_size(count) || !claim(count)) return false;
        RelationValue relation; relation.pairs.reserve(count);
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
            std::string left, right; if (!next_text(left) || !next_text(right)) return false;
            relation.pairs.emplace_back(std::move(left), std::move(right));
        }
        if (!complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::relation(std::move(relation)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "GR") {
        GraphValue graph; if (!next_names(graph.vertices)) return false;
        std::size_t count{}; if (!next_size(count) || !claim(count)) return false;
        graph.edges.reserve(count);
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
            GraphEdge edge; if (!next_text(edge.source) || !next_text(edge.target) || !next_number(edge.weight)) return false;
            graph.edges.push_back(std::move(edge));
        }
        if (!complete()) return false;
        std::unordered_set<std::string> vertices;
        vertices.reserve(graph.vertices.size());
        for (const auto& vertex : graph.vertices) {
            if (!vertices.insert(vertex).second) { error = "canonical graph vertex IDs must be unique"; return false; }
        }
        for (const auto& edge : graph.edges) {
            if (!vertices.contains(edge.source) || !vertices.contains(edge.target) || !std::isfinite(edge.weight)) {
                error = "canonical graph edge has an absent endpoint or nonfinite weight";
                return false;
            }
        }
        operand = Operand::graph(std::move(graph)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "PR") {
        ProbabilityValue probability;
        if (!next_names(probability.outcomes) || !next_numbers(probability.weights) || !complete()) return false;
        if (probability.outcomes.size() != probability.weights.size()) {
            error = "canonical probability outcomes and weights have different extents";
            return false;
        }
        operand = Operand::probability(std::move(probability)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "TM") {
        double seconds{}; if (!next_number(seconds) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::time(seconds); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "RS" || tag == "AR") {
        std::string route; if (!next_text(route) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = tag == "RS" ? Operand::resource(std::move(route)) : Operand::authored(std::move(route));
        return true;
    }
    if (tag == "TR") {
        TermValue term; if (!next_text(term.operation) || !next_names(term.arguments) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::term(std::move(term)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "OT") {
        OperadTreeValue tree; if (!next_names(tree.labels)) return false;
        std::size_t count{}; if (!next_size(count) || !claim(count)) return false;
        tree.parents.reserve(count);
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) { std::int64_t parent{}; if (!next_integer(parent)) return false; tree.parents.push_back(parent); }
        if (!complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::operad_tree(std::move(tree)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "OS") {
        std::size_t count{}; if (!next_size(count) || !claim(count)) return false;
        OperadSubstitutions substitutions; substitutions.grafts.reserve(count);
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < count; ++i) {
            OperadGraft graft; if (!next_text(graft.slot) || !next_names(graft.tree.labels)) return false;
            std::size_t parents{}; if (!next_size(parents) || !claim(parents)) return false;
            graft.tree.parents.reserve(parents);
            for (std::size_t j = 0; j < parents; ++j) { std::int64_t parent{}; if (!next_integer(parent)) return false; graft.tree.parents.push_back(parent); }
            substitutions.grafts.push_back(std::move(graft));
        }
        if (!complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::operad_substitutions(std::move(substitutions)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "VO") {
        VoronoiDiagram diagram;
        std::size_t sites{}; if (!next_size(sites) || !claim(sites)) return false;
        diagram.sites.reserve(sites);
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < sites; ++i) { Vec2 point{}; if (!next_number(point.x) || !next_number(point.y)) return false; diagram.sites.push_back(point); }
        std::size_t cells{}; if (!next_size(cells) || !claim(cells)) return false;
        diagram.cells.reserve(cells);
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < cells; ++i) {
            std::size_t points{}; if (!next_size(points) || !claim(points)) return false;
            Point2List cell; cell.reserve(points);
            for (std::size_t j = 0; j < points; ++j) { Vec2 point{}; if (!next_number(point.x) || !next_number(point.y)) return false; cell.push_back(point); }
            diagram.cells.push_back(std::move(cell));
        }
        if (!complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::voronoi(std::move(diagram)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "FM") {
        FreeModuleValue module;
        if (!next_text(module.ring) || !next_names(module.basis) || !next_numbers(module.coordinates) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::free_module(std::move(module)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "DV") {
        DivinandValue divinand;
        if (!next_u64(divinand.catalog_extent) || !next_names(divinand.units) ||
            !next_names(divinand.assigned_operators) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::divinand(std::move(divinand)); return true;
    }
    if (tag == "EX") {
        std::size_t route{}; if (!next_size(route) || !complete()) return false;
        operand = Operand::expression(route); return true;
    }
    error = "unknown canonical operand tag: " + std::string(tag);
    return false;
}

inline bool expression_route_precedes(const Operand& operand, std::size_t expression) noexcept {
    const auto* route = std::get_if<ExpressionRoute>(&operand.body);
    return !route || route->value < expression;
}

inline bool validate_expression_ledger(std::span<const Expression> expressions,
                                       std::size_t limit, std::string& error) {
    if (expressions.size() > limit) { error = "expression ledger exceeds the runtime retention bound"; return false; }
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < expressions.size(); ++i) {
        const Expression& expression = expressions[i];
        if (expression.route.value != i) { error = "ExpressionRoutes must be unique, contiguous, and stable"; return false; }
        if (expression.catalog_index >= light_catalog.size()) { error = "expression catalog route is outside MY LIGHT"; return false; }
        const auto& definition = light_catalog[expression.catalog_index];
        if (expression.operands.size() < definition.minimum_operands ||
            expression.operands.size() > definition.maximum_operands) {
            error = "expression arity disagrees with its assigned Light operator"; return false;
        }
        for (const Operand& operand : expression.operands) {
            if (!expression_route_precedes(operand, i)) { error = "expression operand route is forward, self-referential, or absent"; return false; }
        }
        if (expression.value && !expression_route_precedes(*expression.value, i)) {
            error = "expression result route is forward, self-referential, or absent"; return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
}

inline bool claim_replay_work(std::size_t& total, std::size_t amount,
                              std::size_t limit) noexcept {
    if (amount > limit - total) return false;
    total += amount;
    return true;
}

inline bool claim_replay_product(std::size_t& total,
                                 std::initializer_list<std::size_t> factors,
                                 std::size_t limit) noexcept {
    std::size_t product = 1;
    for (const auto factor : factors) {
        if (factor != 0 && product > (limit - total) / factor) return false;
        product *= factor;
    }
    return claim_replay_work(total, product, limit);
}

inline std::size_t operand_replay_items(const Operand& operand,
                                        std::size_t ceiling) noexcept {
    const auto add = [ceiling](std::size_t left, std::size_t right) {
        return right > ceiling - (std::min)(left, ceiling) ? ceiling : left + right;
    };
    return std::visit([&](const auto& value) -> std::size_t {
        using T = std::decay_t<decltype(value)>;
        if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, std::monostate> || std::is_same_v<T, bool> ||
                      std::is_same_v<T, std::int64_t> || std::is_same_v<T, double> ||
                      std::is_same_v<T, Vec2> || std::is_same_v<T, Vec3> ||
                      std::is_same_v<T, TimeValue> || std::is_same_v<T, ExpressionRoute>) return 1;
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, std::string>) return (std::max)(std::size_t{1}, value.size());
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, NumberList> || std::is_same_v<T, ComplexList> ||
                           std::is_same_v<T, Point2List> || std::is_same_v<T, Point3List>) return value.size();
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, NameList>) {
            std::size_t result = value.size(); for (const auto& name : value) result = add(result, name.size()); return result;
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, Matrix>) {
            return add(value.values.size(), add(value.rows, value.columns));
        }
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, RelationValue>) {
            std::size_t result = value.pairs.size(); for (const auto& pair : value.pairs) result = add(add(result, pair.first.size()), pair.second.size()); return result;
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, GraphValue>) return add(value.vertices.size(), value.edges.size());
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, ProbabilityValue>) return add(value.outcomes.size(), value.weights.size());
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, ResourceRoute>) return (std::max)(std::size_t{1}, value.path.size());
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, AuthoredBodyRoute>) return (std::max)(std::size_t{1}, value.route.size());
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, TermValue>) return add(value.operation.size(), value.arguments.size());
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, OperadTreeValue>) return add(value.labels.size(), value.parents.size());
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, OperadSubstitutions>) {
            std::size_t result = value.grafts.size(); for (const auto& graft : value.grafts) result = add(result, add(graft.tree.labels.size(), graft.tree.parents.size())); return result;
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, VoronoiDiagram>) {
            std::size_t result = value.sites.size(); for (const auto& cell : value.cells) result = add(result, cell.size()); return result;
        } else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, FreeModuleValue>) return add(value.basis.size(), value.coordinates.size());
        else if constexpr (std::is_same_v<T, DivinandValue>) return add(value.units.size(), value.assigned_operators.size());
        else return ceiling;
    }, operand.body);
}

inline bool claim_expression_replay_work(const Expression& expression,
                                         std::size_t& total,
                                         std::size_t limit) {
    if (!claim_replay_work(total, 64, limit)) return false;
    std::size_t item_extent{};
    for (const Operand& operand : expression.operands) {
        if (!claim_replay_work(total, canonical_operand(operand).size(), limit)) return false;
        const auto items = operand_replay_items(operand, limit);
        if (items > limit - item_extent) return false;
        item_extent += items;
    }
    // Every accepted replay gets a conservative quadratic allowance before
    // operation-specific higher-order costs. This closes generic nested-scan
    // bypasses without trusting compact encodings of very large collections.
    if (!claim_replay_product(total, {item_extent, item_extent}, limit)) return false;
    const auto code = light_catalog[expression.catalog_index].code;
    const auto matrix_at = [&](std::size_t index) -> const Matrix* {
        return index < expression.operands.size()
            ? std::get_if<Matrix>(&expression.operands[index].body) : nullptr;
    };
    const auto numbers_at = [&](std::size_t index) -> const NumberList* {
        return index < expression.operands.size()
            ? std::get_if<NumberList>(&expression.operands[index].body) : nullptr;
    };
    const auto points_at = [&](std::size_t index) -> const Point2List* {
        return index < expression.operands.size()
            ? std::get_if<Point2List>(&expression.operands[index].body) : nullptr;
    };
    const auto graph_at = [&](std::size_t index) -> const GraphValue* {
        return index < expression.operands.size()
            ? std::get_if<GraphValue>(&expression.operands[index].body) : nullptr;
    };
    const auto relation_at = [&](std::size_t index) -> const RelationValue* {
        return index < expression.operands.size()
            ? std::get_if<RelationValue>(&expression.operands[index].body) : nullptr;
    };
    const auto names_at = [&](std::size_t index) -> const NameList* {
        return index < expression.operands.size()
            ? std::get_if<NameList>(&expression.operands[index].body) : nullptr;
    };
    if (code == "exact_cover") {
        if (const auto* matrix = matrix_at(0)) {
            const std::size_t visits = matrix->rows >= 18
                ? 250000 : (std::size_t{1} << matrix->rows);
            return claim_replay_product(total, {matrix->rows, matrix->columns, visits}, limit);
        }
        return claim_replay_work(total, 1, limit);
    }
    if (code == "growth" || code == "iterate") {
        std::int64_t count{};
        if (expression.operands.size() == 3 && integral_operand(expression.operands[1], count) && count > 0) {
            const auto current = operand_replay_items(expression.operands[2], limit);
            return claim_replay_product(total, {static_cast<std::size_t>(count), current, current}, limit);
        }
    }
    if (code == "prim_rec") {
        std::int64_t count{};
        if (expression.operands.size() == 3 && integral_operand(expression.operands[2], count) && count > 0) {
            const auto current = operand_replay_items(expression.operands[0], limit);
            return claim_replay_product(total, {static_cast<std::size_t>(count), current, current}, limit);
        }
    }
    if (code == "l_system_step") {
        const auto* word = expression.operands.empty() ? nullptr : std::get_if<std::string>(&expression.operands[0].body);
        const auto* rules = relation_at(1);
        if (word && rules) {
            std::size_t maximum_replacement = 1;
            for (const auto& rule : rules->pairs) maximum_replacement = (std::max)(maximum_replacement, rule.second.size());
            return claim_replay_product(total, {word->size(), rules->pairs.size() + maximum_replacement}, limit);
        }
    }
    if (code == "up_closure") {
        if (const auto* relation = relation_at(0)) {
            const auto seed = names_at(1); const auto n = relation->pairs.size();
            return claim_replay_product(total, {n, n, n + (seed ? seed->size() : 0) + 1}, limit);
        }
    }
    if (code == "covers") {
        if (const auto* relation = relation_at(0)) {
            const auto n = relation->pairs.size(); return claim_replay_product(total, {n, n, n}, limit);
        }
    }
    if (code == "concept_close") {
        if (const auto* relation = relation_at(0)) {
            const auto objects = names_at(1); const auto n = relation->pairs.size();
            return claim_replay_product(total, {n, n, (objects ? objects->size() : 0) + 1}, limit);
        }
    }
    if (code == "preimage") {
        if (const auto* relation = relation_at(0)) if (const auto* target = names_at(1))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {relation->pairs.size(), target->size() + 1}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "compose") {
        if (const auto* outer = relation_at(0)) if (const auto* inner = relation_at(1))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {outer->pairs.size(), inner->pairs.size()}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "dft") {
        if (const auto* values = numbers_at(0)) return claim_replay_product(total, {values->size(), values->size()}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "dtw_path") {
        if (const auto* left = numbers_at(0)) if (const auto* right = numbers_at(1))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {left->size(), right->size()}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "spectral_bisect") {
        if (const auto* graph = graph_at(0))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {graph->vertices.size(), graph->vertices.size(),
                                                 graph->vertices.size(), graph->vertices.size(), 20}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "astar_path") {
        if (const auto* graph = graph_at(0))
            return claim_replay_work(total, graph->vertices.size() + graph->edges.size() * 8, limit);
    }
    if (code == "voronoi") {
        if (const auto* points = points_at(0))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {points->size(), points->size(), 8}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "hutchinson") {
        if (const auto* points = points_at(0)) if (const auto* maps = matrix_at(1))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {points->size(), maps->rows, 8}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "kernel") {
        if (const auto* matrix = matrix_at(0))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {matrix->rows, matrix->columns,
                                                 (std::min)(matrix->rows, matrix->columns)}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "ols") {
        if (const auto* matrix = matrix_at(0))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {matrix->rows + matrix->columns,
                                                 matrix->columns, matrix->columns}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "mahalanobis") {
        if (const auto* matrix = matrix_at(2))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {matrix->rows, matrix->rows, matrix->rows}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "pareto_front") {
        if (const auto* matrix = matrix_at(0))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {matrix->rows, matrix->rows, matrix->columns}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "stable_match") {
        if (const auto* matrix = matrix_at(0))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {matrix->rows, matrix->columns, 4}, limit);
    }
    if (code == "homology") {
        if (const auto* first = matrix_at(0)) if (const auto* second = matrix_at(1))
            return claim_replay_product(total, {first->rows + second->rows,
                                                 first->columns + second->columns,
                                                 first->columns + 1}, limit);
    }
    return true;
}

inline bool replay_expression_ledger(std::span<const Expression> claimed,
                                     std::size_t expression_limit,
                                     std::size_t maximum_work,
                                     std::vector<Expression>& replayed,
                                     std::string& error) {
    if (!validate_expression_ledger(claimed, expression_limit, error)) return false;
    replayed.clear();
    replayed.reserve(claimed.size());
    std::size_t work{};
    for (const Expression& expression : claimed) {
        if (!claim_expression_replay_work(expression, work, maximum_work)) {
            error = "deterministic expression replay exceeds its bounded work budget";
            return false;
        }
        try {
            // A fresh runtime isolates nested finite realizations. Every ledger
            // entry is still replayed in its stable route order; claimed values
            // and notes never become authority over the assigned operator.
            LightRuntime probe(expression_limit);
            const auto& definition = light_catalog[expression.catalog_index];
            Invocation actual = probe.invoke_with_validated_prefix(
                definition.code, expression.operands, expression.route.value);
            if (actual.value.has_value() != expression.value.has_value() ||
                (actual.value && canonical_operand(*actual.value) != canonical_operand(*expression.value))) {
                error = "serialized expression RESULT disagrees with deterministic operator replay";
                return false;
            }
            if (actual.note != expression.note) {
                error = "serialized expression note disagrees with deterministic operator semantics";
                return false;
            }
            replayed.push_back(Expression{expression.route, expression.catalog_index,
                                          expression.operands, std::move(actual.value),
                                          std::move(actual.note)});
        } catch (const std::exception& failure) {
            error = std::string("deterministic operator replay failed: ") + failure.what();
            return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
}

inline bool finite_world_number(double value, double magnitude = 1.0e12) noexcept {
    return std::isfinite(value) && std::abs(value) <= magnitude;
}

inline bool validate_world(const AuthoredWorld& world, std::string& error) {
    const AuthoredWorld canonical = AuthoredWorld::from_light();
    if (world.revision == 0) { error = "world revision must be positive"; return false; }
    if (world.nodes.size() != light_catalog.size() || world.nodes.size() != canonical.nodes.size()) {
        error = "workspace must contain every current Light self number exactly once"; return false;
    }
    if (world.relations.size() != canonical.relations.size() || world.authored_order.size() != world.nodes.size()) {
        error = "world relation or authored-order extent is inconsistent"; return false;
    }
    std::vector<bool> ids(world.nodes.size(), false), catalogs(light_catalog.size(), false);
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < world.nodes.size(); ++i) {
        const WorldNode& node = world.nodes[i];
        const WorldNode& expected = canonical.nodes[i];
        if (node.id >= ids.size() || ids[node.id] || node.catalog_index >= catalogs.size() || catalogs[node.catalog_index]) {
            error = "world node IDs and catalog routes must be unique and in range"; return false;
        }
        ids[node.id] = true; catalogs[node.catalog_index] = true;
        if (node.id != expected.id || node.catalog_index != expected.catalog_index || node.parent != expected.parent) {
            error = "world node ID, catalog association, or parent differs from the current Light structure"; return false;
        }
        if (!finite_world_number(node.planar.x) || !finite_world_number(node.planar.y) ||
            !finite_world_number(node.spatial.x) || !finite_world_number(node.spatial.y) ||
            !finite_world_number(node.spatial.z) || !finite_world_number(node.rotation) ||
            !finite_world_number(node.extent, 1.0e9) || node.extent < 0.0) {
            error = "world geometry contains a nonfinite or unsafe value"; return false;
        }
    }
    std::unordered_set<std::size_t> relation_keys;
    relation_keys.reserve(world.relations.size());
    for (const WorldRelation& relation : world.relations) {
        if (relation.source >= world.nodes.size() || relation.target >= world.nodes.size() || relation.source == relation.target) {
            error = "world relation contains an invalid node ID"; return false;
        }
        const auto key = relation.source * world.nodes.size() + relation.target;
        if (!relation_keys.insert(key).second || world.nodes[relation.target].parent != relation.source) {
            error = "world relation is duplicated or disagrees with the target parent"; return false;
        }
    }
    for (std::size_t i = 1; i < world.nodes.size(); ++i) {
        const auto key = world.nodes[i].parent * world.nodes.size() + world.nodes[i].id;
        if (!relation_keys.contains(key)) { error = "world parent edge is absent from the relation ledger"; return false; }
    }
    std::vector<bool> ordered(world.nodes.size(), false);
    for (const auto id : world.authored_order) {
        if (id >= ordered.size() || ordered[id]) { error = "authored order is not a complete permutation of stable node IDs"; return false; }
        ordered[id] = true;
    }
    return true;
}

inline bool validate_applied(const ParsedWorkspace& workspace, std::string& error) {
    const auto& expressions = workspace.runtime.expressions();
    std::optional<std::size_t> previous_route;
    for (const AppliedOperation& applied : workspace.applied_operations) {
        if (applied.expression.value >= expressions.size()) { error = "applied operation names an absent ExpressionRoute"; return false; }
        if (previous_route && applied.expression.value <= *previous_route) {
            error = "applied operation receipts are duplicated or out of expression order"; return false;
        }
        previous_route = applied.expression.value;
        const Expression& expression = expressions[applied.expression.value];
        const WorldNode* operator_node = workspace.world.find(applied.operator_world_node);
        if (!operator_node || applied.catalog_index >= light_catalog.size() ||
            expression.catalog_index != applied.catalog_index ||
            operator_node->catalog_index != applied.catalog_index) {
            error = "applied expression, operator node, and Light catalog route disagree"; return false;
        }
        if (applied.operands.size() != expression.operands.size()) {
            error = "applied operand designation count disagrees with the expression"; return false;
        }
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < applied.operands.size(); ++i) {
            const OperandDesignation& designation = applied.operands[i];
            if (designation.operand_index != i ||
                canonical_operand(designation.value) != canonical_operand(expression.operands[i])) {
                error = "applied operand index or exact designated value disagrees with the expression"; return false;
            }
            if (designation.authored_node && !workspace.world.find(*designation.authored_node)) {
                error = "operand designation names an absent authored node"; return false;
            }
            if (designation.spatial_position &&
                (!finite_world_number(designation.spatial_position->x) ||
                 !finite_world_number(designation.spatial_position->y) ||
                 !finite_world_number(designation.spatial_position->z))) {
                error = "operand designation contains a nonfinite spatial position"; return false;
            }
        }
        if (applied.result.has_value() != expression.value.has_value() ||
            (applied.result && canonical_operand(*applied.result) != canonical_operand(*expression.value))) {
            error = "applied result disagrees with its retained expression result"; return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
}

} // namespace canonical_detail

inline bool LightRuntime::restore_expressions(std::vector<Expression> expressions,
                                              std::string& error,
                                              std::size_t maximum_replay_work) {
    std::vector<Expression> replayed;
    const auto accepted_work = (std::min)(maximum_replay_work, replay_work_limit_);
    if (!canonical_detail::replay_expression_ledger(expressions, expression_limit_,
                                                     accepted_work,
                                                     replayed, error)) return false;
    std::size_t retained_work{};
    for (const Expression& expression : replayed) {
        if (!canonical_detail::claim_expression_replay_work(
                expression, retained_work, accepted_work)) {
            error = "restored expression ledger exceeds the live replay-work extent";
            return false;
        }
    }
    expressions_.swap(replayed);
    replay_work_retained_ = retained_work;
    error.clear();
    return true;
}

inline bool validate_parsed_workspace(const ParsedWorkspace& workspace,
                                      std::string& error) {
    if (!canonical_detail::validate_world(workspace.world, error)) return false;
    if (!canonical_detail::validate_expression_ledger(workspace.runtime.expressions(),
                                                       workspace.runtime.expression_limit(), error)) return false;
    if (!canonical_detail::validate_applied(workspace, error)) return false;
    std::unordered_set<std::size_t> attended;
    attended.reserve(workspace.attention.size());
    for (const auto id : workspace.attention) {
        if (!workspace.world.find(id) || !attended.insert(id).second) {
            error = "attention must contain unique stable authored node IDs";
            return false;
        }
    }
    return true;
}

inline bool exact_legacy_v1_node_tuple(std::size_t catalog_index,
                                       std::string_view self_number,
                                       std::string_view code,
                                       std::string_view origin) noexcept {
    // Version 1 is accepted only through its exact published tuples.  ABSENTISM
    // used the historical code spelling logical_not, and the definitions below
    // used the exact historical origin spellings enumerated here. Current meaning
    // never inherits either historical spelling from the file.
    if (catalog_index >= 111 || catalog_index >= light_catalog.size()) return false;
    const auto& current = light_catalog[catalog_index];
    std::string_view legacy_code = current.code;
    std::string_view legacy_origin = current.origin;
    static constexpr std::array<std::size_t, 70> lowercase_origin_routes{
        8, 9, 11, 14, 15, 17, 19, 20, 22, 24, 25, 26, 28, 29,
        30, 32, 33, 35, 37, 38, 39, 40, 41, 42, 44, 46, 47, 49,
        50, 52, 53, 54, 55, 57, 58, 59, 60, 61, 62, 64, 65, 69,
        70, 71, 73, 74, 75, 80, 81, 82, 83, 84, 85, 90, 91, 92,
        93, 94, 95, 96, 98, 99, 101, 102, 103, 105, 107, 108, 109, 110
    };
    switch (catalog_index) {
    case 6:  legacy_code = "logical_not";
             legacy_origin = "intuitionistic propositional logic"; break;       // ABSENTISM
    case 13: legacy_origin = "Riemann-sphere arithmetic"; break;                // INFINITY
    case 43: legacy_origin = "reproducing-kernel functional analysis"; break;   // PRESENTLY
    case 45: legacy_origin = "BEDMAS arithmetic"; break;                         // DESIGNING
    case 77: legacy_origin = "Morse theory"; break;                              // CREST
    case 88: legacy_origin = "cardinal arithmetic"; break;                       // SIZE
    case 97: legacy_origin = "nominal-set theory"; break;                        // NAMA
    default: break;
    }
    bool exact_origin = origin == legacy_origin;
    if (std::find(lowercase_origin_routes.begin(), lowercase_origin_routes.end(),
                  catalog_index) != lowercase_origin_routes.end()) {
        exact_origin = origin.size() == current.origin.size() && !origin.empty() &&
            current.origin.front() >= 'A' && current.origin.front() <= 'Z' &&
            origin.front() == static_cast<char>(current.origin.front() - 'A' + 'a') &&
            origin.substr(1) == current.origin.substr(1);
    }
    return self_number == current.self_number && code == legacy_code && exact_origin;
}

inline bool exact_legacy_v1_divinand_value(const DivinandValue& value) noexcept {
    if (value.catalog_extent != 111 || value.units.size() != 111 ||
        value.assigned_operators.size() != 111) return false;
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < 111; ++i) {
        const std::string_view legacy_code = i == 6 ? std::string_view{"logical_not"}
                                                    : light_catalog[i].code;
        if (value.units[i] != light_catalog[i].self_number ||
            value.assigned_operators[i] != legacy_code) return false;
    }
    return true;
}

inline std::size_t exact_legacy_v1_expression_arity(std::size_t catalog_index) noexcept {
    switch (catalog_index) {
    case 0:  return 0; // MY LIGHT: published catalog snapshot
    case 4:  return 0; // NULLISM: implicit untagged bottom
    case 6:  return 1; // ABSENTISM: Boolean fixture before the finite Heyting frame was explicit
    case 54: return 2; // RIGHTLY: implicit source and target chains
    case 61: return 1; // TENSIONS: implicit consecutive path graph
    case 76: return 2; // TRUST: implicit discernment frame
    case 77: return 1; // CREST: implicit path graph
    case 98: return 1; // HOLA: implicit closed row-index route
    default:
        return catalog_index < light_catalog.size()
            ? light_catalog[catalog_index].minimum_operands : 0;
    }
}

inline bool legacy_v1_operands_require_migration(std::size_t catalog_index) noexcept {
    return catalog_index == 0 || catalog_index == 4 || catalog_index == 6 ||
           catalog_index == 54 || catalog_index == 61 || catalog_index == 76 ||
           catalog_index == 77 || catalog_index == 98;
}

inline std::size_t legacy_v1_designation_target(std::size_t catalog_index,
                                                 std::size_t historical_index) noexcept {
    if (catalog_index == 6 || catalog_index == 61 || catalog_index == 77 || catalog_index == 98)
        return historical_index + 1;
    if (catalog_index == 54) return historical_index + 2;
    if (catalog_index == 76) return historical_index + 1;
    return historical_index;
}

inline std::string_view legacy_v1_synthesized_role(std::size_t catalog_index,
                                                    std::size_t current_index) noexcept {
    if (catalog_index == 0) return current_index == 0
        ? "published version-1 divinand value" : "empty migrated Light route";
    if (catalog_index == 4 && current_index == 0) return "singleton pointed domain derived from published bottom";
    if (catalog_index == 6 && current_index == 0) return "singleton finite Heyting frame";
    if (catalog_index == 54 && current_index == 0) return "index-chain source poset";
    if (catalog_index == 54 && current_index == 1) return "numeric image-plus-target poset";
    if (catalog_index == 61 && current_index == 0) return "consecutive oriented path graph";
    if (catalog_index == 76 && current_index == 0) return "exact discernment frame derived from focal sets";
    if (catalog_index == 77 && current_index == 0) return "consecutive undirected path graph";
    if (catalog_index == 98 && current_index == 0) return "closed row-index loop";
    return {};
}

inline bool legacy_v1_designation_matches(std::size_t catalog_index,
                                          std::size_t historical_index,
                                          const Operand& historical_value,
                                          const Expression& current_expression) {
    const auto target = legacy_v1_designation_target(catalog_index, historical_index);
    if (target >= current_expression.operands.size()) return false;
    if (catalog_index == 6 && historical_index == 0) {
        const auto* proposition = std::get_if<bool>(&historical_value.body);
        const auto* current = std::get_if<NameList>(&current_expression.operands[target].body);
        return proposition && current &&
            (*proposition ? *current == NameList{"world"} : current->empty());
    }
    return canonical_operand(historical_value) ==
           canonical_operand(current_expression.operands[target]);
}

inline bool legacy_v1_claim_matches(const std::optional<Operand>& claimed,
                                    const std::optional<Operand>& expected) {
    return claimed.has_value() == expected.has_value() &&
           (!claimed || canonical_operand(*claimed) == canonical_operand(*expected));
}

inline bool migrate_exact_legacy_v1_expression(Expression& expression,
                                                std::string& error) {
    const auto fail = [&](std::string message) {
        error = std::move(message);
        return false;
    };
    switch (expression.catalog_index) {
    case 0: {
        const auto* legacy_whole = expression.value
            ? std::get_if<DivinandValue>(&expression.value->body) : nullptr;
        if (!legacy_whole || !exact_legacy_v1_divinand_value(*legacy_whole))
            return fail("version-1 zero-arity divinand must retain its exact published 111-entry catalog value");
        expression.operands = {*expression.value, Operand::names({})};
        return true;
    }
    case 4: {
        if (expression.operands.size() != 0 || !expression.value ||
            !std::holds_alternative<std::monostate>(expression.value->body))
            return fail("version-1 NULLISM must carry its exact historical untagged bottom result");
        expression.operands = {Operand::term(
            TermValue{"singleton_pointed_domain", {"bottom"}})};
        return true;
    }
    case 6: {
