        const auto* proposition = expression.operands.size() == 1
            ? std::get_if<bool>(&expression.operands[0].body) : nullptr;
        const std::optional<Operand> expected = proposition
            ? std::optional<Operand>{Operand::truth(!*proposition)} : std::nullopt;
        if (!proposition || !legacy_v1_claim_matches(expression.value, expected))
            return fail("version-1 ABSENTISM must carry one Boolean proposition and its exact historical negation");
        expression.operands = {
            Operand::graph(GraphValue{{"world"}, {}}),
            Operand::names(*proposition ? NameList{"world"} : NameList{})};
        return true;
    }
    case 54: {
        const auto* map = expression.operands.size() == 2
            ? std::get_if<NumberList>(&expression.operands[0].body) : nullptr;
        const auto y = expression.operands.size() == 2 && expression.operands[1].numeric()
            ? std::optional<double>{expression.operands[1].as_number()} : std::nullopt;
        if (!map || !y || !std::isfinite(*y) ||
            !std::all_of(map->begin(), map->end(), [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); }) ||
            !std::is_sorted(map->begin(), map->end()))
            return fail("version-1 RIGHTLY must carry one exact finite monotone numeric chain map and one finite target");
        const auto position = std::upper_bound(map->begin(), map->end(), *y);
        if (position == map->begin())
            return fail("version-1 RIGHTLY target has no historical preimage-below member to migrate");
        const std::optional<Operand> expected{Operand::integer(
            static_cast<std::int64_t>((position - map->begin()) - 1))};
        if (!legacy_v1_claim_matches(expression.value, expected))
            return fail("version-1 RIGHTLY result disagrees with its exact historical finite-chain right adjoint");
        const Operand old_map = expression.operands[0];
        const Operand old_y = expression.operands[1];
        expression.operands = {
            Operand::term(TermValue{"index_chain", {std::to_string(map->size())}}),
            Operand::term(TermValue{"induced_numeric_chain", {}}), old_map, old_y};
        return true;
    }
    case 61: {
        const auto* values = expression.operands.size() == 1
            ? std::get_if<NumberList>(&expression.operands[0].body) : nullptr;
        if (!values || !std::all_of(values->begin(), values->end(),
                                    [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); }))
            return fail("version-1 TENSIONS must carry one exact finite vertex-value sequence");
        NumberList differences(values->size() > 1 ? values->size() - 1 : 0);
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < differences.size(); ++i)
            differences[i] = (*values)[i + 1] - (*values)[i];
        if (!legacy_v1_claim_matches(expression.value,
                                     std::optional<Operand>{Operand::numbers(std::move(differences))}))
            return fail("version-1 TENSIONS result disagrees with its exact historical consecutive coboundary");
        const Operand old_values = expression.operands[0];
        expression.operands = {
            Operand::term(TermValue{"oriented_path_graph", {std::to_string(values->size())}}),
            old_values};
        return true;
    }
    case 76: {
        const auto* left = expression.operands.size() == 2
            ? std::get_if<ProbabilityValue>(&expression.operands[0].body) : nullptr;
        const auto* right = expression.operands.size() == 2
            ? std::get_if<ProbabilityValue>(&expression.operands[1].body) : nullptr;
        if (!left || !right)
            return fail("version-1 TRUST must carry two finite focal-mass assignments");
        NameList frame;
        for (const auto& focal : left->outcomes) {
            const auto atoms = split_set_label(focal); frame.insert(frame.end(), atoms.begin(), atoms.end());
        }
        for (const auto& focal : right->outcomes) {
            const auto atoms = split_set_label(focal); frame.insert(frame.end(), atoms.begin(), atoms.end());
        }
        frame = sorted_unique_names(std::move(frame));
        if (frame.empty()) return fail("version-1 TRUST focal assignments do not determine a finite discernment frame");
        LightRuntime probe(2);
        const auto current = probe.invoke("dempster_combine", {
            Operand::names(frame), expression.operands[0], expression.operands[1]});
        if (!current.value || !legacy_v1_claim_matches(expression.value, current.value))
            return fail("version-1 TRUST result or focal masses disagree with exact normalized Dempster combination on their least derived frame");
        const Operand old_left = expression.operands[0];
        const Operand old_right = expression.operands[1];
        expression.operands = {Operand::names(std::move(frame)), old_left, old_right};
        return true;
    }
    case 77: {
        const auto* field = expression.operands.size() == 1
            ? std::get_if<NumberList>(&expression.operands[0].body) : nullptr;
        if (!field || !std::all_of(field->begin(), field->end(),
                                   [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); }))
            return fail("version-1 CREST must carry one exact finite path scalar field");
        NumberList strict_indices;
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < field->size(); ++i) {
            const bool above_left = i == 0 || (*field)[i] > (*field)[i - 1];
            const bool above_right = i + 1 == field->size() || (*field)[i] > (*field)[i + 1];
            if (above_left && above_right) strict_indices.push_back(static_cast<double>(i));
        }
        if (!legacy_v1_claim_matches(expression.value,
                                     std::optional<Operand>{Operand::numbers(std::move(strict_indices))}))
            return fail("version-1 CREST result disagrees with its exact historical strict path maxima");
        const Operand old_field = expression.operands[0];
        expression.operands = {
            Operand::term(TermValue{"undirected_path_graph", {std::to_string(field->size())}}),
            old_field};
        return true;
    }
    case 98: {
        const auto* transports = expression.operands.size() == 1
            ? std::get_if<Matrix>(&expression.operands[0].body) : nullptr;
        if (!transports || !transports->valid() || transports->rows == 0 || transports->columns != 4 ||
            !std::all_of(transports->values.begin(), transports->values.end(),
                         [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); }))
            return fail("version-1 HOLA must carry a nonempty finite row-ordered family of 2x2 transports");
        std::array<double, 4> product{1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0};
        for (std::size_t row = 0; row < transports->rows; ++row) {
            const std::array<double, 4> next{transports->at(row, 0), transports->at(row, 1),
                                              transports->at(row, 2), transports->at(row, 3)};
            product = {next[0] * product[0] + next[1] * product[2],
                       next[0] * product[1] + next[1] * product[3],
                       next[2] * product[0] + next[3] * product[2],
                       next[2] * product[1] + next[3] * product[3]};
        }
        if (!std::all_of(product.begin(), product.end(), [](double value) { return std::isfinite(value); }) ||
            !legacy_v1_claim_matches(expression.value,
                std::optional<Operand>{Operand::matrix(Matrix{2, 2, NumberList(product.begin(), product.end())})}))
            return fail("version-1 HOLA result disagrees with its exact historical traversal-order transport product");
        const Operand old_transports = expression.operands[0];
        expression.operands = {
            Operand::term(TermValue{"closed_row_loop", {std::to_string(transports->rows)}}),
            old_transports};
        return true;
    }
    default:
        return true;
    }
}

inline WorkspaceParseResult parse_canonical_workspace(
    std::string_view body,
    const WorkspaceParseLimits& limits = {}) {
    try {
        using canonical_detail::require;
        require(!body.empty(), 0, "workspace body is empty");
        require(body.size() <= limits.maximum_bytes, 0, "workspace byte bound exceeded");
        require(body.back() == '\n', 0, "canonical workspace must end with exactly one line feed");
        require(body.find('\r') == std::string_view::npos && body.find('\0') == std::string_view::npos,
                0, "canonical workspace contains a carriage return or NUL byte");

        std::vector<std::string_view> lines;
        lines.reserve((std::min)(limits.maximum_lines, body.size() / 24 + 1));
        std::size_t begin = 0;
        while (begin < body.size()) {
            const auto end = body.find('\n', begin);
            require(end != std::string_view::npos, lines.size() + 1, "unterminated canonical line");
            const auto line = body.substr(begin, end - begin);
            require(line.size() <= limits.maximum_line_bytes, lines.size() + 1, "canonical line bound exceeded");
            require(lines.size() < limits.maximum_lines, lines.size() + 1, "canonical line-count bound exceeded");
            require(!line.empty(), lines.size() + 1, "blank canonical lines are not permitted");
            lines.push_back(line);
            begin = end + 1;
        }

        std::size_t cursor{};
        std::vector<std::string_view> fields;
        const auto fields_at = [&](std::size_t expected) -> const std::vector<std::string_view>& {
            require(cursor < lines.size(), cursor + 1, "workspace ended before the required line");
            require(canonical_detail::split_canonical_spaces(lines[cursor], fields), cursor + 1,
                    "canonical line spacing is malformed");
            require(fields.size() == expected, cursor + 1, "canonical line has the wrong field count");
            return fields;
        };
        const auto parse_size_at = [&](std::string_view token, std::string message) {
            std::size_t value{};
            require(canonical_detail::parse_size(token, value), cursor + 1, std::move(message));
            return value;
        };
        const auto parse_u64_at = [&](std::string_view token, std::string message) {
            std::uint64_t value{};
            require(canonical_detail::parse_unsigned(token, value), cursor + 1, std::move(message));
            return value;
        };
        const auto parse_double_at = [&](std::string_view token, std::string message) {
            double value{};
            require(canonical_detail::parse_canonical_double(token, value), cursor + 1, std::move(message));
            return value;
        };
        const auto decode_token_at = [&](std::string_view token, std::string message) {
            std::string value;
            require(canonical_detail::decode_hex(token, value, limits, true), cursor + 1, std::move(message));
            return value;
        };

        const bool legacy_version_one = lines[cursor] == "MILESING-LIGHT-WORKSPACE 1";
        const bool current_version_two = lines[cursor] == "MILESING-LIGHT-WORKSPACE 2";
        require(legacy_version_one || current_version_two, cursor + 1,
                "unsupported or malformed workspace header");
        ++cursor;

        const auto& world_fields = fields_at(5);
        require(world_fields[0] == "WORLD", cursor + 1, "WORLD header is absent");
        const auto revision = parse_u64_at(world_fields[1], "invalid world revision");
        const auto node_count = parse_size_at(world_fields[2], "invalid world node count");
        const auto relation_count = parse_size_at(world_fields[3], "invalid world relation count");
        const auto order_count = parse_size_at(world_fields[4], "invalid authored-order count");
        const std::size_t expected_node_count = legacy_version_one
            ? light_catalog.size() - 1 : light_catalog.size();
        require(node_count == expected_node_count, cursor + 1,
                legacy_version_one
                    ? "version-1 workspace must contain the original 111 self numbers"
                    : "version-2 workspace must contain all 112 self numbers");
        require(relation_count + 1 == node_count && order_count == node_count,
                cursor + 1, "workspace relation or authored-order count is inconsistent");
        ++cursor;

        ParsedWorkspace parsed;
        parsed.world.revision = revision;
        parsed.world.nodes.reserve(node_count);
        parsed.world.relations.reserve(relation_count);
        parsed.world.authored_order.reserve(order_count);

        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < node_count; ++i) {
            const auto& node_fields = fields_at(16);
            require(node_fields[0] == "NODE", cursor + 1, "NODE line is absent");
            WorldNode node;
            node.id = parse_size_at(node_fields[1], "invalid world node ID");
            node.catalog_index = parse_size_at(node_fields[2], "invalid node catalog route");
            node.parent = parse_size_at(node_fields[3], "invalid world parent ID");
            node.planar.x = parse_double_at(node_fields[4], "invalid planar x value");
            node.planar.y = parse_double_at(node_fields[5], "invalid planar y value");
            node.spatial.x = parse_double_at(node_fields[6], "invalid spatial x value");
            node.spatial.y = parse_double_at(node_fields[7], "invalid spatial y value");
            node.spatial.z = parse_double_at(node_fields[8], "invalid spatial z value");
            node.extent = parse_double_at(node_fields[9], "invalid node extent");
            node.rotation = parse_double_at(node_fields[10], "invalid node rotation");
            require(node_fields[11] == "0" || node_fields[11] == "1", cursor + 1,
                    "invalid node visibility flag");
            require(node_fields[12] == "0" || node_fields[12] == "1", cursor + 1,
                    "invalid node lock flag");
            node.visible = node_fields[11] == "1";
            node.locked = node_fields[12] == "1";
            require(node.catalog_index < expected_node_count, cursor + 1,
                    "node catalog route is outside MY LIGHT");
            const auto self_number = decode_token_at(node_fields[13], "invalid node self-number token");
            const auto code = decode_token_at(node_fields[14], "invalid node operator token");
            const auto origin = decode_token_at(node_fields[15], "invalid node origin token");
            const auto& definition = light_catalog[node.catalog_index];
            if (legacy_version_one) {
                require(exact_legacy_v1_node_tuple(node.catalog_index, self_number, code, origin),
                        cursor + 1,
                        "version-1 NODE self-number/code/origin tuple disagrees with its exact published catalog route");
            } else {
                require(self_number == definition.self_number && code == definition.code &&
                            origin == definition.origin,
                        cursor + 1,
                        "version-2 NODE self-number/code/origin tuple disagrees with its exact current catalog route");
            }
            parsed.world.nodes.push_back(std::move(node));
            ++cursor;
        }

        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < relation_count; ++i) {
            const auto& relation_fields = fields_at(3);
            require(relation_fields[0] == "RELATION", cursor + 1, "RELATION line is absent");
            parsed.world.relations.push_back({
                parse_size_at(relation_fields[1], "invalid relation source ID"),
                parse_size_at(relation_fields[2], "invalid relation target ID")});
            ++cursor;
        }

        require(cursor < lines.size(), cursor + 1, "ORDER line is absent");
        require(canonical_detail::split_canonical_spaces(lines[cursor], fields), cursor + 1,
                "ORDER spacing is malformed");
        require(fields.size() == order_count + 1 && fields[0] == "ORDER", cursor + 1,
                "ORDER must contain every declared authored body exactly once");
        for (std::size_t i = 0; i < order_count; ++i) {
            parsed.world.authored_order.push_back(parse_size_at(fields[i + 1], "invalid authored-order node ID"));
        }
        ++cursor;

        bool has_explicit_attention = false;
        if (cursor < lines.size() &&
            (lines[cursor] == "ATTENTION" || lines[cursor].starts_with("ATTENTION "))) {
            require(canonical_detail::split_canonical_spaces(lines[cursor], fields), cursor + 1,
                    "ATTENTION spacing is malformed");
            require(fields[0] == "ATTENTION" && fields.size() <= node_count + 1,
                    cursor + 1, "ATTENTION count exceeds the authored world");
            parsed.attention.reserve(fields.size() - 1);
            for (std::size_t i = 1; i < fields.size(); ++i) {
                parsed.attention.push_back(parse_size_at(fields[i], "invalid attended node ID"));
            }
            has_explicit_attention = true;
            ++cursor;
        }

        canonical_detail::OperandBudget operand_budget{limits};
        std::vector<Expression> expressions;
        expressions.reserve((std::min)(limits.maximum_expressions,
                                       lines.size() > cursor ? lines.size() - cursor : std::size_t{}));
        while (cursor < lines.size() && lines[cursor].starts_with("EXPRESSION ")) {
            require(expressions.size() < limits.maximum_expressions, cursor + 1,
                    "expression count exceeds its bound");
            const auto& expression_fields = fields_at(6);
            require(expression_fields[0] == "EXPRESSION", cursor + 1, "malformed EXPRESSION line");
            Expression expression;
            expression.route.value = parse_size_at(expression_fields[1], "invalid ExpressionRoute");
            require(expression.route.value == expressions.size(), cursor + 1,
                    "ExpressionRoutes must be contiguous and begin at zero");
            expression.catalog_index = parse_size_at(expression_fields[2], "invalid expression catalog route");
            const auto operand_count = parse_size_at(expression_fields[3], "invalid expression operand count");
            require(expression.catalog_index < expected_node_count, cursor + 1,
                    "expression catalog route is outside MY LIGHT");
            const auto& definition = light_catalog[expression.catalog_index];
            const bool exact_expression_arity = legacy_version_one
                ? operand_count == exact_legacy_v1_expression_arity(expression.catalog_index)
                : operand_count >= definition.minimum_operands && operand_count <= definition.maximum_operands;
            require(exact_expression_arity,
                    cursor + 1, "expression operand count disagrees with its assigned operator");
            require(expression_fields[4] == "0" || expression_fields[4] == "1", cursor + 1,
                    "invalid expression result flag");
            const bool has_result = expression_fields[4] == "1";
            expression.note = decode_token_at(expression_fields[5], "invalid expression note token");
            ++cursor;
            expression.operands.reserve(operand_count);
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < operand_count; ++i) {
                const auto& operand_fields = fields_at(3);
                require(operand_fields[0] == "OPERAND", cursor + 1, "OPERAND line is absent");
                require(parse_size_at(operand_fields[1], "invalid operand index") == i,
                        cursor + 1, "operand indices must be contiguous and stable");
                Operand operand; std::string operand_error;
                require(canonical_detail::parse_operand(operand_fields[2], operand_budget, operand, operand_error),
                        cursor + 1, std::move(operand_error));
                require(operand_within_workspace_bounds(operand), cursor + 1,
                        "operand exceeds the live canonical workspace extent");
                expression.operands.push_back(std::move(operand));
                ++cursor;
            }
            if (has_result) {
                const auto& result_fields = fields_at(2);
                require(result_fields[0] == "RESULT", cursor + 1, "RESULT line is absent");
                Operand result; std::string operand_error;
                require(canonical_detail::parse_operand(result_fields[1], operand_budget, result, operand_error),
                        cursor + 1, std::move(operand_error));
                require(operand_within_workspace_bounds(result), cursor + 1,
                        "result exceeds the live canonical workspace extent");
                expression.value = std::move(result);
                ++cursor;
            }
            if (legacy_version_one &&
                legacy_v1_operands_require_migration(expression.catalog_index)) {
                std::string migration_error;
                require(migrate_exact_legacy_v1_expression(expression, migration_error),
                        cursor + 1, std::move(migration_error));
            }
            expressions.push_back(std::move(expression));
        }

        if (legacy_version_one) {
            // Version 1 retained the original 111 self numbers. Every unchanged
            // route must prove that its serialized result already agrees with
            // replay; the eight changed routes prove their historical results in
            // their dedicated migrations. Current notes and results are retained
            // only after that historical claim has been validated.
            for (Expression& expression : expressions) {
                const bool changed_route =
                    legacy_v1_operands_require_migration(expression.catalog_index);
                const std::optional<Operand> historical_result = expression.value;
                std::optional<Invocation> formed;
                try {
                    LightRuntime current_meaning(limits.maximum_expressions);
                    const auto& definition = light_catalog[expression.catalog_index];
                    formed = current_meaning.invoke_with_validated_prefix(
                        definition.code, expression.operands, expression.route.value);
                } catch (const std::exception& failure) {
                    require(false, cursor + 1,
                            std::string("version-1 operation migration failed: ") + failure.what());
                }
                require(formed.has_value(), cursor + 1,
                        "version-1 operation migration formed no current replay");
                if (!changed_route) {
                    require(historical_result.has_value() == formed->value.has_value(),
                            cursor + 1,
                            "version-1 unchanged operation result presence disagrees with current replay");
                    require(!historical_result ||
                                canonical_operand(*historical_result) ==
                                    canonical_operand(*formed->value),
                            cursor + 1,
                            "version-1 unchanged operation result disagrees with current replay");
                }
                expression.value = std::move(formed->value);
                expression.note = std::move(formed->note);
            }
        }

        std::string restore_error;
        const bool restored = parsed.runtime.restore_expressions(
            std::move(expressions), restore_error, limits.maximum_replay_work);
        require(restored, cursor + 1, "invalid expression ledger: " + restore_error);

        std::optional<std::size_t> prior_applied_route;
        while (cursor < lines.size() && lines[cursor].starts_with("APPLIED ")) {
            require(parsed.applied_operations.size() < limits.maximum_applied_operations, cursor + 1,
                    "applied operation count exceeds its bound");
            const auto& applied_fields = fields_at(7);
            require(applied_fields[0] == "APPLIED", cursor + 1, "malformed APPLIED line");
            AppliedOperation applied;
            applied.expression.value = parse_size_at(applied_fields[1], "invalid applied ExpressionRoute");
            applied.operator_world_node = parse_size_at(applied_fields[2], "invalid applied operator node ID");
            applied.catalog_index = parse_size_at(applied_fields[3], "invalid applied catalog route");
            const auto designation_count = parse_size_at(applied_fields[4], "invalid designation count");
            require(applied.expression.value < parsed.runtime.expressions().size(), cursor + 1,
                    "applied operation references an absent expression");
            require(!prior_applied_route || applied.expression.value > *prior_applied_route, cursor + 1,
                    "applied receipts must follow unique increasing ExpressionRoutes");
            prior_applied_route = applied.expression.value;
            const Expression& expression = parsed.runtime.expressions()[applied.expression.value];
            const bool migrated_v1_application = legacy_version_one &&
                legacy_v1_operands_require_migration(applied.catalog_index);
            const auto expected_designations = migrated_v1_application
                ? exact_legacy_v1_expression_arity(applied.catalog_index)
                : expression.operands.size();
            require(applied.catalog_index == expression.catalog_index &&
                    designation_count == expected_designations, cursor + 1,
                    "applied catalog or designation count disagrees with the expression");
            const WorldNode* operator_node = parsed.world.find(applied.operator_world_node);
            require(operator_node && operator_node->catalog_index == applied.catalog_index,
                    cursor + 1, "applied operator node does not carry the expression's assigned operator");
            applied.consumer = decode_token_at(applied_fields[5], "invalid applied consumer token");
            applied.purpose = decode_token_at(applied_fields[6], "invalid applied purpose token");
            applied.result = expression.value;
            ++cursor;
            applied.operands.reserve(expression.operands.size());
            std::vector<std::optional<OperandDesignation>> current_designations(
                expression.operands.size());
            if (migrated_v1_application) {
                for (std::size_t current_index = 0; current_index < expression.operands.size(); ++current_index) {
                    const auto role = legacy_v1_synthesized_role(applied.catalog_index, current_index);
                    if (role.empty()) continue;
                    current_designations[current_index] = OperandDesignation{
                        current_index, expression.operands[current_index], std::string(role),
                        std::nullopt, std::nullopt};
                }
            }
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < designation_count; ++i) {
                const auto& designation_fields = fields_at(6);
                require(designation_fields[0] == "DESIGNATION", cursor + 1,
                        "DESIGNATION line is absent");
                OperandDesignation designation;
                designation.operand_index = parse_size_at(designation_fields[1], "invalid designation index");
                require(designation.operand_index == i, cursor + 1,
                        "designation indices must be contiguous and stable");
                designation.role = decode_token_at(designation_fields[2], "invalid designation role token");
                if (designation_fields[3] != "-") {
                    designation.authored_node = parse_size_at(designation_fields[3], "invalid designated authored node ID");
                    require(parsed.world.find(*designation.authored_node) != nullptr, cursor + 1,
                            "designation references an absent authored node");
                }
                if (designation_fields[4] != "-") {
                    canonical_detail::ColonFields spatial(designation_fields[4]);
                    std::string_view x, y, z;
                    Vec3 value{};
                    require(spatial.next(x) && spatial.next(y) && spatial.next(z) && spatial.done() &&
                            canonical_detail::parse_canonical_double(x, value.x) &&
                            canonical_detail::parse_canonical_double(y, value.y) &&
                            canonical_detail::parse_canonical_double(z, value.z) &&
                            canonical_detail::finite_world_number(value.x) &&
                            canonical_detail::finite_world_number(value.y) &&
                            canonical_detail::finite_world_number(value.z), cursor + 1,
                            "invalid or nonfinite designation spatial position");
                    designation.spatial_position = value;
                }
                std::string operand_error;
                require(canonical_detail::parse_operand(designation_fields[5], operand_budget,
                                                        designation.value, operand_error),
                        cursor + 1, std::move(operand_error));
                require(operand_within_workspace_bounds(designation.value), cursor + 1,
                        "designation exceeds the live canonical workspace extent");
                const auto current_index = migrated_v1_application
                    ? legacy_v1_designation_target(applied.catalog_index, i) : i;
                require(current_index < current_designations.size() &&
                        (migrated_v1_application
                            ? legacy_v1_designation_matches(applied.catalog_index, i,
                                                            designation.value, expression)
                            : canonical_operand(designation.value) ==
                                  canonical_operand(expression.operands[current_index])) &&
                        !current_designations[current_index],
                        cursor + 1, "designation value disagrees with its exact expression operand");
                designation.operand_index = current_index;
                designation.value = expression.operands[current_index];
                current_designations[current_index] = std::move(designation);
                ++cursor;
            }
            for (auto& designation : current_designations) {
                require(designation.has_value(), cursor + 1,
                        "version-1 applied operand migration did not form every current designation");
                applied.operands.push_back(std::move(*designation));
            }
            parsed.applied_operations.push_back(std::move(applied));
        }

        if (!has_explicit_attention) {
            require(legacy_version_one, cursor + 1,
                    "version-2 workspace requires an explicit ATTENTION line");
            // Early version-1 writers did not carry ATTENTION. Recovery is safe
            // only when the latest SIZE receipt proves the exact selected names.
            bool recovered{};
            const auto* size_definition = find_light_by_unit("SIZE");
            const auto size_index = size_definition ? light_catalog_index(*size_definition) : light_catalog.size();
            for (auto it = parsed.applied_operations.rbegin(); it != parsed.applied_operations.rend(); ++it) {
                if (it->catalog_index != size_index || it->operands.empty()) continue;
                const auto* names = std::get_if<NameList>(&it->operands.front().value.body);
                if (!names) continue;
                std::vector<std::size_t> inferred;
                inferred.reserve(names->size());
                bool valid = true;
                for (const std::string& name : *names) {
                    const WorldNode* node = parsed.world.find_unit(name);
                    if (!node || std::find(inferred.begin(), inferred.end(), node->id) != inferred.end()) { valid = false; break; }
                    inferred.push_back(node->id);
                }
                if (valid) { parsed.attention = std::move(inferred); recovered = true; break; }
            }
            require(recovered, cursor + 1,
                    "legacy version-1 workspace has no ATTENTION line or SIZE receipt proving selection");
        }

        require(cursor < lines.size() && lines[cursor] == "END", cursor + 1,
                "END line is absent or an unknown record appears before it");
        ++cursor;
        require(cursor == lines.size(), cursor + 1, "trailing records appear after END");

        if (legacy_version_one) {
            // Associate the newly introduced LIGHT TREATMENT body with the
            // authored REALITY body while retaining all original IDs, geometry,
            // expressions, designations, and attention. The new satellite is
            // derived from the current position of its associated REALITY body.
            const AuthoredWorld current = AuthoredWorld::from_light();
            require(current.nodes.size() == parsed.world.nodes.size() + 1 &&
                    current.nodes.back().catalog_index == light_catalog.size() - 1 &&
                    current.nodes.back().id == parsed.world.nodes.size(), cursor,
                    "internal version-1 migration extent is inconsistent");
            WorldNode satellite = current.nodes.back();
            const WorldNode* reality = parsed.world.find(satellite.parent);
            require(reality != nullptr, cursor,
                    "version-1 workspace has no REALITY body for LIGHT TREATMENT association");
            const double theta = reality->rotation;
            satellite.planar = reality->planar + Vec2{185.0 * std::cos(theta), 185.0 * std::sin(theta)};
            satellite.spatial = reality->spatial +
                Vec3{255.0 * std::cos(theta), 255.0 * std::sin(theta), 235.0};
            satellite.rotation = theta + pi * 0.25;
            parsed.world.nodes.push_back(satellite);
            parsed.world.relations.push_back({satellite.parent, satellite.id});
            parsed.world.authored_order.push_back(satellite.id);
        }

        std::string validation_error;
        require(validate_parsed_workspace(parsed, validation_error), cursor,
                "workspace integrity failure: " + validation_error);

        if (current_version_two) {
            const auto round_trip = canonical_workspace_text(parsed.world, parsed.runtime,
                parsed.applied_operations, parsed.attention);
            require(round_trip == body, cursor,
                    "workspace is valid in shape but not exact canonical version-2 text");
        }

        WorkspaceParseResult answer;
        answer.workspace.emplace(std::move(parsed));
        return answer;
    } catch (const canonical_detail::ParseFailure& failure) {
        return WorkspaceParseResult{std::nullopt, failure.what(), failure.line};
    } catch (const std::bad_alloc&) {
        return WorkspaceParseResult{std::nullopt, "workspace allocation failed within the declared bounds", 0};
    } catch (const std::exception& failure) {
        return WorkspaceParseResult{std::nullopt,
            std::string("workspace parse failed safely: ") + failure.what(), 0};
    }
}

struct OperatorVerification {
    bool passed{};
    std::string self_number;
    // Compatibility spelling for the v0.1 guarded-console output.
    std::string unit;
    std::string code;
    std::string law;
    std::string detail;

    OperatorVerification() = default;
    OperatorVerification(bool source_passed, std::string source_self_number,
                         std::string source_code, std::string source_law,
                         std::string source_detail = {})
        : passed(source_passed), self_number(source_self_number),
          unit(std::move(source_self_number)), code(std::move(source_code)),
          law(std::move(source_law)), detail(std::move(source_detail)) {}
};

struct OperatorVerificationReport {
    std::size_t checked{};
    std::size_t passed{};
    std::vector<OperatorVerification> failures;

    bool all_passed() const noexcept { return checked == passed && failures.empty(); }
};

inline std::optional<double> verification_number(const Operand& operand) noexcept {
    if (const auto* value = std::get_if<double>(&operand.body)) return *value;
    if (const auto* value = std::get_if<std::int64_t>(&operand.body)) return static_cast<double>(*value);
    return std::nullopt;
}

inline bool verification_near(double left, double right, double scale = 1.0) noexcept {
    return std::abs(left - right) <= 1e-8 * (std::max)({1.0, std::abs(left), std::abs(right), scale});
}

inline bool verification_numbers(const Operand& operand, std::initializer_list<double> expected) noexcept {
    const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&operand.body);
    if (!values || values->size() != expected.size()) return false;
    return std::equal(values->begin(), values->end(), expected.begin(),
                      [](double left, double right) { return verification_near(left, right); });
}

inline bool verification_names(const Operand& operand, std::initializer_list<std::string_view> expected) {
    const auto* values = std::get_if<NameList>(&operand.body);
    if (!values || values->size() != expected.size()) return false;
    return std::equal(values->begin(), values->end(), expected.begin(),
                      [](const std::string& left, std::string_view right) { return left == right; });
}

inline bool verification_matrix(const Operand& operand, std::size_t rows, std::size_t columns,
                                std::initializer_list<double> expected) noexcept {
    const auto* matrix = std::get_if<Matrix>(&operand.body);
    if (!matrix || !matrix->valid() || matrix->rows != rows || matrix->columns != columns || matrix->values.size() != expected.size()) return false;
    return std::equal(matrix->values.begin(), matrix->values.end(), expected.begin(),
                      [](double left, double right) { return verification_near(left, right); });
}

inline bool verification_relation_has(const RelationValue& relation, std::string_view left, std::string_view right) {
    return std::find(relation.pairs.begin(), relation.pairs.end(),
                     std::pair<std::string, std::string>{std::string(left), std::string(right)}) != relation.pairs.end();
}

inline OperatorVerification verify_operator_exercise(const AuthoredWorld& world,
                                                      const LightRuntime& runtime,
                                                      std::string_view unit,
                                                      const AuthoredInvocation& exercise) {
    const auto* definition = find_light_by_unit(unit);
    const auto verdict = [&](bool passed, std::string law, std::string detail = {}) {
        return OperatorVerification{passed, std::string(unit), definition ? std::string(definition->code) : std::string{},
                                    std::move(law), std::move(detail)};
    };
    if (!definition) return verdict(false, "catalog membership", "self number is absent from the Light catalog");
    const auto* body = world.find_unit(unit);
    if (!body) return verdict(false, "authored self-number relation", "self number has no conceptual body in the world");
    const auto expected_catalog = light_catalog_index(*definition);
    if (exercise.application.catalog_index != expected_catalog ||
        exercise.application.operator_world_node != body->id) {
        return verdict(false, "authored self-number relation", "application route does not name this self-number body and assigned operator");
    }
    const auto* expression = runtime.find(exercise.invocation.expression);
    if (!expression || expression->catalog_index != expected_catalog ||
        expression->route.value != exercise.application.expression.value) {
        return verdict(false, "expression provenance", "runtime expression does not retain the assigned operator route");
    }
    if (!exercise.invocation.value || !exercise.application.result || !expression->value) {
        return verdict(false, "finite realization", "fixture did not produce a retained finite value");
    }
    if (canonical_operand(*exercise.invocation.value) != canonical_operand(*exercise.application.result) ||
        canonical_operand(*exercise.invocation.value) != canonical_operand(*expression->value)) {
        return verdict(false, "result provenance", "invocation, application, and expression disagree on the result");
    }
    const auto fixture = operator_fixture(world, unit);
    if (fixture.size() != exercise.application.operands.size() || fixture.size() != expression->operands.size()) {
        return verdict(false, "operand designation", "fixture arity was not retained");
    }
    for (std::size_t i = 0; i < fixture.size(); ++i) {
        if (exercise.application.operands[i].operand_index != i ||
            exercise.application.operands[i].role != fixture[i].role ||
            canonical_operand(exercise.application.operands[i].value) != canonical_operand(fixture[i].value) ||
            canonical_operand(expression->operands[i]) != canonical_operand(fixture[i].value)) {
            return verdict(false, "operand designation", "actual operand value or role differs from the domain fixture");
        }
    }
    const auto& result = *exercise.invocation.value;
    const auto code = definition->code;
    const auto number_is = [&](double expected) {
        const auto value = verification_number(result); return value && verification_near(*value, expected);
    };
    const auto truth_is = [&](bool expected) {
        const auto* value = std::get_if<bool>(&result.body); return value && *value == expected;
    };

    if (code == "divinand") {
        const auto* source = expression->operands.empty() ? nullptr :
            std::get_if<double>(&expression->operands[0].body);
        const auto* route = expression->operands.size() < 2 ? nullptr :
            std::get_if<NameList>(&expression->operands[1].body);
        bool exact = source && verification_near(*source, 0.25) && route &&
                     *route == NameList{"doubling_map", "reciprocal"} && number_is(2.0);
        LightRuntime whole_runtime(8);
        const DurationWhole duration{10, 20, 1000, "verification-clock"};
        const auto source_measure = form_measure_whole(
            "divinand-source", "guarded verification", "source typed whole", "canonical byte",
            "finite DivinandWhole verification", duration, {0x3f}, {0, 0, 0});
        const auto route_measure = form_measure_whole(
            "divinand-route", "guarded verification", "finite operation route", "canonical byte",
            "finite DivinandWhole verification", duration, {0xa5}, {0, 8, 0});
        const auto source_view = form_typed_whole_view(
            "source-view", source_measure, WholeViewKind::real_scalar,
            "Milesing mathematics", "W=1/4", Operand::number(0.25),
            GraphValue{{"source-view"}, {}});
        const auto route_view = form_typed_whole_view(
            "route-view", route_measure, WholeViewKind::names,
            "Milesing mathematics", "(doubling_map,reciprocal)",
            Operand::names({"doubling_map", "reciprocal"}),
            GraphValue{{"route-view"}, {}});
        const auto derived = derive_whole_self(whole_runtime, WholeSelfDerivationBody{
            "constructive-divinand", "MY LIGHT",
            "D(1/4;doubling_map,reciprocal)=(1/4,2)",
            "the runtime expression retains both supplied typed views and its result is the exact sequential unary derivation",
            "finite DivinandWhole verification", duration,
            {source_measure, route_measure}, {}, {source_view, route_view}});
        const auto whole = form_divinand_whole(
            source_view, {"doubling_map", "reciprocal"},
            derived.formation.graph_whole, derived.invocation.expression);
        exact = exact && whole.operations == NameList{"doubling_map", "reciprocal"} &&
                whole.source_whole.exact_bit_ancestry.size() == 8 &&
                whole.exact_bit_ancestry.size() == 16 &&
                whole.carrier_expression.value == derived.invocation.expression.value;
        return verdict(exact,
            "D(W; doubling_map, reciprocal) retains W and its finite route in the enclosing expression and derives reciprocal(doubling_map(1/4)) = 2 exactly",
            "constructive DivinandWhole retains all 8 exact source bits plus the 8 associated route bits; generic Operand carries no invented measured-bit ancestry");
    }
    if (code == "sub") return verdict(number_is(4.0), "6 - 2 = 4");
    if (code == "is_empty") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto scalar = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::number(0.0), "arbitrary scalar", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "finite-carrier domain law");
        return verdict(truth_is(true) && !scalar.invocation.exact(),
            "the designated empty finite carrier has cardinality zero, while an arbitrary scalar is not silently classified as a set");
    }
    if (code == "exclusive_or") return verdict(truth_is(true), "true XOR false is true");
    if (code == "bottom") {
        const auto* bottom = std::get_if<TermValue>(&result.body);
        return verdict(bottom && bottom->operation == "bottom" &&
                       bottom->arguments == NameList{"bottom"},
            "the validated finite pointed domain has bottom <= bottom and bottom <= value; the domain-tagged bottom term names exactly that least member while the expression retains the supplied domain");
    }
    if (code == "zero") return verdict(number_is(0.0), "Peano zero realizes as 0");
    if (code == "heyting_not") return verdict(verification_names(result, {"c"}),
        "in the finite frame a<=b with c incomparable, the largest upward-closed set disjoint from P={b} is {c}, exactly the Heyting pseudocomplement");
    if (code == "both") return verdict(truth_is(true), "Belnap both recognizes simultaneous true and false evidence");
    if (code == "delete_vertex") {
        const auto* graph = std::get_if<GraphValue>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = graph && graph->vertices == NameList{"a"} && graph->edges.empty();
        return verdict(valid, "vertex deletion removes the vertex and all incident edges");
    }
    if (code == "rule30") return verdict(truth_is(true), "Rule 30 neighborhood 100 maps to 1");
    if (code == "converse") return verdict(canonical_operand(result) == canonical_operand(Operand::relation({{{"b", "a"}, {"c", "b"}}})),
                                            "relational converse exchanges every ordered pair");
    if (code == "minimax_loss") return verdict(number_is(3.0), "min over row maxima of [[1,4],[3,2]] is 3");
    if (code == "add") return verdict(number_is(8.0), "6 + 2 = 8");
    if (code == "recip_inf") {
        const auto* homogeneous = std::get_if<ComplexList>(&result.body);
        return verdict(homogeneous && homogeneous->size() == 2 &&
                       (*homogeneous)[0] == std::complex<double>{1.0, 0.0} &&
                       (*homogeneous)[1] == std::complex<double>{2.0, 0.0},
            "Riemann-sphere reciprocal swaps homogeneous coordinates: finite [2:1] maps to tagged [1:2], whose affine value is 1/2; the same law exchanges zero and infinity without an untagged sentinel");
    }
    if (code == "forward_diff") return verdict(number_is(5.0), "forward difference at position 1 is 9 - 4 = 5");
    if (code == "diagonal") return verdict(verification_numbers(result, {3.0, 3.0}), "diagonal maps x to (x,x)");
    if (code == "box_all") return verdict(truth_is(true), "every world accessible from a satisfies the supplied predicate");
    if (code == "iterate") return verdict(number_is(0.5), "two doubling-map iterations carry 1/8 to 1/2");
    if (code == "luk_or") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto outside_degree = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::number(1.2), "left degree", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::number(0.1), "right degree", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "membership-degree domain law");
        return verdict(number_is(0.8) && !outside_degree.invocation.exact(),
            "Lukasiewicz union is min(1,0.35+0.45), and degrees outside [0,1] are outside this fuzzy-logic operation");
    }
    if (code == "compose") return verdict(canonical_operand(result) == canonical_operand(Operand::relation({{{"a", "c"}}})),
                                           "relational composition joins a->b with b->c");
    if (code == "term") {
        const auto* term = std::get_if<TermValue>(&result.body);
        return verdict(term && term->operation == "f" && term->arguments == NameList{"x", "y"},
                       "free-term construction retains its operation and ordered arguments");
    }
    if (code == "action_prefix") {
        const auto* prefixed = std::get_if<TermValue>(&result.body);
        return verdict(prefixed && prefixed->operation == "action_prefix" &&
                       prefixed->arguments == NameList{"open", "shape", "commit"},
            "action prefix retains a distinct constructor and the exact action-before-process argument order");
    }
    if (code == "aitken") return verdict(number_is(2.0), "Aitken delta-squared accelerates the supplied geometric approach to 2");
    if (code == "mul") return verdict(number_is(12.0), "6 * 2 = 12");
    if (code == "erode") {
        const auto* points = std::get_if<Point2List>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = points && points->size() == 2 && verification_near((*points)[0].x, 0.0) && verification_near((*points)[1].x, 1.0) &&
                           verification_near((*points)[0].y, 0.0) && verification_near((*points)[1].y, 0.0);
        return verdict(valid, "finite erosion retains exactly translations 0 and 1 containing the structuring element");
    }
    if (code == "shapley") return verdict(number_is(1.5), "two-player Shapley allocation averages the player's two marginal contributions");
    if (code == "discrete_partition") {
        const auto* relation = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = relation && relation->pairs.size() == 3 && verification_relation_has(*relation, "a", "a") &&
                           verification_relation_has(*relation, "b", "b") && verification_relation_has(*relation, "c", "c");
        return verdict(valid, "discrete partition contains only singleton equivalence pairs");
    }
    if (code == "bayes") {
        const auto* posterior = std::get_if<ProbabilityValue>(&result.body);
        bool valid = posterior && posterior->outcomes == NameList{"a", "b"} && posterior->weights.size() == 2 &&
                           verification_near(posterior->weights[0], 6.0 / 7.0) && verification_near(posterior->weights[1], 1.0 / 7.0) &&
                           verification_near(std::accumulate(posterior->weights.begin(), posterior->weights.end(), 0.0), 1.0);
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto malformed_prior = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::probability({{"a", "b"}, {0.6, 0.6}}), "prior", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::probability({{"a", "b"}, {0.8, 0.2}}), "likelihood", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "Bayes domain law");
        valid = valid && !malformed_prior.invocation.exact();
        return verdict(valid, "Bayesian posterior is normalized prior times likelihood; a non-normalized prior is rejected");
    }
    if (code == "reduce_free") {
        const auto* word = std::get_if<std::string>(&result.body);
        return verdict(word && *word == "c", "adjacent inverse generators cancel in the free group");
    }
    if (code == "nearest_decode") {
        const auto* word = std::get_if<std::string>(&result.body);
        bool valid = word && *word == "111";
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto tie = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::names({"1111", "0000"}), "code", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::text("0011"), "received", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "deterministic equal-distance law");
        const auto* tied_word = tie.invocation.value ? std::get_if<std::string>(&tie.invocation.value->body) : nullptr;
        const auto wrong_extent = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::names({"00", "111"}), "code", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::text("010"), "received", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "fixed-length code law");
        valid = valid && tied_word && *tied_word == "0000" && !wrong_extent.invocation.exact();
        return verdict(valid, "111 uniquely minimizes Hamming distance to 110; equal distances resolve lexicographically and mixed lengths are rejected");
    }
    if (code == "snell") return verdict(verification_matrix(result, 2, 2, {2.6, 2.0, 3.0, 1.0}),
                                        "Snell envelope equals max(immediate gain, conditional continuation) backward in time");
    if (code == "huber") return verdict(number_is(1.5), "Huber loss at error 2 and delta 1 is 1.5");
    if (code == "covers") {
        const auto* relation = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = relation && relation->pairs.size() == 2 && verification_relation_has(*relation, "a", "b") && verification_relation_has(*relation, "b", "c");
        return verdict(valid, "cover relation removes reflexive and transitively implied a->c pairs");
    }
    if (code == "concept_close") return verdict(verification_names(result, {"o1"}),
                                                 "formal object closure A'' is the fixed object set sharing all common attributes");
    if (code == "mix") {
        bool valid = verification_names(result, {"c", "a", "b"});
        bool seeded_distinct_and_repeatable = false;
        LightRuntime probe(64);
        for (std::int64_t seed = 0; seed < 8 && valid && !seeded_distinct_and_repeatable; ++seed) {
            const auto designations = std::vector<OperandDesignation>{
                {0, Operand::names({"a", "b", "c"}), "values", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
                {1, Operand::integer(seed), "deterministic random seed", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
            };
            const auto first = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, designations, "verification", "seeded Mix law");
            const auto second = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, designations, "verification", "seeded Mix repeatability");
            if (!first.invocation.value || !second.invocation.value) { valid = false; break; }
            const auto* names = std::get_if<NameList>(&first.invocation.value->body);
            if (!names) { valid = false; break; }
            auto sorted = *names; std::sort(sorted.begin(), sorted.end());
            seeded_distinct_and_repeatable = sorted == NameList{"a", "b", "c"} && *names != NameList{"b", "c", "a"} &&
                                             canonical_operand(*first.invocation.value) == canonical_operand(*second.invocation.value);
        }
        return verdict(valid && seeded_distinct_and_repeatable,
                       "Mix supports explicit choice and repeatable seeded randomness, preserves members, and is not cyclic shift");
    }
    if (code == "lyap_residual") return verdict(verification_matrix(result, 2, 2, {-0.75, 0.0, 0.0, -0.9375}),
                                                "Lyapunov residual equals A^T P A - P");
    if (code == "l_system_step") {
        const auto* word = std::get_if<std::string>(&result.body);
        return verdict(word && *word == "ABA", "parallel productions A->AB and B->A rewrite AB to ABA");
    }
    if (code == "exact_cover") {
        const auto* rows = std::get_if<NumberList>(&result.body);
        const Matrix incidence{3, 3, {1, 0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 0, 1, 0}};
        NumberList coverage(3, 0.0); bool valid = rows != nullptr;
        if (rows) for (const auto raw : *rows) {
            const auto row = static_cast<std::size_t>(raw);
            valid = valid && raw >= 0.0 && std::floor(raw) == raw && row < incidence.rows;
            if (row < incidence.rows) for (std::size_t column = 0; column < incidence.columns; ++column) coverage[column] += incidence.at(row, column);
        }
        valid = valid && std::all_of(coverage.begin(), coverage.end(), [](double value) { return value == 1.0; });
        return verdict(valid, "selected exact-cover rows cover every column exactly once");
    }
    if (code == "delay_k") return verdict(verification_numbers(result, {0.0, 1.0, 2.0}), "one-step discrete delay inserts fill then prior samples");
    if (code == "kl_div") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto nonnormalized = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::numbers({0.5, 0.4}), "p", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::numbers({0.25, 0.75}), "q", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "distribution domain law");
        return verdict(number_is(0.5 * std::log(4.0 / 3.0)) && !nonnormalized.invocation.exact(),
            "finite KL divergence equals sum p log(p/q) on normalized distributions; unnormalized weights are rejected");
    }
    if (code == "reciprocal") return verdict(number_is(0.5), "field inverse of 2 is 1/2");
    if (code == "log_spiral") {
        const auto* point = std::get_if<Vec2>(&result.body);
        const auto radius = std::exp(0.1 * pi);
        const bool valid = point && verification_near(length(*point), radius) && verification_near(point->x, -radius) && verification_near(point->y, 0.0, radius);
        return verdict(valid, "logarithmic spiral obeys r = a exp(b theta) at theta = pi");
    }
    if (code == "bellman_opt") return verdict(verification_numbers(result, {3.5, 2.75}),
                                              "Bellman update maximizes immediate reward plus transition-weighted continuation");
    if (code == "eval_at") {
        const auto* value = std::get_if<std::string>(&result.body);
        return verdict(value && *value == "4", "the supplied finite function contains exactly now->4, so evaluation at domain member now is 4");
    }
    if (code == "dft") {
        const auto* spectrum = std::get_if<ComplexList>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = spectrum && spectrum->size() == 4 && verification_near((*spectrum)[0].real(), 0.0) &&
                           verification_near((*spectrum)[1].real(), 2.0) && verification_near((*spectrum)[2].real(), 0.0) &&
                           verification_near((*spectrum)[3].real(), 2.0) &&
                           std::all_of(spectrum->begin(), spectrum->end(), [](auto value) { return verification_near(value.imag(), 0.0); });
        return verdict(valid, "DFT of [1,0,-1,0] is the expected real four-bin spectrum");
    }
    if (code == "group") {
        const auto* route = std::get_if<ExpressionRoute>(&result.body);
        return verdict(route && route->value == 0, "grouping preserves the complete nested expression operand");
    }
    if (code == "voronoi") {
        const auto* diagram = std::get_if<VoronoiDiagram>(&result.body);
        bool valid = diagram && diagram->sites.size() == 3 && diagram->cells.size() == 3;
        if (valid) for (std::size_t i = 0; i < diagram->cells.size(); ++i) {
            valid = valid && !diagram->cells[i].empty();
            for (const auto vertex : diagram->cells[i]) for (std::size_t j = 0; j < diagram->sites.size(); ++j)
                valid = valid && length(vertex - diagram->sites[i]) <= length(vertex - diagram->sites[j]) + 1e-7;
        }
        return verdict(valid, "each clipped Voronoi cell contains only points no farther from its site than any rival site");
    }
    if (code == "gossip_step") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto nonstochastic = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::matrix({2, 2, {0.8, 0.8, 0.5, 0.5}}), "weights", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::numbers({0, 2}), "values", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "convex-association law");
        return verdict(verification_numbers(result, {1.0, 1.0}) && !nonstochastic.invocation.exact(),
            "doubly averaging gossip reaches consensus at 1, and every accepted row is a convex association rather than arbitrary gain");
    }
    if (code == "hill_diversity") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto negative_weight = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::numbers({1, -1, 2}), "weights", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::number(1), "order", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "nonnegative-weight law");
        return verdict(number_is(std::sqrt(8.0)) && !negative_weight.invocation.exact(),
            "order-one Hill diversity is exp(Shannon entropy) after finite normalization; negative weights are rejected");
    }
    if (code == "maxplus_mv") return verdict(verification_numbers(result, {5.0, 5.0}), "max-plus matrix-vector product uses max_j(A_ij + x_j)");
    if (code == "safe_gfp") {
        const auto* region = std::get_if<NameList>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = region && *region == NameList{"a", "b"};
        return verdict(valid, "nu X.(Safe intersect [R]X) starts from the supplied safe set and removes every vertex with a transition outside the current approximation; {a,b} is closed, and every removed vertex has a finite escape chain, so no larger fixed point exists; safe deadlocks satisfy [R]X vacuously");
    }
    if (code == "offspring_pgf") return verdict(number_is(0.74375), "offspring PGF evaluates sum p_k z^k");
    if (code == "hutchinson") {
        const auto* points = std::get_if<Point2List>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = points && points->size() == 6 && verification_near((*points)[0].x, 0.0) &&
                           verification_near((*points)[1].x, 0.5) && verification_near((*points)[3].x, 1.0) &&
                           verification_near((*points)[4].x, 1.5);
        return verdict(valid, "Hutchinson operator returns the union of both affine images of every source point");
    }
    if (code == "cyclic_shift") return verdict(verification_names(result, {"b", "c", "a"}), "one cyclic shift preserves members and advances their order");
    if (code == "right_adjoint") {
        const auto* adjoint = std::get_if<std::string>(&result.body);
        bool law = adjoint && *adjoint == "a2";
        const std::array<std::string_view, 4> images{"b0", "b1", "b1", "b3"};
        for (std::size_t x = 0; x < images.size(); ++x)
            law = law && ((images[x] <= std::string_view{"b1"}) == (x <= 2));
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto nonmonotone = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::relation({{{"a0", "a0"}, {"a1", "a1"}, {"a2", "a2"},
                                     {"a0", "a1"}, {"a0", "a2"}, {"a1", "a2"}}}), "source poset", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::relation({{{"b0", "b0"}, {"b1", "b1"}, {"b2", "b2"},
                                     {"b0", "b1"}, {"b0", "b2"}, {"b1", "b2"}}}), "target poset", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {2, Operand::relation({{{"a0", "b0"}, {"a1", "b2"}, {"a2", "b1"}}}), "nonmonotone map", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {3, Operand::text("b1"), "target", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "finite-chain adjunction law");
        return verdict(law && !nonmonotone.invocation.exact(),
            "for every supplied source member x, f(x)<=b1 iff x<=a2=right_adjoint(b1); a nonmonotone map is rejected");
    }
    if (code == "ols") return verdict(verification_numbers(result, {1.0, 2.0}), "OLS normal equations recover intercept 1 and slope 2");
    if (code == "div") return verdict(number_is(3.0), "6 / 2 = 3");
    if (code == "operad_substitute") {
        const auto* tree = std::get_if<OperadTreeValue>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = tree && tree->valid() && tree->labels == NameList{"root", "branch", "leaf"} &&
                           tree->parents == std::vector<std::int64_t>{-1, 0, 1};
        return verdict(valid, "operadic substitution grafts the complete nested branch tree into the declared leaf slot");
    }
    if (code == "prim_rec") return verdict(number_is(0.5), "bounded primitive recursion applies the doubling step twice");
    if (code == "prox") return verdict(number_is(1.5), "L1 proximal map is soft-thresholding by lambda = 0.5");
    if (code == "replicator_rhs") return verdict(verification_numbers(result, {-0.125, 0.125}),
                                                 "replicator field is x_i(f_i - mean fitness) and conserves total mass");
    if (code == "coboundary") return verdict(verification_numbers(result, {3.0, 5.0}),
        "on oriented edges a->b and b->c, the exact coboundary is (4-1, 9-4)=(3,5) in supplied edge order; the two differences telescope to 9-1 along the path");
    if (code == "union_sets") {
        const auto* relation = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = relation && relation->pairs.size() == 4 && verification_relation_has(*relation, "a", "a") &&
                           verification_relation_has(*relation, "a", "b") && verification_relation_has(*relation, "b", "a") &&
                           verification_relation_has(*relation, "b", "b");
        return verdict(valid, "disjoint-set union produces one reflexive symmetric equivalence class");
    }
    if (code == "cut_rule") {
        const auto* proof = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&result.body);
        bool valid = proof && proof->pairs.size() == 1 && verification_relation_has(*proof, "Gamma", "Delta");
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto absent_cut = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::relation({{{"Gamma", "Q"}}}), "left proof", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::relation({{{"P", "Delta"}}}), "right proof", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {2, Operand::text("P"), "formula", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "cut-premise law");
        valid = valid && !absent_cut.invocation.exact();
        return verdict(valid, "cut eliminates the shared formula P between actual matching sequents; an absent premise yields no claimed conclusion");
    }
    if (code == "givens_rotation") {
        const auto* values = std::get_if<NumberList>(&result.body);
        bool valid = values && values->size() == 5;
        if (valid) {
            const auto c = (*values)[0], minus_s = (*values)[1], s = (*values)[2], second_c = (*values)[3];
            valid = verification_near(c, 0.6) && verification_near(minus_s, 0.8) && verification_near(s, -0.8) &&
                    verification_near(second_c, 0.6) && verification_near((*values)[4], 5.0) &&
                    verification_near(c * c + s * s, 1.0) && verification_near(c * minus_s + s * second_c, 0.0) &&
                    verification_near(s * 3.0 + second_c * 4.0, 0.0);
        }
        return verdict(valid, "Givens matrix is orthogonal and annihilates the second component of (3,4)");
    }
    if (code == "jain_fairness") return verdict(number_is(6.0 / 7.0), "Jain index is (sum x)^2 / (n sum x^2)");
    if (code == "sinkhorn_step") {
        const auto* matrix = std::get_if<Matrix>(&result.body);
        bool valid = matrix && matrix->valid() && matrix->rows == 2 && matrix->columns == 2;
        if (valid) for (std::size_t column = 0; column < matrix->columns; ++column)
            valid = valid && verification_near(matrix->at(0, column) + matrix->at(1, column), 1.0) && matrix->at(0, column) > 0.0 && matrix->at(1, column) > 0.0;
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto zero_entry = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::matrix({2, 2, {1, 0, 3, 4}}), "matrix", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "positive-matrix domain law");
        return verdict(valid && !zero_entry.invocation.exact(),
            "one Sinkhorn row/column balancing step leaves positive columns normalized; this declared domain requires strict positivity");
    }
    if (code == "pow") return verdict(number_is(36.0), "6^2 = 36");
    if (code == "pareto_front") return verdict(verification_numbers(result, {0.0, 1.0, 2.0}), "all three tradeoff candidates are mutually nondominated");
    if (code == "involute") {
        const auto* values = std::get_if<ComplexList>(&result.body);
        bool valid = values && values->size() == 2 && (*values)[0] == std::complex<double>(1, -2) && (*values)[1] == std::complex<double>(3, 1);
        if (valid) {
            auto restored = *values;
            for (auto& value : restored) value = std::conj(value);
            valid = restored == ComplexList{{1, 2}, {3, -1}};
        }
        return verdict(valid, "complex conjugation is an involution and the second application restores the fixture");
    }
    if (code == "astar_path") {
        const auto* path = std::get_if<NameList>(&result.body);
        bool valid = path && *path == NameList{"a", "b", "c"};
        LightRuntime probe(16);
        const auto alternate_order = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::graph({{"S", "A", "B", "G"}, {{"S", "A", 2.0}, {"S", "B", 1.0}, {"B", "A", 0.5}, {"A", "G", 2.0}, {"B", "G", 100.0}}}), "graph", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::text("S"), "start", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {2, Operand::text("G"), "goal", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {3, Operand::numbers({3.5, 0.0, 2.5, 0.0}), "admissible inconsistent heuristic", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "A-star reopen law");
        const auto* reopened = alternate_order.invocation.value ? std::get_if<NameList>(&alternate_order.invocation.value->body) : nullptr;
        valid = valid && reopened && *reopened == NameList{"S", "B", "A", "G"};
        return verdict(valid, "A-star returns the optimal path and reopens a closed node under an admissible inconsistent heuristic");
    }
    if (code == "kernel") {
        const auto* basis = std::get_if<Matrix>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = basis && basis->valid() && basis->rows == 2 && basis->columns == 1 &&
                           verification_near(basis->at(0, 0) + basis->at(1, 0), 0.0) &&
                           std::abs(basis->at(0, 0)) + std::abs(basis->at(1, 0)) > 0.0;
        return verdict(valid, "returned nonzero basis vector lies in the nullspace of [1,1]");
    }
    if (code == "np_test") return verdict(truth_is(true), "likelihood ratio of the supplied sample exceeds threshold 1");
    if (code == "conjugate") {
        const auto* word = std::get_if<std::string>(&result.body);
        return verdict(word && *word == "abA", "group conjugation returns g x g^{-1} in the finite free-group word domain");
    }
    if (code == "convex_hull") {
        const auto* hull = std::get_if<Point2List>(&result.body);
        bool valid = hull && hull->size() == 3;
        if (valid) {
            double twice_area = 0.0;
            for (std::size_t i = 0; i < hull->size(); ++i) twice_area += (*hull)[i].x * (*hull)[(i + 1) % hull->size()].y - (*hull)[i].y * (*hull)[(i + 1) % hull->size()].x;
            valid = verification_near(std::abs(twice_area), 1.0);
        }
        return verdict(valid, "convex hull excludes the interior point and retains the unit right triangle");
    }
    if (code == "isotonic_fit") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto repeated_position = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::numbers({3, 1, 2}), "values", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::names({"a", "a", "c"}), "order", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "named-chain law");
        return verdict(verification_numbers(result, {2.0, 2.0, 2.0}) && !repeated_position.invocation.exact(),
            "pool-adjacent-violators produces the nearest nondecreasing fit in the unique supplied named chain order");
    }
    if (code == "dempster_combine") {
        const auto* probability = std::get_if<ProbabilityValue>(&result.body);
        bool valid = probability && probability->outcomes == NameList{"a", "b"} && probability->weights.size() == 2 &&
                     verification_near(probability->weights[0], 5.0 / 6.0) && verification_near(probability->weights[1], 1.0 / 6.0) &&
                     verification_near(probability->weights[0] + probability->weights[1], 1.0);
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto frame_mismatch = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::names({"a", "b"}), "declared frame", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::probability({{"a"}, {1.0}}), "evidence one", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {2, Operand::probability({{"c"}, {1.0}}), "evidence outside frame", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "declared-frame law");
        const auto total_conflict = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::names({"a", "b"}), "declared frame", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::probability({{"a"}, {1.0}}), "evidence one", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {2, Operand::probability({{"b"}, {1.0}}), "disjoint evidence two", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "total-conflict law");
        valid = valid && !frame_mismatch.invocation.exact() && !total_conflict.invocation.exact();
        return verdict(valid,
            "the explicit frame {a,b} validates both normalized masses; compatible intersections total 0.72 and normalize to 5/6 on {a} and 1/6 on {b}; out-of-frame focal sets and K=1 total conflict are rejected");
    }
    if (code == "local_maxima") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto plateau = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::graph({{"a", "b", "c"}, {{"a", "b", 1.0}, {"b", "c", 1.0}}}), "graph", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::numbers({2.0, 2.0, 1.0}), "plateau field", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "non-strict local-maximum law");
        const bool valid = verification_names(result, {"b", "d"}) &&
                           plateau.invocation.value &&
                           verification_names(*plateau.invocation.value, {"a", "b"});
        return verdict(valid,
            "local_maxima returns exactly v with f(v)>=f(u) for every adjacent u; consequently both vertices of the top 2,2 plateau are retained while its lower neighbor is excluded");
    }
    if (code == "growth") return verdict(number_is(0.5), "bounded Growth repeats the assigned doubling operation exactly twice");
    if (code == "rule_of_succession") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto fractional_count = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::number(2.5), "successes", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::integer(5), "trials", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "exact-count law");
        return verdict(number_is(4.0 / 7.0) && !fractional_count.invocation.exact(),
            "Laplace succession probability is (successes+1)/(trials+2) on exact event counts; fractional counts are rejected");
    }
    if (code == "vector_norm") return verdict(number_is(5.0), "Euclidean norm of (3,4) is 5");
    if (code == "preimage") return verdict(verification_names(result, {"a", "c"}), "preimage contains exactly inputs mapped into target {x}");
    if (code == "spectral_bisect") {
        const auto* partition = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&result.body);
        bool valid = partition && partition->pairs.size() == 4;
        if (valid) {
            const auto label = [&](std::string_view vertex) -> std::string {
                const auto found = std::find_if(partition->pairs.begin(), partition->pairs.end(), [&](const auto& pair) { return pair.first == vertex; });
                return found == partition->pairs.end() ? std::string{} : found->second;
            };
            const auto a = label("a"), b = label("b"), c = label("c"), d = label("d");
            valid = !a.empty() && a == b && c == d && a != c;
        }
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto negative_edge = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::graph({{"a", "b"}, {{"a", "b", -1.0}}}), "graph", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "positive-weight graph law");
        return verdict(valid && !negative_edge.invocation.exact(),
            "Fiedler-vector median ordering separates the two strong pairs across the weak bridge; negative-weight input is outside this Laplacian domain");
    }
    if (code == "highest_bid") return verdict(number_is(9.0), "highest finite bid is 9");
    if (code == "some_satisfy") return verdict(truth_is(true), "there exists a positive value in [-1,0,2]");
    if (code == "generating_poly") return verdict(number_is(9.0), "1 + 2z + z^2 evaluates to 9 at z=2");
    if (code == "kleene_not") return verdict(truth_is(false), "strong Kleene negation maps true to false");
    if (code == "up_closure") return verdict(verification_names(result, {"a", "b", "c"}), "upward closure is extensive, transitive, and fixed under the supplied order");
    if (code == "cardinality") return verdict(number_is(3.0),
        "the finite carrier {a,b,a,c} has cardinality 3 because repeated representations of a name form one member");
    if (code == "spin") return verdict(verification_names(result, {"INTIMACY", "FUSING", "REALITY", "SPIRALLY", "INFINITY", "CARE"}),
                                          "Spin turns classes forward and subclasses counter to them while preserving every body");
    if (code == "median3") return verdict(number_is(4.0), "median of 7,2,4 is 4");
    if (code == "mahalanobis") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto nonsymmetric = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::numbers({2, 1}), "x", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::numbers({0, 0}), "mean", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {2, Operand::matrix({2, 2, {2, 1, 0, 1}}), "covariance", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "covariance geometry law");
        return verdict(number_is(std::sqrt(3.0)) && !nonsymmetric.invocation.exact(),
            "Cholesky whitening proves Mahalanobis distance sqrt(3) for the supplied symmetric positive-definite covariance; nonsymmetric input is rejected");
    }
    if (code == "free_module") {
        const auto* module = std::get_if<FreeModuleValue>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = module && module->ring == "Z" && module->basis == NameList{"e1", "e2"} && module->coordinates == NumberList{0.0, 0.0};
        return verdict(valid, "free Z-module constructor retains basis and creates its additive zero coordinates");
    }
    if (code == "decibel") return verdict(number_is(10.0), "10 log10(10/1) = 10 dB");
    if (code == "dtw_path") {
        const auto* path = std::get_if<Point2List>(&result.body);
