        bool valid = path && !path->empty() && verification_near(path->front().x, 0.0) && verification_near(path->front().y, 0.0) &&
                     verification_near(path->back().x, 2.0) && verification_near(path->back().y, 2.0);
        if (valid) for (std::size_t i = 1; i < path->size(); ++i) {
            const auto dx = (*path)[i].x - (*path)[i - 1].x, dy = (*path)[i].y - (*path)[i - 1].y;
            valid = valid && dx >= 0.0 && dx <= 1.0 && dy >= 0.0 && dy <= 1.0 && (dx > 0.0 || dy > 0.0);
        }
        return verdict(valid, "DTW path begins and ends at both signal boundaries and advances monotonically by legal steps");
    }
    if (code == "doubling_map") return verdict(number_is(0.75), "doubling map carries 3/8 to 3/4 modulo 1");
    if (code == "inclusion_exclusion") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto nonbinary = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::matrix({2, 2, {1, 0.5, 0, 1}}), "incidence", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "incidence-domain law");
        return verdict(number_is(3.0) && !nonbinary.invocation.exact(),
            "inclusion-exclusion gives union cardinality 2+2-1=3 on exact binary incidence; fractional membership is rejected");
    }
    if (code == "alpha_rename") {
        const auto* term = std::get_if<std::string>(&result.body);
        bool valid = term && *term == "lambda y. y";
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto capture = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::text("lambda x. lambda y. x"), "term", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::text("x"), "old name", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {2, Operand::text("y"), "fresh name", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "capture rejection law");
        const auto shadowing = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::text("lambda x. x (lambda x. x)"), "term", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::text("x"), "old name", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {2, Operand::text("z"), "fresh name", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "lexical-shadowing law");
        const auto* shadowed = shadowing.invocation.value ? std::get_if<std::string>(&shadowing.invocation.value->body) : nullptr;
        valid = valid && !capture.invocation.exact() && shadowed && *shadowed == "lambda z. z (lambda x. x)";
        return verdict(valid,
            "capture-avoiding parsed alpha-conversion renames exactly the outer bound occurrences, rejects capture, and preserves a nested shadowing binder");
    }
    if (code == "holonomy_product") return verdict(verification_matrix(result, 2, 2, {-1.0, 0.0, 0.0, -1.0}),
        "the explicit closed loop a-b-a has exactly two ordered quarter-turn transports; their traversal-order product is the displayed half-turn");
    if (code == "face_map") return verdict(verification_names(result, {"a", "c"}), "face map d_1 removes vertex b from the ordered simplex");
    if (code == "reverse") return verdict(verification_names(result, {"c", "b", "a"}), "Reversal inverts authored order while preserving all members");
    if (code == "stable_match") {
        const auto* matching = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&result.body);
        const bool valid = matching && matching->pairs.size() == 2 && verification_relation_has(*matching, "A0", "B0") && verification_relation_has(*matching, "A1", "B1");
        return verdict(valid, "Gale-Shapley fixture returns complete matching with no blocking pair");
    }
    if (code == "expected_loss") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto nonnormalized = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::numbers({0, 10}), "losses", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::numbers({0.8, 0.4}), "probabilities", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "probability-domain law");
        return verdict(number_is(2.0) && !nonnormalized.invocation.exact(),
            "expected loss is the finite loss-probability inner product, and non-normalized probability weights are rejected");
    }
    if (code == "filtration_at") return verdict(verification_names(result, {"v0", "e0"}), "sublevel filtration retains exactly bodies with value <= 1");
    if (code == "borda_count") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto repeated_rank = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::matrix({1, 3, {1, 1, 3}}), "rankings", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "strict-ranking law");
        return verdict(verification_numbers(result, {3.0, 3.0, 0.0}) && !repeated_rank.invocation.exact(),
            "Borda scores sum positional points across both strict rankings; repeated ranks are rejected");
    }
    if (code == "eventually") return verdict(truth_is(true), "eventually threshold >=1 holds at the final supplied trace point");
    if (code == "poisson_birth") return verdict(number_is(2.0 * std::exp(-2.0)), "Poisson probability for mean 2 and count 2 is 2e^-2");
    if (code == "homology") {
        const auto value = verification_number(result);
        const Matrix boundary_k{1, 2, {1, 1}}, boundary_next{2, 1, {1, 1}};
        bool chain = true;
        for (std::size_t row = 0; row < boundary_k.rows; ++row) for (std::size_t column = 0; column < boundary_next.columns; ++column) {
            std::int64_t sum = 0;
            for (std::size_t middle = 0; middle < boundary_k.columns; ++middle)
                sum += static_cast<std::int64_t>(boundary_k.at(row, middle)) * static_cast<std::int64_t>(boundary_next.at(middle, column));
            chain = chain && (sum % 2 == 0);
        }
        const auto expected_betti = boundary_k.columns - binary_matrix_rank(boundary_k) - binary_matrix_rank(boundary_next);
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto invalid = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::matrix({1, 2, {1, 0}}), "boundary k", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::matrix({2, 1, {1, 0}}), "boundary next", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "chain-complex rejection law");
        return verdict(chain && value && verification_near(*value, static_cast<double>(expected_betti)) && !invalid.invocation.exact(),
                       "GF(2) boundaries require d_k d_{k+1}=0; valid Betti dimension is dim C_k-rank d_k-rank d_{k+1}, invalid chains are rejected");
    }
    if (code == "outage_probability") return verdict(number_is(0.05), "outage probability is 1 - reliability");
    if (code == "fold_all") {
        LightRuntime probe(8);
        const auto wrong_neutral = invoke_authored_light(world, probe, unit, {
            {0, Operand::numbers({1, 2, 3}), "values", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {1, Operand::text("add"), "combine", std::nullopt, std::nullopt},
            {2, Operand::number(1), "unit", std::nullopt, std::nullopt}
        }, "verification", "monoid-neutral-element law");
        return verdict(number_is(6.0) && !wrong_neutral.invocation.exact(),
            "additive monoid fold of 1,2,3 from its actual neutral element 0 is 6; a false neutral element is rejected");
    }
    if (code == "surreal_cut") return verdict(number_is(1.0), "Conway simplest dyadic strictly between left {0} and right {3} is 1");
    if (code == "sheaf_glue") {
        const auto* relation = std::get_if<RelationValue>(&result.body);
        const bool finite_result = relation && relation->pairs ==
            std::vector<std::pair<std::string, std::string>>{{"a", "red"}, {"b", "gold"}, {"c", "blue"}};
        const DurationWhole duration{100, 120, 1000, "QueryPerformanceCounter"};
        const auto measure = form_measure_whole("treatment-fixture", "authored fixture", "whole values", "exact labels",
                                                "three-member finite measured domain", duration, {0x5a});
        const auto local = [&](std::string name, NameList members,
                               std::vector<WholeGraphFact> facts,
                               std::vector<GraphEdge> edges) {
            return DerivedGraphWhole{std::move(name), "REALITY", "add", "local measured section",
                "Each local fact is supplied by its exact measured-bit ancestry on this finite open.",
                "three-member finite measured domain", duration,
                GraphValue{std::move(members), std::move(edges)}, std::move(facts),
                NameList{measure.name}, {}, {measure.duration}, measure.measured_bits, true};
        };
        FiniteWholeCover cover{"treatment-cover", "three-member finite measured domain", duration,
                               {"a", "b", "c"}, {{"U", {"a", "b"}}, {"V", {"b", "c"}}}};
        FiniteLocalWholeSections sections{{
            {"U", local("section-U", {"a", "b"}, {{"a", "red"}, {"b", "gold"}}, {{"a", "b", 1.0}})},
            {"V", local("section-V", {"b", "c"}, {{"b", "gold"}, {"c", "blue"}}, {{"b", "c", 1.0}})}
        }};
        const auto typed_result = sheaf_glue(cover, sections);
        return verdict(finite_result && static_cast<bool>(typed_result) && typed_result.whole &&
                       typed_result.whole->graph_whole.facts.size() == 3 &&
                       typed_result.whole->graph_whole.exact_bit_ancestry.size() == measure.measured_bits.size(),
            "compatible finite local graph wholes agree on overlap {b}; their glued graph whole restricts to U and V, and cover membership makes that global whole unique on the declared measured domain");
    }

    return verdict(false, "verification coverage", "assigned operator has no mathematical verification branch");
}

struct SelfNumberDirectFormat {
    std::string_view self_number;
    std::string_view operation;
    std::string_view codable_symbol;
    std::string_view mathematical_notation;
    std::string_view origin;
    std::string_view operands;
    std::string_view function;
    std::string_view reason;
    std::string_view actual_cpp_use;
    std::string_view direct_proof;

    constexpr std::array<std::string_view, 10> ordered_fields() const noexcept {
        return {self_number, operation, codable_symbol, mathematical_notation,
                origin, operands, function, reason, actual_cpp_use, direct_proof};
    }
};

inline SelfNumberDirectFormat direct_format_for_catalog_index(std::size_t index) {
    if (index >= generated_self_number_bindings::entry_count) {
        throw std::out_of_range("direct format catalog route is outside the binding ledger");
    }
    using generated_self_number_bindings::value;
    return SelfNumberDirectFormat{
        value(index, 0), value(index, 1), value(index, 2), value(index, 3),
        value(index, 4), value(index, 5), value(index, 6), value(index, 7),
        value(index, 8), value(index, 9)
    };
}

inline SelfNumberDirectFormat direct_format_for_self_number(
    std::string_view self_number) {
    const auto* definition = find_light_by_self_number(self_number);
    if (!definition) {
        throw std::invalid_argument("direct format names an absent self number");
    }
    return direct_format_for_catalog_index(light_catalog_index(*definition));
}

inline std::string render_self_number_direct_format(const SelfNumberDirectFormat& format) {
    std::ostringstream output;
    output.imbue(std::locale::classic());
    const auto fields = format.ordered_fields();
    for (std::size_t field = 0; field < fields.size(); ++field) {
        output << generated_self_number_bindings::field_names[field]
               << ": " << fields[field] << '\n';
    }
    return output.str();
}

// Deliberate guarded-console entry point only. The application never calls this at startup.
inline OperatorVerificationReport verify_all_operator_fixtures() {
    OperatorVerificationReport report;
    auto world = AuthoredWorld::from_light();
    LightRuntime runtime;
    for (const auto& definition : light_catalog) {
        ++report.checked;
        try {
            const auto exercise = exercise_operator(world, runtime, definition.unit,
                                                    "guarded operator verification",
                                                    "one finite assigned mathematical law");
            auto verification = verify_operator_exercise(world, runtime, definition.unit, exercise);
            if (verification.passed) ++report.passed;
            else report.failures.push_back(std::move(verification));
        } catch (const std::exception& error) {
            report.failures.push_back(OperatorVerification{false, std::string(definition.unit), std::string(definition.code),
                                                           "guarded finite exercise", error.what()});
        }
    }
    return report;
}

class NativeHandle {
public:
    NativeHandle() = default;
    explicit NativeHandle(HANDLE value) noexcept : value_(value) {}
    NativeHandle(const NativeHandle&) = delete;
    NativeHandle& operator=(const NativeHandle&) = delete;
    NativeHandle(NativeHandle&& other) noexcept : value_(std::exchange(other.value_, INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE)) {}
    NativeHandle& operator=(NativeHandle&& other) noexcept {
        if (this != &other) { reset(); value_ = std::exchange(other.value_, INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE); }
        return *this;
    }
    ~NativeHandle() { reset(); }
    HANDLE get() const noexcept { return value_; }
    explicit operator bool() const noexcept { return value_ != nullptr && value_ != INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE; }
    void reset(HANDLE value = INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) noexcept {
        if (*this) CloseHandle(value_);
        value_ = value;
    }
private:
    HANDLE value_{INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE};
};

struct CngHashState {
    BCRYPT_ALG_HANDLE algorithm{};
    BCRYPT_HASH_HANDLE hash{};
    ~CngHashState() {
        if (hash) BCryptDestroyHash(hash);
        if (algorithm) BCryptCloseAlgorithmProvider(algorithm, 0);
    }
};

inline void require_cng(NTSTATUS status, std::string_view operation) {
    if (status < 0) throw std::runtime_error("CNG " + std::string(operation) + " failed");
}

inline std::string sha256_hex(std::span<const std::byte> bytes) {
    CngHashState state;
    require_cng(BCryptOpenAlgorithmProvider(&state.algorithm, BCRYPT_SHA256_ALGORITHM, nullptr, 0), "open SHA-256");
    ULONG object_size{}, digest_size{}, returned{};
    require_cng(BCryptGetProperty(state.algorithm, BCRYPT_OBJECT_LENGTH,
                                  reinterpret_cast<PUCHAR>(&object_size), sizeof(object_size), &returned, 0), "read object size");
    require_cng(BCryptGetProperty(state.algorithm, BCRYPT_HASH_LENGTH,
                                  reinterpret_cast<PUCHAR>(&digest_size), sizeof(digest_size), &returned, 0), "read digest size");
    std::vector<UCHAR> object(object_size), digest(digest_size);
    require_cng(BCryptCreateHash(state.algorithm, &state.hash, object.data(), object_size, nullptr, 0, 0), "create hash");
    std::size_t offset = 0;
    while (offset < bytes.size()) {
        const auto amount = (std::min)(bytes.size() - offset, static_cast<std::size_t>((std::numeric_limits<ULONG>::max)()));
        require_cng(BCryptHashData(state.hash,
                                  reinterpret_cast<PUCHAR>(const_cast<std::byte*>(bytes.data() + offset)),
                                  static_cast<ULONG>(amount), 0), "hash data");
        offset += amount;
    }
    require_cng(BCryptFinishHash(state.hash, digest.data(), digest_size, 0), "finish hash");
    static constexpr char digits[] = "0123456789abcdef";
    std::string result;
    result.reserve(digest.size() * 2);
    for (const auto byte : digest) { result.push_back(digits[byte >> 4]); result.push_back(digits[byte & 0x0f]); }
    return result;
}

inline std::string sha256_hex(std::string_view body) {
    return sha256_hex(std::span<const std::byte>{reinterpret_cast<const std::byte*>(body.data()), body.size()});
}

inline std::string read_local_text(const std::filesystem::path& path,
                                   std::uintmax_t maximum_bytes = 256ull * 1024ull * 1024ull) {
    std::ifstream input(path, std::ios::binary | std::ios::ate);
    if (!input) throw std::runtime_error("cannot open local body: " + path.string());
    const auto end = input.tellg();
    if (end < 0 || static_cast<std::uintmax_t>(end) > maximum_bytes) throw std::runtime_error("local body exceeds read bound");
    std::string body(static_cast<std::size_t>(end), '\0');
    input.seekg(0, std::ios::beg);
    if (!body.empty() && !input.read(body.data(), static_cast<std::streamsize>(body.size()))) throw std::runtime_error("cannot read complete local body");
    return body;
}

inline WorkspaceParseResult parse_canonical_workspace_file(
    const std::filesystem::path& path,
    const WorkspaceParseLimits& limits = {}) {
    try {
        return parse_canonical_workspace(read_local_text(path, limits.maximum_bytes), limits);
    } catch (const std::exception& failure) {
        return WorkspaceParseResult{std::nullopt,
            std::string("workspace file could not be read safely: ") + failure.what(), 0};
    }
}

inline bool is_canonical_workspace(std::string_view body) noexcept {
    try {
        return static_cast<bool>(parse_canonical_workspace(body));
    } catch (...) {
        return false;
    }
}

inline std::filesystem::path unique_sibling(const std::filesystem::path& final_path,
                                            std::wstring_view role) {
    static std::atomic<std::uint64_t> sequence{};
    const auto suffix = std::wstring(L".") + std::wstring(role) + L"-" +
        std::to_wstring(GetCurrentProcessId()) + L"-" + std::to_wstring(GetTickCount64()) + L"-" +
        std::to_wstring(sequence.fetch_add(1, std::memory_order_relaxed));
    return final_path.parent_path() / (final_path.filename().wstring() + suffix);
}

struct WriteReceipt {
    std::filesystem::path final_path;
    std::filesystem::path candidate_path;
    std::filesystem::path prior_path;
    std::string sha256;
    std::uint64_t bytes{};
    bool replaced_existing{};
    bool reopened_equal{};
    bool reopened_hash_equal{};
    bool reopened_canonical{};
    std::size_t canonical_priors_retained{};
    std::size_t canonical_priors_pruned{};
    std::size_t unverified_priors_held{};
    std::size_t diagnostic_candidates_held{};
    bool recovery_inventory_truncated{};
    std::string recovery_note{};
};

struct RecoveryCleanup {
    std::size_t canonical_priors_retained{};
    std::size_t canonical_priors_pruned{};
    std::size_t unverified_priors_held{};
    std::size_t diagnostic_candidates_held{};
    bool inventory_truncated{};
    std::string note{};
};

template <class Visitor>
inline bool visit_workspace_siblings(const std::filesystem::path& directory,
                                     const std::wstring& wildcard,
                                     std::size_t& admitted,
                                     std::size_t maximum_admitted,
                                     Visitor&& visitor) {
    WIN32_FIND_DATAW found{};
    const std::filesystem::path pattern = directory / wildcard;
    HANDLE search = FindFirstFileW(pattern.c_str(), &found);
    if (search == INVALID_HANDLE_VALUE) {
        const DWORD error = GetLastError();
        if (error == ERROR_FILE_NOT_FOUND || error == ERROR_PATH_NOT_FOUND ||
            error == ERROR_NO_MORE_FILES) return false;
        throw std::runtime_error("workspace recovery prefix enumeration could not begin");
    }
    bool truncated{};
    try {
        while (true) {
            if ((found.dwFileAttributes & FILE_ATTRIBUTE_DIRECTORY) == 0) {
                if (admitted >= maximum_admitted) {
                    truncated = true;
                    break;
                }
                ++admitted;
                visitor(directory / found.cFileName);
            }
            if (!FindNextFileW(search, &found)) {
                const DWORD error = GetLastError();
                if (error != ERROR_NO_MORE_FILES) {
                    throw std::runtime_error("workspace recovery prefix enumeration did not complete");
                }
                break;
            }
        }
    } catch (...) {
        FindClose(search);
        throw;
    }
    FindClose(search);
    return truncated;
}

inline RecoveryCleanup clean_verified_workspace_priors(
    const std::filesystem::path& final_path,
    std::size_t protected_canonical_priors = 2,
    std::size_t maximum_directory_entries = 4096,
    std::size_t maximum_bodies_inspected = 8,
    std::uintmax_t maximum_total_inspected_bytes = 64ull * 1024ull * 1024ull) noexcept {
    RecoveryCleanup answer;
    try {
        auto directory = final_path.parent_path();
        if (directory.empty()) directory = std::filesystem::current_path();
        const auto filename = final_path.filename().wstring();
        const auto candidate_prefix = filename + L".candidate-";
        const auto prior_prefix = filename + L".prior-";
        struct PriorEntry {
            std::filesystem::path path;
            std::filesystem::file_time_type written{};
        };
        std::vector<PriorEntry> priors;
        std::size_t enumerated{};
        answer.inventory_truncated = visit_workspace_siblings(
            directory, candidate_prefix + L"*", enumerated, maximum_directory_entries,
            [&](const std::filesystem::path&) { ++answer.diagnostic_candidates_held; });
        answer.inventory_truncated = visit_workspace_siblings(
            directory, prior_prefix + L"*", enumerated, maximum_directory_entries,
            [&](const std::filesystem::path& path) {
                std::error_code time_error;
                const auto written = std::filesystem::last_write_time(path, time_error);
                priors.push_back(PriorEntry{path,
                    time_error ? std::filesystem::file_time_type::min() : written});
            }) || answer.inventory_truncated;
        std::sort(priors.begin(), priors.end(), [](const PriorEntry& left, const PriorEntry& right) {
            if (left.written != right.written) return left.written > right.written;
            return left.path.filename().wstring() > right.path.filename().wstring();
        });

        std::size_t inspected{};
        std::uintmax_t inspected_bytes{};
        for (const PriorEntry& prior : priors) {
            if (inspected >= maximum_bodies_inspected) {
                answer.inventory_truncated = true;
                ++answer.unverified_priors_held;
                continue;
            }
            std::error_code size_error;
            const auto bytes = std::filesystem::file_size(prior.path, size_error);
            if (size_error || bytes > WorkspaceParseLimits{}.maximum_bytes ||
                bytes > maximum_total_inspected_bytes - inspected_bytes) {
                ++answer.unverified_priors_held;
                answer.inventory_truncated = answer.inventory_truncated ||
                    !size_error && bytes > maximum_total_inspected_bytes - inspected_bytes;
                continue;
            }
            ++inspected;
            inspected_bytes += bytes;
            bool canonical{};
            try {
                canonical = static_cast<bool>(parse_canonical_workspace_file(prior.path));
            } catch (...) {
                canonical = false;
            }
            if (!canonical) {
                ++answer.unverified_priors_held;
                continue;
            }
            if (answer.canonical_priors_retained < protected_canonical_priors) {
                ++answer.canonical_priors_retained;
                continue;
            }
            std::error_code removal_error;
            const bool removed = std::filesystem::remove(prior.path, removal_error);
            if (removed && !removal_error) ++answer.canonical_priors_pruned;
            else {
                ++answer.unverified_priors_held;
                answer.inventory_truncated = true;
            }
        }
        answer.note = "protected " + std::to_string(answer.canonical_priors_retained) +
            " canonical prior(s), pruned " + std::to_string(answer.canonical_priors_pruned) +
            ", held " + std::to_string(answer.unverified_priors_held) +
            " unverified prior(s) and " + std::to_string(answer.diagnostic_candidates_held) +
            " diagnostic candidate(s)" +
            (answer.inventory_truncated ? "; bounded inventory was truncated" : "");
    } catch (const std::exception& failure) {
        answer.inventory_truncated = true;
        answer.note = std::string("recovery cleanup held every uncertain body: ") + failure.what();
    } catch (...) {
        answer.inventory_truncated = true;
        answer.note = "recovery cleanup held every uncertain body after an unknown inspection failure";
    }
    return answer;
}

inline WriteReceipt write_text_recoverably(const std::filesystem::path& final_path,
                                            std::string_view body,
                                            bool require_canonical_reopen = false) {
    if (final_path.empty() || !final_path.has_filename()) throw std::invalid_argument("final workspace path is empty");
    const auto parent = final_path.parent_path();
    if (!parent.empty() && !std::filesystem::is_directory(parent)) throw std::invalid_argument("workspace directory must already exist");
    const auto candidate = unique_sibling(final_path, L"candidate");
    const auto prior = unique_sibling(final_path, L"prior");
    NativeHandle file(CreateFileW(candidate.c_str(), GENERIC_WRITE, 0, nullptr, CREATE_NEW,
                                  FILE_ATTRIBUTE_NORMAL | FILE_FLAG_WRITE_THROUGH, nullptr));
    if (!file) throw std::runtime_error("cannot create unique workspace candidate");
    std::size_t offset = 0;
    while (offset < body.size()) {
        const auto amount = (std::min)(body.size() - offset, static_cast<std::size_t>((std::numeric_limits<DWORD>::max)()));
        DWORD written{};
        if (!WriteFile(file.get(), body.data() + offset, static_cast<DWORD>(amount), &written, nullptr) || written == 0) {
            throw std::runtime_error("workspace candidate write failed");
        }
        offset += written;
    }
    if (!FlushFileBuffers(file.get())) throw std::runtime_error("workspace candidate flush failed");
    file.reset();

    const auto attributes = GetFileAttributesW(final_path.c_str());
    const bool existed = attributes != INVALID_FILE_ATTRIBUTES;
    if (!existed) {
        const auto error = GetLastError();
        if (error != ERROR_FILE_NOT_FOUND && error != ERROR_PATH_NOT_FOUND) throw std::runtime_error("cannot inspect final workspace path");
        if (!MoveFileExW(candidate.c_str(), final_path.c_str(), MOVEFILE_WRITE_THROUGH)) throw std::runtime_error("workspace candidate promotion failed");
    } else {
        if (attributes & FILE_ATTRIBUTE_DIRECTORY) throw std::invalid_argument("final workspace path is a directory");
        if (!ReplaceFileW(final_path.c_str(), candidate.c_str(), prior.c_str(),
                          REPLACEFILE_WRITE_THROUGH | REPLACEFILE_IGNORE_MERGE_ERRORS, nullptr, nullptr)) {
            throw std::runtime_error("workspace replacement failed; candidate retained");
        }
    }

    const auto reopened = read_local_text(final_path, body.size() + 1);
    const auto reopened_equal = reopened == body;
    if (!reopened_equal) throw std::runtime_error("reopened workspace differs from committed body");
    const std::string body_hash = sha256_hex(body);
    const bool reopened_hash_equal = sha256_hex(reopened) == body_hash;
    if (!reopened_hash_equal) throw std::runtime_error("reopened workspace hash differs from committed body");
    const bool reopened_canonical = require_canonical_reopen &&
        static_cast<bool>(parse_canonical_workspace(reopened));
    if (require_canonical_reopen && !reopened_canonical) {
        throw std::runtime_error("committed workspace bytes reopened exactly but failed semantic replay");
    }
    const RecoveryCleanup cleanup = clean_verified_workspace_priors(final_path);
    return WriteReceipt{final_path, candidate, existed ? prior : std::filesystem::path{},
                        body_hash, static_cast<std::uint64_t>(body.size()), existed, true,
                        reopened_hash_equal, reopened_canonical,
                        cleanup.canonical_priors_retained, cleanup.canonical_priors_pruned,
                        cleanup.unverified_priors_held, cleanup.diagnostic_candidates_held,
                        cleanup.inventory_truncated, cleanup.note};
}

inline WriteReceipt write_workspace_recoverably(const std::filesystem::path& final_path,
                                                 const AuthoredWorld& world,
                                                 const LightRuntime& runtime,
                                                 std::span<const AppliedOperation> applied = {},
                                                 std::span<const std::size_t> attention = {}) {
    const std::string body = canonical_workspace_text(world, runtime, applied, attention);
    const WorkspaceParseResult preflight = parse_canonical_workspace(body);
    if (!preflight) {
        throw std::invalid_argument("workspace is not reopenable; no bytes were written: " +
                                    preflight.error);
    }
    return write_text_recoverably(final_path, body, true);
}

struct RecoverableBody {
    std::filesystem::path path;
    std::uint64_t bytes{};
    std::string sha256;
    bool canonical{};
};

inline std::vector<RecoverableBody> inspect_workspace_recovery(const std::filesystem::path& final_path,
                                                               std::uintmax_t maximum_bytes = 64ull * 1024ull * 1024ull,
                                                               std::size_t maximum_directory_entries = 4096,
                                                               std::size_t maximum_bodies = 128) {
    std::vector<std::filesystem::path> paths;
    if (std::filesystem::is_regular_file(final_path)) paths.push_back(final_path);
    auto directory = final_path.parent_path();
    if (directory.empty()) directory = std::filesystem::current_path();
    if (!std::filesystem::is_directory(directory)) return {};
    const auto filename = final_path.filename().wstring();
    const auto candidate_prefix = filename + L".candidate-";
    const auto prior_prefix = filename + L".prior-";
    std::size_t enumerated{};
    (void)visit_workspace_siblings(directory, candidate_prefix + L"*", enumerated,
        maximum_directory_entries, [&](const std::filesystem::path& path) { paths.push_back(path); });
    (void)visit_workspace_siblings(directory, prior_prefix + L"*", enumerated,
        maximum_directory_entries, [&](const std::filesystem::path& path) { paths.push_back(path); });
    std::sort(paths.begin(), paths.end());
    if (paths.size() > maximum_bodies) paths.resize(maximum_bodies);
    std::vector<RecoverableBody> result;
    result.reserve(paths.size());
    for (const auto& path : paths) {
        const auto body = read_local_text(path, maximum_bytes);
        result.push_back(RecoverableBody{path, static_cast<std::uint64_t>(body.size()), sha256_hex(body), is_canonical_workspace(body)});
    }
    return result;
}
